# Normative Rule Traceability ‚Äî Ade

> **Status:** Living architectural document. Regenerated by `/traceability`; not hand-edited.
>
> **HEAD:** `862cd2cb` (PHASE4-N-AO CLOSE ‚Äî the multi-candidate fork-choice SELECT cluster, S1‚ÄìS14: live two-producer fork-choice convergence end-to-end). **THE HEADLINE: `CN-CONS-03` FLIPPED `declared ‚Üí enforced`.** After temporary partition, honest nodes converge using only protocol-defined observables ‚Äî proven on a NATURAL two-producer multi-candidate SELECT pass (CE-AO-6, 2026-06-13; `ade_node` @ `2a03ac73`; both Haskell producers cn1/cn2 live throughout, NO loser-freeze, NO post-fork operator intervention; the SELECT decision is entirely Ade's). The replayable post-switch checker (`ci_check_post_switch_convergence_window.sh` / the `post_switch_continuity` reducer) PASSED: `ContinuesSelectedBranch`, terminal `AgreedAtSwitchTip{slot 391}` (exact agreement, our_hash==peer_hash), 25 admitted descendants chained, 0 diverged, every fork-choice win terminal. Transcript OUTSIDE-REPO (competition-secrecy). SCOPE (honest): proves convergence for the EXERCISED two-producer partition-and-reconverge venue; NOT an unbounded multi-peer ChainSel claim. **PHASE4-N-AO added 11 NEW rules (all `enforced`):** `DC-NODE-34` (peer-identity restoration, SELECT foundation) ‚Üí `DC-NODE-35` (BLUE-safe candidate construction from Ade's own validated headers ‚Äî the load-bearing S2 entry gate) ‚Üí `DC-NODE-36` (live single-selector dispatch ‚Äî the participant `NeedsForkChoice` arm routes the candidate set to the SINGLE existing BLUE `select_best_chain`, never a second selector) ‚Üí `DC-NODE-37` (fork-switch never-abandon ‚Äî the H-1 class at fork-choice scale: never roll back the durable chain until the replacement branch's bodies are FETCHED+LINKED+VALIDATED) ‚Üí `DC-NODE-38` (live multi-block fork-anchor discovery ‚Äî the `walk_to_durable_lca` k-bounded-by-block-depth LCA walk over a self-binding per-peer branch cache) ‚Üí `DC-NODE-39` (post-ForkChoiceWin forward-follow continuity ‚Äî admit winner descendants in parent-link order OR fail closed with a structured `MissingBridge`, never silent stall) ‚Üí `DC-NODE-40` (rolled-back branch evidence retention ‚Äî a k-bounded self-binding `BTreeMap` of Ade's OWN rolled-back blocks lets the LCA walk traverse them, closing the `MissingBridge` over-fire) ‚Üí `DC-NODE-41` (missing-bridge range re-fetch ‚Äî actively re-fetch X+1..descendant from the WINNING peer via `BlockFetch RequestRange` and admit in parent-link order through `pump_block`, OR remain fail-closed) ‚Üí `DC-PUMP-04` (multi-peer wire-pump fairness ‚Äî per-peer bounded lanes + a deterministic configured-order `fair_merge`; no hot peer may starve a quiet peer) ‚Üí `DC-EVIDENCE-04` (closed fork-choice convergence evidence ‚Äî a 10-event closed observe-only vocabulary `needs_fork_choice ‚Üí ‚Ä¶ ‚Üí fork_switch_applied|failed|superseded`, every win paired to EXACTLY ONE terminal by a bounded deterministic `fork_switch_id`) ‚Üí `DC-EVIDENCE-05` (replayable post-switch branch-continuity verdict ‚Äî a GREEN pure reducer `derive_post_switch_continuity` over Ade's OWN validated admitted-block lineage, the single implementation behind both the hermetic replay test AND the live CE-AO-6 gate; peer tip NEVER an input). **`9` carry-forward strengthenings (`strengthened_in += PHASE4-N-AO`):** `CN-CONS-01`, `DC-CONS-03`, `DC-CONS-20`, `DC-NODE-24`/`25`/`26`/`27`/`28`/`29`. **PHASE4-N-AO delta:** registry **361 ‚Üí 372** (227 ‚Üí **239** enforced ‚Äî `+11` new + the `+1` `CN-CONS-03` flip; declared **114 ‚Üí 113**), `9` strengthenings, **`0` rules removed / deprecated / weakened.** CI **161 ‚Üí 173** (+12 gates ADDED, one per new rule; 0 removed; on-disk `ci/ci_check_*.sh` count = **173**, verified by `ls`). **NO** new crate (11) / new BLUE canonical type (the SELECT lives in GREEN/RED `ade_node` modules ‚Äî `candidate_aggregator`, `lca_walk`, `fair_merge`, `fork_switch`, `post_switch_continuity`, `selector_state`; the BLUE `select_best_chain` / header-validate / apply / `pump_block` authorities are REUSED unchanged). NO `RO-LIVE` flip (the natural CE-AO-6 SELECT pass is a C2/testnet convergence proof, NOT a preprod bounty-acceptance claim; `RO-LIVE-01` stays operator-gated/partial). ¬∑ **Generated:** 2026-06-13 ¬∑ **Prior pass:** `b8860b16` (PHASE4-N-AM + PHASE4-N-AN close, 361 rules) ¬∑ **Registry:** `docs/ade-invariant-registry.toml` @ **372 rules** (239 enforced / 1 enforced_scaffolding / 19 partial / 113 declared / 0 deprecated) ¬∑ **CODEMAP:** `docs/ade-CODEMAP.md` @ `862cd2cb` (462 canonical types ¬∑ **173 CI** ¬∑ **372 rules** ‚Äî **REGENERATED to this HEAD** by the sibling `/codemap` close pass; carries all six new `ade_node` SELECT modules (`candidate_aggregator` √ó21, `lca_walk` √ó21, `fair_merge` √ó16, `fork_switch` √ó47, `post_switch_continuity` √ó20, `selector_state` √ó18), all 11 new rule IDs, and the 12 new gates; CI 173 and rule count 372 MATCH this pass; canonical types 462 ‚Üí 462 ‚Äî the cluster hypothesis held, ZERO new BLUE type) ¬∑ **HEAD_DELTAS:** `docs/ade-HEAD_DELTAS.md` @ `862cd2cb` (¬ß0 HEAD `862cd2cb`; ¬ß5 @ **173 CI**; ¬ß7 @ **372 rules** / 239 enforced ‚Äî **REGENERATED to this HEAD** by the sibling `/head-deltas` close pass; all 11 named PHASE4-N-AO gates are catalogued in ¬ß5 (0 orphans) bound to their owning rule)

This document is the **invariant ‚Üî enforcement audit** IDD ¬ß10 demands. For every rule the project commits to, it traces *where the rule is specified* ‚Üí *where it is enforced in code* ‚Üí *which tests prove it* ‚Üí *which CI check fails the build on violation*. A rule that cannot fill all four cells is an **enforcement gap**; this doc surfaces gaps rather than hiding them.

## Source of rules

The canonical source is the **invariant registry** at `docs/ade-invariant-registry.toml` (`.idd-config.json` `invariant_registry`), **372 rules** at HEAD `862cd2cb` (239 enforced / 1 enforced_scaffolding / 19 partial / 113 declared / 0 deprecated). **This pass traces the PHASE4-N-AO close (`b8860b16` ‚Üí `862cd2cb`); the prior TRACEABILITY was pinned at `b8860b16` (the PHASE4-N-AM + PHASE4-N-AN close).** It re-traces the rules PHASE4-N-AO added or changed from scratch against disk (`git grep` / `ls` only; no build or test execution) and preserves every other rule's four-cell row verbatim from the prior pass.

**`+11` NEW rules** (361 ‚Üí 372), all `enforced`, all `introduced_in = "PHASE4-N-AO"`, all `tier = derived` ‚Äî the multi-candidate fork-choice SELECT cluster (S1‚ÄìS14):

- **The SELECT spine (S1‚ÄìS4):** `DC-NODE-34` (peer-identity restoration ‚Äî `AdmissionPeerEvent.peer` is carried end-to-end through `NodeSyncItem` to the participant loop so per-peer candidate tracking is possible; provenance-only, byte-identical single-peer follow), `DC-NODE-35` (BLUE-safe candidate construction ‚Äî a `CandidateFragment` fed to BLUE `select_best_chain` is derived ONLY from Ade's OWN `validate_and_apply_header` output, never a peer-trusted minted summary, never a raw `followed_peer_tip`; THE load-bearing S2 entry gate), `DC-NODE-36` (live single-selector dispatch ‚Äî the participant `NeedsForkChoice` arm, formerly fail-closed, routes the aggregated candidate set to the SINGLE existing BLUE `select_best_chain` ‚Äî routed-to, never duplicated), `DC-NODE-37` (fork-switch never-abandon ‚Äî the H-1 class at fork-choice scale: never commit a rollback of the durable chain until the replacement branch's bodies are FETCHED+LINKED+VALIDATED; adoption then via the enforced `RolledBack`‚Üí`materialize`‚Üí`pump_block` authorities; the security-critical slice).
- **Live geometry + fairness + recovery (S7, S8, S11, S13, S14):** `DC-NODE-38` (live multi-block fork-anchor discovery ‚Äî `walk_to_durable_lca` k-bounded by BLOCK DEPTH over a self-binding per-peer branch cache; the durable LCA is the ChainDb stored slot+hash ONLY, `DC-NODE-29`), `DC-PUMP-04` (multi-peer wire-pump fairness ‚Äî per-peer bounded lanes + a deterministic configured-order `fair_merge`; no hot peer may starve a quiet peer; the RED merge order never decides fork-choice), `DC-NODE-39` (post-ForkChoiceWin forward-follow continuity ‚Äî admit winner descendants in parent-link order OR fail closed with a structured `MissingBridge`, never silent stall), `DC-NODE-40` (rolled-back branch evidence retention ‚Äî a k-bounded self-binding `BTreeMap` of Ade's OWN rolled-back blocks lets the LCA walk traverse them; closes the `MissingBridge` over-fire on loser-branch blocks), `DC-NODE-41` (missing-bridge range re-fetch ‚Äî actively re-fetch X+1..descendant from the WINNING peer via `BlockFetch RequestRange` and admit in parent-link order through `pump_block`, OR remain fail-closed; recovery, not selection).
- **Closed observe-only evidence (S9, S10):** `DC-EVIDENCE-04` (closed fork-choice convergence evidence ‚Äî a 10-event closed observe-only vocabulary whose discriminators EQUAL the emit-only allow-list; every `fork_choice_selected{win}` paired to EXACTLY ONE terminal `fork_switch_applied|failed|superseded` by a bounded deterministic `fork_switch_id`; no event ever consumed by selection/apply), `DC-EVIDENCE-05` (replayable post-switch branch-continuity verdict ‚Äî a GREEN pure reducer `derive_post_switch_continuity` over Ade's OWN validated admitted-block lineage yielding a closed `PostSwitchContinuity`; peer tip NEVER an input; replay-equivalent; the SINGLE implementation behind both the hermetic replay test and the live CE-AO-6 release gate).

**`9` carry-forward strengthenings (`strengthened_in += "PHASE4-N-AO"`):** `CN-CONS-01` (the live multi-peer SELECT is the live analog of the arrival-order-independence proof), `DC-CONS-03` (BLUE `select_best_chain` is now the LIVE multi-candidate resolver target), `DC-CONS-20` (the lockstep receive reducer now applies a live fork-switch `RolledBack`+`ChainSelected`), `DC-NODE-24` (the participant `NeedsForkChoice` consequent PHASE4-N-AI left fail-closed is now WIRED), `DC-NODE-25` (the live durable-apply authority now drives the fork-switch adoption), `DC-NODE-26` (decision/durable reconciliation across the fork-switch), `DC-NODE-27` (the `WalEntry::RollBack{ForkChoiceWin}` marker is now CONSTRUCTED live for the first time), `DC-NODE-28` (no-forge-across-pending-reselection now covers the live fork-switch window), `DC-NODE-29` (the canonical rollback-target slot+hash binding is the fork-anchor binding for the SELECT). **`0` rules removed / deprecated / weakened.**

**ENFORCEMENT-SURFACE HONESTY (recorded, NOT papered over):**

- **All 11 NEW rows are fully four-cell** ‚Äî each carries a dedicated `ci_check_*.sh` gate (one per rule, all 12 PHASE4-N-AO gates present + executable on disk and each names its owning rule in its header), named tests that resolve on disk, and a path-qualified Code row. These rows are NOT gaps.
- **The registry `code_locus` for the new rules reads `CANDIDATE (pending S* impl)` on several entries ‚Äî but the rules are `enforced` and the real enforcing code resolves on disk.** Where the registry placeholder is stale, the four-cell tables below record the REAL disk-verified loci (`crates/ade_node/src/candidate_aggregator.rs`, `lca_walk.rs`, `fair_merge.rs`, `fork_switch.rs`, `post_switch_continuity.rs`, `selector_state.rs`, plus the `node_lifecycle.rs` dispatch/apply taps and the `convergence_evidence.rs` / `admission_log/{event,writer}.rs` evidence surfaces). The registry placeholders are surfaced here as a registry-grooming item, not a TRACEABILITY gap.
- **`CN-CONS-03`'s live witness (the CE-AO-6 natural two-producer transcript) is operator-produced and OUTSIDE-REPO (competition-secrecy / no-credential-leak).** The MECHANICAL contract that backs the flip ‚Äî the replayable `post_switch_continuity` reducer + the hermetic tests + the `ci_check_post_switch_convergence_window.sh` gate (which invokes the reducer bin) ‚Äî IS fully in CI. The flip rests on a replayable verdict reducer, not on an eyeballed transcript: the gate re-derives `ContinuesSelectedBranch` + the terminal from the committed/supplied transcript bytes. Only the live witness itself is off-repo; this is surfaced in `CN-CONS-03`'s CI row, not hidden.
- **The recovered-anchor family (`DC-NODE-31` / `DC-NODE-32` / `DC-NODE-33`) remains TEST-ENFORCED with `ci_script = ""` (no dedicated static gate).** Enforcement surface = the registry-named tests (all resolving on disk) + the `ci/ci_check_bootstrap_closure.sh` (`CN-NODE-01`) closure fence over `bootstrap.rs`. Matches the established `DC-PROTO-10` / `T-REC-05` precedent; recorded honestly in those rows, NOT a hidden gap. Carried unchanged this pass.

**CI: `161 ‚Üí 173` ‚Äî `+12` gates ADDED, one per new rule, 0 removed.** `ci_check_peer_identity_preserved.sh` (`DC-NODE-34`), `ci_check_candidate_construction_validated.sh` (`DC-NODE-35`), `ci_check_live_selector_dispatch.sh` (`DC-NODE-36`), `ci_check_fork_switch_never_abandons.sh` (`DC-NODE-37`), `ci_check_lca_anchor_walk.sh` (`DC-NODE-38`), `ci_check_wire_pump_fairness.sh` (`DC-PUMP-04`), `ci_check_fork_choice_evidence_closed.sh` (`DC-EVIDENCE-04`), `ci_check_post_switch_convergence_window.sh` (`DC-EVIDENCE-05` + the `CN-CONS-03` release gate), `ci_check_missing_bridge_fail_closed.sh` (`DC-NODE-39`), `ci_check_rollback_retention_evidence.sh` (`DC-NODE-40`), `ci_check_missing_bridge_refetch.sh` (`DC-NODE-41`). The on-disk `ci/ci_check_*.sh` count is **173** (verified by `ls`). The registry‚ÜîTRACEABILITY join is **372 ‚Üî 372** (1:1). Verification this pass is `git grep` / `ls` only ‚Äî no build or test execution.

**Window disk-verification.** The 11 NEW rows, the flipped `CN-CONS-03` row, and the 9 carry-forward strengthenings were re-traced against the working tree at `862cd2cb`. **Every registry-cited test fn, every CI gate, and every enforcing code symbol across the re-traced set resolves on disk ‚Äî 0 drift.** Spot-resolved decisive symbols: `walk_to_durable_lca` (`lca_walk.rs`), `fair_merge` (`fair_merge.rs`), `build_candidate_fragment` (`candidate_aggregator.rs`), `dispatch_competing_fork_choice` + `apply_fork_switch` + `recover_missing_range` (`node_lifecycle.rs`), `derive_post_switch_continuity` + `enum PostSwitchContinuity` (`post_switch_continuity.rs`), `RangeRefetchOutcome` + `enum ForkChoiceResult` + `fork_switch_superseded` (`fork_switch.rs` / `admission_log/{event,writer}.rs` / `convergence_evidence.rs`), `select_best_chain` (BLUE `fork_choice.rs`, REUSED). A decisive test fn per new rule resolves (`best_of_two_peers_wins_and_is_identified`, `build_candidate_fragment_assembles_from_validated_headers`, `win_emits_switch_to_winning_peer_and_durable_anchor`, `fork_switch_win_adopts_via_rolledback_then_chainselected`, `multi_block_branch_walks_to_durable_lca`, `post_switch_missing_bridge_emits_structured_and_holds_fence`, `rollback_retains_removed_blocks_for_lca_walk`, `refetched_bridge_admits_in_order`, `hot_peer_cannot_starve_quiet_peer`, `fork_choice_win_paired_with_exactly_one_terminal_applied`, `post_switch_continuity_replays_byte_identical`). **The prior PHASE4-N-AM / AN / AL / AJ / AI close-pass narratives are preserved below verbatim.**

Normative documents (per `.idd-config.json` `normative_docs`): `docs/active/CE-79_gate_statement.md`, `docs/active/CE-79_tier5_addendum.md`, `docs/active/comparison_surface_contract.md`, `docs/active/shelley_bootstrap_contract.md`, `docs/active/CE-73_reclassification.md`, `CLAUDE.md`. ## Conventions

- **Families** are the registry ID-prefix scheme: `T` (true), `DC` (derived), `CN` (constraint-network / classification table), `RO` (release obligation), `OP` (operational). The registry `tier` field (true / derived / operational / release / constraint / constraint_network) is noted per rule; it does not always coincide with the ID prefix (e.g. some `CN-*` and `DC-*` entries carry `tier = "release"`).
- **Status** is the registry `status`: `enforced` (Code+Tests+CI present and load-bearing), `enforced_scaffolding` (the gate is real + executable but the artifact it gates ‚Äî here a CE-AI-6 same-best-peer reorg transcript ‚Äî is pending, vacuous-until-committed), `partial` (some cells filled, scope-limited), `declared` (named but not yet mechanically enforced ‚Äî an open enforcement gap by design).
- A **Code / Tests / CI** cell reading `_(no ‚Ä¶ ‚Äî gap)_` is an explicit enforcement gap, not an omission. A CI cell reading **`N/A ‚Äî test-enforced`** (`DC-NODE-31`, `DC-NODE-32`, `DC-NODE-33`, `T-REC-05`, `DC-PROTO-10`) means the rule is enforced by its named tests (+ a structural closure fence where noted), with `ci_script = ""` in the registry by design ‚Äî NOT a hidden gap; the no-dedicated-gate state is recorded explicitly.
- **Live-evidence note (NOT a gap):** `CN-CONS-03`'s flip rests on the replayable `post_switch_continuity` reducer (`DC-EVIDENCE-05`) + the hermetic tests + `ci_check_post_switch_convergence_window.sh` (which invokes the reducer bin and re-derives the verdict from the transcript bytes) ‚Äî all in CI. Only the live CE-AO-6 two-producer transcript ITSELF is operator-produced + OUTSIDE-REPO (competition-secrecy / no-credential-leak). `T-REC-06`'s LIVE half (CE-AN-LIVE) is likewise off-repo with its mechanical contract in CI. The off-repo live witnesses are recorded explicitly in those rules' CI rows, not hidden.
- **`code_locus` placeholder note (NOT a gap):** several PHASE4-N-AO registry entries carry `code_locus = "CANDIDATE (pending S* impl)"` (the text written at scoping); the rules are `enforced` and the REAL enforcing code resolves on disk. The four-cell tables below record the disk-verified loci; the stale placeholders are a registry-grooming item.
- **[not found on disk ‚Äî drift]** (tests) / **[not on disk ‚Äî drift]** (CI) flags a registry-named test/CI that could not be located in the working tree at `862cd2cb`. **This pass: ZERO such drift on the re-traced set** ‚Äî the 11 NEW rows, the flipped `CN-CONS-03`, and the 9 strengthenings resolve every cited test fn, CI gate, and enforcing code symbol on disk. Rows outside the re-traced PHASE4-N-AO set were not re-verified this delta-refresh ‚Äî their drift status is carried from the prior pass.
- **Honest status notes (NOT gaps):** `DC-EVIDENCE-03` STAYS `enforced_scaffolding` (the AJ single-best-peer reorg transcript-shape gate; its committed transcript is still pending ‚Äî distinct from the CE-AO-6 multi-candidate SELECT transcript that backs `CN-CONS-03` and is off-repo). `DC-NODE-19` is `declared`/partial by design; `DC-NODE-17` is `declared` (safety/observation-only). These are intentional, recorded, and distinct from the four-cell gaps.

## T ‚Äî True Invariants (Project Constitution ¬ß2)

Constitution-level true invariants ‚Äî the properties that must always hold for the authoritative core (determinism, purity, fail-fast, replay-equivalence, no-double-spend, conservation).

_32 rules._

### `T-REC-04`: WarmStart-recovered forge eta0 (`chain_dep.epoch_nonce`) comes from the recovered seed-epoch input, never a placeholder‚Ä¶

_tier: true ¬∑ status: enforced_ ¬∑ _introduced_in: PHASE4-N-F-G-N_

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | `docs/clusters/PHASE4-N-F-G-N/cluster.md` |
| **Requirement** | The WarmStart-recovered forge `chain_dep.epoch_nonce` (eta0) MUST come from the imported/recovered consensus input, never from a snapshot placeholder and never from genesis. Authoritative recovered state is explicit, persisted, replayable, and comparable: the seed-epoch eta0 is an EXPLICIT field in the persisted `SeedEpochConsensusInputs` sidecar and is overlaid onto the recovered `PraosChainDepState` in the single `bootstrap_initial_state` authority. A snapshot-seeded `Nonce::ZERO` must NEVER reach the forge/self_accept path when a seed-epoch lineage exists. Fail-closed: an old sidecar omitting `epoch_nonce` decodes as a version mismatch (`UnknownVersion`, schema v1 vs v2), never a default-to-zero eta0. Authority split preserved: snapshot = ledger/chain skeleton; seed-epoch sidecar = the Praos consensus inputs incl. eta0. (Replay-equivalence obligation: same checkpoint + same sidecar ‚Üí byte-identical WarmStart eta0 overlay ‚Üí same forge view.) |
| **Code** | `crates/ade_ledger/src/seed_consensus_inputs.rs` (`SeedEpochConsensusInputs.epoch_nonce` field + versioned codec, `SEED_CINPUT_SCHEMA_VERSION = 2` fail-closed on the schema change); `crates/ade_runtime/src/seed_consensus_merge.rs` (merge persists `canonical.epoch_nonce`); `crates/ade_runtime/src/bootstrap.rs` (`bootstrap_initial_state` overlays the recovered sidecar `epoch_nonce` onto `chain_dep.epoch_nonce` + `evolving_nonce`) |
| **Tests** | `crates/ade_runtime/src/bootstrap.rs`: `warm_start_overlays_recovered_eta0_onto_chain_dep_g_n`, `warm_start_restores_seed_epoch_consensus_inputs_byte_identical`. `crates/ade_ledger/src/seed_consensus_inputs.rs`: `seed_cinput_decode_rejects_unknown_version`, `seed_epoch_consensus_inputs_round_trips_byte_identical`. `crates/ade_testkit/src/consensus/genesis_pinning.rs`: `pinning_preseed_warmstart_roundtrip_faithful`. (5 named; all resolve on disk.) |
| **CI** | `ci/ci_check_warmstart_eta0_overlay.sh` (NEW ‚Äî pins that the sidecar carries `epoch_nonce`, that WarmStart overlays it onto `chain_dep.epoch_nonce`, and that the forge VRF input is `praos_vrf_input(slot, epoch_nonce)`, never a defaulted/zero eta0) |

### `T-REC-05`: Replay/recovery equivalence including forged admits ‚Äî same anchor + same WAL (incl. forged AdmitBlock) ‚Üí byte-identical recovered tip + ledger fp‚Ä¶

_tier: true ¬∑ status: enforced_ ¬∑ _introduced_in: PHASE4-N-U ¬∑ strengthened_in: PHASE4-N-AD, PHASE4-N-AE, PHASE4-N-AH, PHASE4-N-AI, PHASE4-N-AK_

> **Strengthened in PHASE4-N-AK (AK-S1, 2026-06-10).** Replay-equivalence now extends to the recovered live-follow START tip. `DC-NODE-31` persists the bootstrap anchor point as provenance-bound recovery state and resolves the FindIntersect start from it; the new test `same_store_same_anchor_point_same_findintersect_start` proves *same recovered store + same WAL ‚áí same anchor point ‚áí same `BootstrapState.tip` ‚áí same FindIntersect start* ‚Äî the recovered-tip surface is now byte-identical across runs. (Prior PHASE4-N-AE strengthening extended replay-equivalence to the recover‚ÜíFOLLOW‚Üíwarm-start path; PHASE4-N-AD to a multi-block forged progression.)

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | `docs/planning/phase4-n-u-forged-block-durability-invariants.md` |
| **Requirement** | Same `BootstrapAnchor` + same WAL (including forged `AdmitBlock` entries) ‚Üí byte-identical recovered durable tip and ledger fingerprint. Same recovered/bootstrapped state + same ordered canonical block feed + same deterministic clock-tick schedule + same leadership/key inputs + same shutdown schedule ‚Üí byte-identical durable outputs (tip, WAL image, checkpoints, halt state), INCLUDING forged-then-admitted blocks. Extends `T-REC-01/02/03` from received-only to forged+received durable progression; rides the existing snapshot + forward-replay recovery law (NOT full-genesis replay) ‚Äî no new durability law. |
| **Code** | `crates/ade_node/src/node_lifecycle.rs` (`warm_start_recovery`: sidecar-reconstructed `era_schedule`/`ledger_view` + forward-replay via `bootstrap_initial_state` + fingerprint fail-fast guard ‚Äî asserts recovered ledger fp == the WAL-tail `post_fp`; **PHASE4-N-AE.C:** the recover‚Üífollow `ForwardSyncState.prior_fp` is seeded from `fingerprint(&state.ledger).combined` at both lifecycle sites); `crates/ade_node/src/node_sync.rs` (`admit_forged_block_durably ‚Üí pump_block`); `crates/ade_runtime/src/bootstrap.rs` (`bootstrap_initial_state` warm-start forward-replay ‚Äî reused; **PHASE4-N-AK:** the recovered-anchor `resolve_live_follow_start` surface that the new test exercises) |
| **Tests** | `crates/ade_node/src/node_sync.rs`: `forge_kill_then_warm_start_recovers_same_tip_via_forward_replay` (forge block 0 ‚Üí admit ‚Üí kill ‚Üí reopen ‚Üí `warm_start_recovery` ‚Üí recovered tip slot+hash == the pre-kill durable tip; reaching `Ok` with the same tip under the fingerprint guard IS byte-identical replay equivalence). **PHASE4-N-AD:** `forge_tip_successor_kill_then_warm_start_recovers_block_one` (`node_sync.rs`; multi-block forged progression recovers byte-identically). **PHASE4-N-AE.C (recover‚Üífollow path):** `recover_follow_forge_two_runs_byte_identical` (`crates/ade_node/tests/phase4_n_ae_recover_serve_continuity_diag.rs`), `recover_follow_kill_warm_start_chains_from_ledger_fp` + `recover_follow_two_runs_byte_identical` (`node_sync.rs`). **PHASE4-N-AK:** `same_store_same_anchor_point_same_findintersect_start` (`crates/ade_runtime/src/bootstrap.rs`; same recovered store ‚áí same anchor point ‚áí same FindIntersect start ‚Äî extends the equivalence to the recovered live-follow tip). Carried by `DC-WAL-04`'s `warm_start_drops_orphan_block_above_wal_tail` (no-orphan recovery). (6 named; all resolve on disk.) |
| **CI** | **N/A ‚Äî test-enforced** (`ci_script = ""` in the registry, by design ‚Äî NOT an enforcement gap). A forged-block durable tip carries no snapshot-at-tip; `warm_start_recovery` recovers it by FORWARD-REPLAY from the genesis slot-0 snapshot over the durable WAL block, and its fingerprint guard asserts recovered fp == WAL-tail `post_fp`. The equivalence is proven by `forge_kill_then_warm_start_recovers_same_tip_via_forward_replay` (riding the already-CI-gated `bootstrap_initial_state` warm-start branch, proven by `recover_node_state`'s `recovery_crash_at_phase_sync_byte_identical`). **PHASE4-N-AE.C note:** the recover‚Üífollow replay-equivalence clause IS additionally fenced by `ci/ci_check_recover_follow_wal_lineage.sh` via the sibling `DC-WAL-02`. **PHASE4-N-AK note:** the recovered-anchor start-tip clause rides the `ci/ci_check_bootstrap_closure.sh` (`CN-NODE-01`) fence over `bootstrap.rs`. _Honest-drift note: the PHASE4-N-U `cluster.md ¬ß8` CE-5 named a gate `ci_check_forged_tip_recovery.sh` and CE-6 named a test `forge_two_clean_runs_byte_identical` ‚Äî NEITHER was created literally; S2 enforced replay-equivalence via the test above. See Generation notes._ |

### `T-REC-06`: Rollback-materialization replay-equivalence ‚Äî a block that validates on live admit MUST NOT fail rollback-materialize replay; `materialize_rolled_back_state` overlays the recovered eta0 (same as live admit) onto the replay `chain_dep` before the VRF fold‚Ä¶

_tier: true ¬∑ status: enforced_ ¬∑ _introduced_in: PHASE4-N-AN_

> **NEW in PHASE4-N-AN (AN-S2, repro-first).** Surfaced by the CE-AI-6 reorg: the live single-best-peer rollback-follow died at `ReplayFailedAt VrfCert` because `materialize_rolled_back_state` reconstructed the replay `chain_dep` from the persisted snapshot's placeholder/genesis `epoch_nonce` (`Nonce::ZERO`), so a rolled-back block's header VRF was verified against the WRONG nonce. PHASE4-N-AN overlays the recovered seed-epoch eta0 (the `SeedEpochConsensusInputs.epoch_nonce` sidecar) onto the `nearest_le` snapshot `chain_dep` BEFORE the replay-forward `block_validity` fold ‚Äî via the NEW single BLUE authority `PraosChainDepState::overlay_recovered_eta0`, the SAME overlay WarmStart bootstrap uses for the live-admit `chain_dep` ‚Äî so live admit and rollback replay validate the header VRF against the SAME `praos_vrf_input(slot, eta0)`. **VRF validation strength is UNCHANGED on the rollback path (no bypass / skip / loosening):** a `None` overlay (cold-start / no recovered sidecar) keeps the snapshot nonce as-is, and a WRONG eta0 still fails the header VRF (proven by a dedicated regression). AN-S1 (`dbf31c7a`) reproduced the `VrfCert` mechanically; AN-S2 (`deaa6e28`) flipped it to `Valid`. **SCOPE (deliberately narrow):** the recovered seed epoch (no epoch-boundary crossing within the follow window ‚Äî eta0 is the constant epoch nonce); a multi-epoch rollback nonce-evolution is a named out-of-scope follow-on. Unblocks CE-AI-6.

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | `docs/planning/phase4-n-an-rollback-materialize-eta0-invariants.md` + `docs/clusters/completed/PHASE4-N-AN/cluster.md` (planning + cluster docs; no normative-doc anchor in `.idd-config.json` `normative_docs` ‚Äî the established N-series recover‚Üífollow pattern, surfaced here, not a new gap) |
| **Requirement** | A block that validates during live admit (against the eta0-overlaid `chain_dep`, `T-REC-04`) MUST NOT fail rollback-materialize replay because materialization substituted a different nonce source. `materialize_rolled_back_state` (the SOLE rolled-back-state authority, `CN-STORE-07`) MUST reconstruct the replay `chain_dep` with the SAME recovered eta0 (epoch nonce) the live-admit path uses (`praos_vrf_input(slot, eta0)`, `DC-CINPUT-03`); the persisted snapshot's placeholder/genesis `epoch_nonce` MUST NOT reach VRF verification on the rollback-replay path. Same recovered store + same ordered WAL/feed ‚áí same `chain_dep` inputs ‚áí same `block_validity` result on the live-admit and rollback paths. eta0 is the recovered canonical input (the seed-epoch `SeedEpochConsensusInputs.epoch_nonce` sidecar) ‚Äî never peer data, wall-clock, CLI re-supply, or a re-query. VRF validation strength is UNCHANGED on the rollback path (no bypass / skip / loosening). Scope: the recovered seed epoch (no epoch-boundary crossing in the follow window); a multi-epoch rollback nonce-evolution is a named out-of-scope follow-on. |
| **Code** | `crates/ade_core/src/consensus/praos_state.rs` (`PraosChainDepState::overlay_recovered_eta0` ‚Äî the NEW single BLUE eta0-overlay authority; sets both `epoch_nonce` and `evolving_nonce` to the recovered eta0; shared by WarmStart bootstrap AND rollback materialization); `crates/ade_ledger/src/rollback/materialize.rs` (`materialize_rolled_back_state` ‚Äî gains the `recovered_eta0: Option<&Nonce>` param and overlays it onto the `nearest_le` snapshot `chain_dep` via `overlay_recovered_eta0` BEFORE the degenerate return AND the replay-forward `block_validity` fold); `crates/ade_ledger/src/seed_consensus_inputs.rs` (`SeedEpochConsensusInputs.epoch_nonce` ‚Äî the persisted recovered eta0 carrier); `crates/ade_runtime/src/forward_sync/reducer.rs` (`ForwardSyncState.recovered_eta0` ‚Äî the GREEN carrier field); `crates/ade_node/src/node_lifecycle.rs` (`apply_chain_event` threads `state.seed_epoch_consensus_inputs` eta0 ‚Äî i.e. `fwd.recovered_eta0` ‚Äî into the `materialize_rolled_back_state` call on the live rollback-follow path the CE-AI-6 reorg hit); `crates/ade_runtime/src/bootstrap.rs` (the WarmStart restore-before-materialize reorder + eta0 passed into the WarmStart materialize ‚Äî ALSO fixes warm-start replay from a NON-bare store, the SAME root cause) |
| **Tests** | `crates/ade_ledger/src/rollback/materialize.rs`: `rollback_materialize_overlays_recovered_eta0_replay_equivalent` (CE-AN-2/3 ‚Äî `None` overlay ‚áí `VrfCert`; `Some(eta0)` ‚áí `Valid` + the materialized `epoch_nonce == eta0 ==` the live-admit nonce basis), `rollback_materialize_does_not_bypass_vrf_on_wrong_eta0` (CE-AN-4 ‚Äî a WRONG eta0 still fails the header VRF: the overlay is NOT a bypass). (2 named; both resolve on disk; backed by `ade_ledger` materialize 7/7, `ade_runtime` bootstrap 36/36 + `receive_rollback_integration` 5/5, `wal_rollback_ai_s1` 13/13, `ade_node` 338/338.) |
| **CI** | `ci/ci_check_rollback_materialize_eta0.sh` (NEW, PHASE4-N-AN ‚Äî guards: (A) the SINGLE overlay authority `PraosChainDepState::overlay_recovered_eta0` exists; (B) `materialize_rolled_back_state` takes the `recovered_eta0: Option<&Nonce>` param AND applies the overlay; (C) NO VRF bypass ‚Äî the replay still runs `block_validity`, no skip/unchecked; (D) eta0 is sourced from the recovered sidecar (`ForwardSyncState.recovered_eta0` via `apply_chain_event`; bootstrap via the seed-epoch sidecar) ‚Äî never peer/CLI/wall-clock; (E) the replay-equivalence + no-bypass regression tests exist; (F) `T-REC-06` is enforced in the registry). _Live-evidence note (NOT a gap): the mechanical contract above is fully CI-enforced; the LIVE convergence WITNESS ‚Äî **CE-AN-LIVE / CE-AI-6** (2026-06-11, fresh hermetic 2-pool bridge venue, magic 42: bare-anchor recover @ slot 162 ‚Üí induced peer reorg ‚Üí Ade FOLLOWED the `RollBackward` with a strict slot regression admit 371 ‚Üí 361 ‚Üí re-converged `agreement_verdict{agreed}` @ slot 383 with our_hash == peer_hash (the reorged tip), 16 admits / 2 agreed / 0 diverged / Ade ALIVE / 0 `VrfCert`/`ReplayFailedAt` ‚Äî the eta0 overlay HELD through the live rollback; without AN-S2 Ade died here with `ReplayFailedAt VrfCert`) ‚Äî is operator-produced and OUTSIDE-REPO (competition-secrecy + no-credential-leak discipline), with a scrubbed pointer in `T-REC-06.open_obligation`. It is NOT a CI-replayable artifact; it is recorded explicitly, not hidden._

## DC ‚Äî Derived Cardano Compatibility Invariants (Project Constitution ¬ß3)

Derived invariants ‚Äî the concrete Cardano-compatibility obligations (codec fidelity, ledger/tx validity, consensus, credential fidelity, storage/WAL, session reassembly, node lifecycle, epoch discipline) that realize the true invariants against the real protocol.

_195 rules._

### `DC-ADMIT-01`: Closed AgreementVerdict sum (GREEN evidence, not authority): exactly four‚Ä¶

_tier: derived ¬∑ status: enforced_

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | docs/planning/phase4-n-m-b-admission-invariants.md ¬ß1 (I-B1) + ¬ß6 table |
| **Requirement** | Closed AgreementVerdict sum (GREEN evidence, not authority): exactly four variants ‚Äî Agreed{our_hash,peer_hash}, Lagging{our_slot,peer_slot}, Diverged{our_hash,peer_hash,slot}, InputNotFound{tx_in}. Each variant has narrow comparison semantics per the cluster invariants sketch ¬ß1 (I-B1). The reducer compares already-authoritative outputs (CN-CONS-08 admit verdict + peer's announced tip); it never decides validity, chain selection, or canonical state. See memory [[feedback-evidence-reducers-are-green-not-authority]] for the classification doctrine this rule embodies. |
| **Code** | `crates/ade_node/src/admission/verdict.rs`::{AgreementVerdict, BlockAdmitOutcome, derive} |
| **Tests** | `ade_node::admission::verdict::tests::verdict_agreed_when_hashes_match`, `ade_node::admission::verdict::tests::verdict_diverged_when_our_admit_differs_from_peer_hash`, `ade_node::admission::verdict::tests::verdict_diverged_when_admit_invalid_at_same_slot`, `ade_node::admission::verdict::tests::verdict_lagging_when_peer_ahead_of_our_slot`, `ade_node::admission::verdict::tests::verdict_input_not_found_when_admit_missing_input`, `ade_node::admission::verdict::tests::verdict_lagging_when_peer_tip_is_origin`, `ade_node::admission::verdict::tests::verdict_derive_is_pure_two_runs_byte_identical`, `ade_node::admission::verdict::tests::verdict_kind_discriminator_round_trips_each_variant` |
| **CI** | `ci/ci_check_lagging_is_evidence_only.sh` |

### `DC-ADMIT-08`: Lagging is evidence-state only: AgreementVerdict::Lagging means the local‚Ä¶

_tier: derived ¬∑ status: enforced_

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | docs/planning/phase4-n-m-b-admission-invariants.md ¬ß1 (I-B1) + ¬ß2 (¬¨P-B8) |
| **Requirement** | Lagging is evidence-state only: AgreementVerdict::Lagging means the local admitted chain is a prefix of the comparison target (peer's announced chain) up to the peer's announced slot. It MUST NOT be treated as success / healthy / live-ready / consensus-equivalent by any caller. CI grep (ci_check_lagging_is_evidence_only.sh) forbids: - Lagging matched as part of a success-result pattern (Ok(Lagging), Lagging=>true, etc.) outside the verdict reducer and its tests; - Any caller passing a Lagging verdict into a "ready" / "healthy" / "live" predicate. |

### `DC-CINPUT-01`: WARM-START VERIFICATION CAPABILITY (authority surface ‚Äî NOT production‚Ä¶

_tier: derived ¬∑ status: enforced_

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | docs/clusters/PHASE4-N-F-A/cluster.md; A3a-wal-provenance-entry.md; A3b-warm-start-restore.md |
| **Requirement** | WARM-START VERIFICATION CAPABILITY (authority surface ‚Äî NOT production restart). The seed-epoch consensus-input import is a canonical, replay-reconstructable WAL fact: an additive closed WalEntry::SeedEpochConsensusInputsImported variant (distinct tag; does NOT participate in the AdmitBlock prior_fp/post_fp chain), appended AFTER the sidecar put (the WAL append is the commit point). Replay reconstructs a typed RecoveredBootstrapProvenance view (exactly one per store/anchor; duplicate or anchor-mismatch fails closed). Given that view, bootstrap_initial_state's warm-start branch (RequiredFromRecoveredProvenance) restores the sidecar and verifies it fail-closed: sidecar present, blake2b_256 == provenance.sidecar_hash, A1 decode, anchor_fp + epoch_no binding, byte- identity re-encode ‚Äî exposing the recovered SeedEpochConsensusInputs or halting (typed BootstrapError, EXIT_AUTHORITY_FATAL_DECODE, no bundle fallback). This is proven on the AUTHORITY SURFACE (bootstrap_initial_state exercised directly); no production mode is wired to it (node.rs run_node_until_shutdown + recover_node_state are test-only; produce_mode cold-starts). The PRODUCTION restart path is this rule's open obligation, deferred to PHASE4-N-F-C. |
| **Code** | `crates/ade_ledger/src/wal/event.rs` (SeedEpochConsensusInputsImported, tag 3); `crates/ade_ledger/src/wal/replay.rs` (ReplayOutcome + RecoveredBootstrapProvenance); `crates/ade_runtime/src/seed_consensus_provenance.rs` (append helper); `crates/ade_runtime/src/bootstrap.rs` (SeedEpochConsensusSource, BootstrapState, restore_seed_epoch_consensus_inputs) |
| **Tests** | `wal_seed_cinput_entry_round_trips_byte_identical`, `replay_yields_bootstrap_provenance_view`, `replay_rejects_duplicate_provenance_entry`, `replay_rejects_anchor_mismatched_provenance_entry`, `admit_block_chain_unaffected_by_provenance_entry`, `warm_start_restores_seed_epoch_consensus_inputs_byte_identical`, `warm_start_fails_closed_on_missing_sidecar`, `warm_start_fails_closed_on_hash_mismatch`, `warm_start_fails_closed_on_anchor_mismatch`, `warm_start_fails_closed_on_epoch_mismatch`, `warm_start_required_provenance_rejects_malformed_sidecar`, `warm_start_never_falls_back_to_consensus_inputs_path`, `warm_start_recovers_seed_epoch_consensus_inputs_byte_identical`, `warm_start_fails_closed_on_missing_wal_provenance`, `warm_start_fails_closed_on_duplicate_provenance`, `warm_start_fails_closed_on_multiple_anchor_lineages`, `warm_start_dispatch_succeeds_end_to_end`, `node_sync_kill_then_warm_start_recovers_same_tip` |
| **CI** | `ci/ci_check_lifecycle_owner_uses_bootstrap_initial_state.sh` |

### `DC-CINPUT-02a`: PROJECTION EQUIVALENCE. The recovered SeedEpochConsensusInputs projects‚Ä¶

| Aspect | Location |

| **Source** | docs/clusters/PHASE4-N-F-A/cluster.md; A4-projection-pooldistr-vrf.md |
| **Requirement** | PROJECTION EQUIVALENCE. The recovered SeedEpochConsensusInputs projects deterministically to the leadership-consumed PoolDistrView (the full LedgerView surface: total_active_stake, pool_active_stake, pool_vrf_keyhash, active_slots_coeff; single-epoch ‚Äî off-epoch queries return None) via PoolDistrView::from_seed_epoch_consensus_inputs, EQUIVALENT to the prior operator-bundle projection (pool_distr_view_from_consensus_inputs) for the seed epoch; and recovered eta0 (from chain_dep) drives leader_vrf_input identically. The projection is a pure BLUE field map (A2 already merged stake + VRF keyhash). This rule covers the PROJECTION only; producer CONSUMPTION of the projected recovered surface is deferred to PHASE4-N-F-C (CE-A-4b). |

### `DC-CINPUT-03`: Producer Praos VRF input `praos_vrf_input(slot, eta0)` uses the recovered eta0 overlaid at WarmStart (= cardano `mkInputVRF`)‚Ä¶

_tier: derived ¬∑ status: enforced_ ¬∑ _introduced_in: PHASE4-N-F-G-N_

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | `docs/clusters/PHASE4-N-F-G-N/cluster.md` |
| **Requirement** | The producer Praos VRF leader/header input is `praos_vrf_input(slot, eta0)` = `blake2b256(slot_be8 ‚Äñ eta0_32)` (= cardano `mkInputVRF`), where eta0 is the Cardano epoch nonce carried by the recovered `SeedEpochConsensusInputs` and overlaid onto `chain_dep` at WarmStart (`T-REC-04`). A forged Conway header therefore verifies under a real peer's `mkInputVRF(slot, eta0)`. The VRF variant is UNCHANGED ‚Äî IETF draft-03, 80-byte proof (verified against real mainnet + preprod Conway headers, both draft-03); the fix is the recovered eta0 SOURCING, not the crypto. No draft-13/batch-compat migration, no C1-only branch, no genesis-derived nonce. |
| **Code** | `crates/ade_core/src/consensus/vrf_cert.rs` (`praos_vrf_input = blake2b256(slot_be8 ‚Äñ eta0_32) = mkInputVRF`); `crates/ade_runtime/src/producer/signing.rs` (`vrf_prove` over the alpha); `crates/ade_ledger/src/seed_consensus_inputs.rs` (`epoch_nonce` sidecar field); `crates/ade_runtime/src/bootstrap.rs` (overlay onto `chain_dep`) |
| **Tests** | `crates/ade_runtime/src/bootstrap.rs`: `warm_start_overlays_recovered_eta0_onto_chain_dep_g_n`. `crates/ade_testkit/src/consensus/genesis_pinning.rs`: `pinning_praos_vrf_input_and_threshold_match_fixture`. `crates/ade_runtime/src/seed_consensus_merge.rs`: `recovered_surface_projects_pooldistrview_and_expected_vrf_input`. (3 named; all resolve on disk.) |
| **CI** | `ci/ci_check_warmstart_eta0_overlay.sh` (shared with `T-REC-04` ‚Äî pins the forge VRF input is `praos_vrf_input(slot, epoch_nonce)` over the recovered/overlaid eta0) |

### `DC-CINPUT-04`: Feed/receive-side header-validation consensus view (leader threshold) is the recovered consensus surface, never an empty placeholder‚Ä¶

_tier: derived ¬∑ status: enforced_ ¬∑ _introduced_in: PHASE4-N-F-G-P_

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | `docs/clusters/PHASE4-N-F-G-P/cluster.md` |
| **Requirement** | The receive/feed-path header-validation consensus view ‚Äî the `LedgerView` passed to `block_validity ‚Üí validate_and_apply_header` for Step 5 (VRF-keyhash binding) and Step 7 (leader threshold) ‚Äî MUST be the RECOVERED consensus surface: ASC + total_active_stake + pool_distribution + per-pool VRF keyhash, projected from the recovered `SeedEpochConsensusInputs` via the SAME single authority the forge uses (`PoolDistrView::from_seed_epoch_consensus_inputs`). It is NEVER an empty/zero/default placeholder. Forge and feed validation share ONE recovered consensus surface. Fail-closed: a missing recovered `SeedEpochConsensusInputs` on a feed-wired node (`--peer`) ‚Üí a structured `NodeLifecycleError::FeedMissingRecoveredConsensusInputs` / halt ‚Äî never an empty view, never "accept if missing stake," never a leader-threshold bypass. NARROW: the header-validation consensus view ONLY; the authoritative ledger state stays the authority for ledger verdicts. Receive-side mirror of `DC-CINPUT-02b`; same class as `DC-CINPUT-03` / `T-REC-04` but a different recovered input (stake distribution + ASC, not the nonce) on a different path (feed, not forge). |
| **Code** | `crates/ade_node/src/node_lifecycle.rs` (the forge-on On-arm feed `ledger_view` is `PoolDistrView::from_seed_epoch_consensus_inputs(recovered)` ‚Äî NOT `PoolDistrView::new(empty)`; fail-closed `FeedMissingRecoveredConsensusInputs` when `--peer` is set but the recovered record is absent); `crates/ade_ledger/src/consensus_view.rs` (`PoolDistrView::from_seed_epoch_consensus_inputs` ‚Äî the single projection authority shared with the forge); `crates/ade_node/src/node_sync.rs` (`forge_one_from_recovered` uses the SAME projection ‚Äî `DC-CINPUT-02b`) |
| **Tests** | `crates/ade_node/tests/forge_succeeds.rs`: `feed_header_validates_against_recovered_surface_not_empty_view`. (1 named; resolves on disk.) |
| **CI** | `ci/ci_check_feed_leader_threshold_view.sh` (NEW ‚Äî pins that the feed header-validation view is derived from the recovered consensus surface, not a defaulted / empty distribution) |

### `DC-CONS-03`: Praos chain selection ordering: block number first, then Praos TiebreakerView‚Ä¶

_tier: derived ¬∑ status: enforced_ ¬∑ _strengthened_in: PHASE4-N-B, PHASE4-N-AI, PHASE4-N-AO_

> **Strengthened in PHASE4-N-AO (`strengthened_in += PHASE4-N-AO`).** This BLUE fork-choice ordering is now the LIVE MULTI-CANDIDATE resolver target: `DC-NODE-36` routes the aggregated multi-peer candidate SET (built BLUE-safely per `DC-NODE-35`) into `select_best_chain`, and the CE-AO-6 natural two-producer SELECT pass proved the live convergence (`CN-CONS-03` flipped to `enforced`). `DC-CONS-03` itself is byte-unchanged.
>
> **Strengthened in PHASE4-N-AI.** This BLUE fork-choice ordering is now the resolver target for the live Participant venue: `DC-NODE-24` routes a validated peer header summary into the existing `ade_runtime::consensus::chain_selector` orchestrator ‚Üí `select_best_chain` (this rule), and `DC-NODE-25`/`26` apply + reconcile its outcome to the durable stores. `DC-CONS-03` itself is byte-unchanged ‚Äî the rule was NOT weakened or rewritten; PHASE4-N-AI WIRES it into the live receive path (single-best-peer FOLLOW). Broad multi-peer convergence (`CN-CONS-03`) stays `declared`.

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | Project constitution ¬ß3, ouroboros-consensus (pin at code-lock); CN-CONS-01 |
| **Requirement** | Praos chain selection ordering: block number first, then Praos TiebreakerView (slot, issuer, op-cert issue number, VRF output). Density-based ordering is reserved for Genesis/catch-up and must not be used for caught-up Praos fork-choice. |
| **Code** | `crates/ade_core/src/consensus/fork_choice.rs`, `crates/ade_core/src/consensus/candidate.rs`, `crates/ade_runtime/src/consensus/candidate_fragment.rs` |
| **Tests** | `consensus::fork_choice::tests::tiebreaker_prefer_lower_slot_wins`, `consensus::fork_choice::tests::tiebreaker_prefer_higher_op_cert_wins_on_equal_slot_and_issuer`, `consensus::fork_choice::tests::tiebreaker_prefer_lower_vrf_value_wins_on_full_tie`, `consensus::fork_choice::tests::no_candidates_returns_no_candidates_error`, `consensus::fork_choice::tests::equal_to_current_keeps_current_via_tiebreaker_loss`, `consensus::candidate::tests::tiebreaker_view_eq_is_field_wise`, `consensus::candidate::tests::candidate_fragment_carries_anchor_block_no`, `higher_block_no_wins`, `equal_block_no_tiebreaker_decides`, `fork_before_immutable_tip_rejected`, `exceeded_rollback_rejected`, `tiebreaker_loss_keeps_current`, `replay_is_deterministic`, `reject_reason_bytes_are_stable`, `no_candidates_returns_error` |

### `DC-CONS-05`: Authoritative rollback must never exceed the security parameter k measured in‚Ä¶

The four-cell contract below is unchanged.

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | Project constitution ¬ß3, ouroboros-consensus consensus report |
| **Requirement** | Authoritative rollback must never exceed the security parameter k measured in blocks (mainnet k = 2160). Rollback requests deeper than k return ExceededRollback. Forecast/stability windows may be slot-based but must accommodate at least k+1 blocks. |

### `DC-CONS-09`: Consensus-derived queries for slots beyond the ledger-view safe zone return‚Ä¶

_tier: derived ¬∑ status: enforced_

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | Project constitution ¬ß3, DC-EPOCH-02 |
| **Requirement** | Consensus-derived queries for slots beyond the ledger-view safe zone return OutsideForecastRange, never guessed values. The bound is derived from era history + safe zone + HFC schedule, not encoded as a magic constant in caller code. |

### `DC-CONS-20`: ChainDb-ledger-chain_dep lockstep: a successful receive-side admission updates‚Ä¶

_tier: derived ¬∑ status: enforced_ ¬∑ _strengthened_in: PHASE4-N-I, PHASE4-N-J, PHASE4-N-Y, PHASE4-N-AI, PHASE4-N-AO_

> **Strengthened in PHASE4-N-AO (`strengthened_in += PHASE4-N-AO`).** The lockstep reducer now applies a LIVE fork-switch: a `RolledBack(fork_anchor)` + `ChainSelected(body)√óN` from `apply_fork_switch` (`DC-NODE-37`) advances/rolls-back ChainDb + LedgerState + PraosChainDepState as ONE structural transition through this path ‚Äî still NO second apply path. The four-cell contract below is unchanged.
>
> **Strengthened in PHASE4-N-AI.** This lockstep reducer is one of the THREE reused durable-apply authorities the live fork-choice apply driver (`DC-NODE-25`) rides ‚Äî a `ChainSelected`/`RolledBack` outcome advances or rolls back ChainDb + LedgerState + PraosChainDepState as ONE structural transition through this path; there is NO second apply path. `DC-NODE-26` then reconciles the orchestrator's `current_tip` against the durable `ChainDb::tip`. The four-cell contract below is unchanged.

A successful RollBackward rolls back all three to the same slot. No path leaves them out of sync; no partial admission; no partial rollback. |

### `DC-CONS-23`: Own-forged stale-tip race safety by extend-only durable admit‚Ä¶

_tier: derived ¬∑ status: enforced_ ¬∑ _introduced_in: PHASE4-N-U ¬∑ strengthened_in: PHASE4-N-AE_

> **Strengthened in PHASE4-N-AE (AE.B, 2026-06-07).** The extend-only durable-admit safety is now carried onto the recover‚Üífollow‚Üíforge‚Üíserve spine: the AE forge builds on the durable servable tip (the followed peer tip, `DC-NODE-15`), and the forged successor enters durability through the SAME extend-only `admit_via_block_validity` chokepoint ‚Äî no admit-time fork-choice was added on the recover‚Üífollow path. `DC-CONS-03` remains the fork-choice authority in the follow / `chain_selector` paths.

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | `docs/planning/phase4-n-u-forged-block-durability-invariants.md`; **PHASE4-N-AE:** `docs/clusters/PHASE4-N-AE/cluster.md` |
| **Requirement** | An own-forged candidate is admitted to the durable tip ONLY if it EXTENDS the current durable tip at admit time, through the existing EXTEND-ONLY durable admit validation path (`receive_apply ‚Üí admit_via_block_validity ‚Üí block_validity`, incl. `header_position`). If a feed block advanced the tip after forge time (the forge‚Üîfeed race), the forged candidate FAILS CLOSED ‚Äî via header-position / `prev_hash` validation, `TipBeforeDurable`, or WAL `prior_fp` mismatch ‚Äî and the next forge tick re-forges on the current durable tip. N-U adds NO admit-time fork-choice and NO own-block override path. `DC-CONS-03` (`select_best_chain`) remains the fork-choice authority in the follow / `chain_selector` paths ‚Äî NOT the durable admit. |
| **Code** | `crates/ade_ledger/src/receive/{reducer,admitted}.rs` (extend-only `admit_via_block_validity` ‚Äî reused); `crates/ade_ledger/src/block_validity/header_position.rs` (`prev_hash`/position fail-closed ‚Äî reused); `crates/ade_node/src/node_sync.rs` (`admit_forged_block_durably ‚Üí pump_block`, no admit-time fork-choice) |
| **Tests** | `crates/ade_node/tests/forge_succeeds.rs`: `stale_tip_forge_fails_closed` (a re-mint block 0 admitted against a chain already at block 0 fails closed at the extend-only durable admit; the durable tip is unchanged). (1 named; resolves on disk.) |
| **CI** | `ci/ci_check_forged_durable_admit_via_pump.sh` (fences `select_best_chain`/`fork_choice` absent from the driver ‚Äî no admit-time fork-choice was added; `DC-CONS-03` stays the fork-choice authority in the follow/`chain_selector` paths) |

### `DC-CONS-24`: Forged parent hash byte-equals the peer-visible selected tip‚Ä¶

_tier: derived ¬∑ status: enforced_ ¬∑ _introduced_in: PHASE4-N-AE_

> **NEW in PHASE4-N-AE (AE.A, 2026-06-06).** When the forge is admissible (CaughtUp, `DC-NODE-15`), the ForgeTick arm forges on `selected_tip = ChainDb::tip()` = the durable servable tip = the followed peer tip. `forge_header_position` sets the successor `prev_hash = PrevHash::Block(selected_tip.hash)` and `block_no = last_block_no + 1`, so the forged parent hash BYTE-EQUALS the peer-visible selected tip ‚Äî never inferred from block number alone.

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | `docs/clusters/PHASE4-N-AE/cluster.md`; `docs/clusters/PHASE4-N-AE/slices/AE.A.md` |
| **Requirement** | The forged successor's `prev_hash` byte-equals the followed peer tip hash AND its `block_no == followed_tip.block_no + 1`. Parent identity is the canonical hash, never inferred from block number alone. |
| **Code** | `crates/ade_node/src/node_lifecycle.rs` (`run_relay_loop_with_sched` ForgeTick CaughtUp arm forges on `selected_tip` == the durable servable tip == the followed peer tip); `crates/ade_node/src/node_sync.rs` (`forge_header_position` sets `prev_hash = PrevHash::Block(selected_tip.hash)`) |
| **Tests** | `crates/ade_node/tests/phase4_n_ae_recover_serve_continuity_diag.rs::forge_on_followed_tip_proceeds_with_parent_byte_equal` (reads the forged `prev_hash` from the inner Conway header body ‚Äî preserved CBOR, never inferred from `block_no` ‚Äî and asserts byte-equality to the followed peer tip hash + `block_no + 1`). (1 named; resolves on disk.) |
| **CI** | `ci/ci_check_forge_followed_tip_admission.sh` (assertion (b): the classifier compares hash AND block_no) |

| **Requirement** | KES signing transcript equivalence and verification symmetry. ### `DC-CRYPTO-05`: KES evolution discipline: evolve(k_i) -> k_{i+1} is one-way. The evolved key‚Ä¶

_tier: derived ¬∑ status: enforced_

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | docs/planning/phase4-n-c-invariants.md ¬ß1 (NC-KES-2); docs/planning/phase4-n-p-invariants.md ¬ß1 (I6); Cardano Sum6KES specification |
| **Requirement** | KES evolution discipline: evolve(k_i) -> k_{i+1} is one-way. The evolved key signs period i+1 and MUST NOT sign for period i. RED kes_sign is forbidden when the requested period > current_period + evolutions_remaining; kes_evolve is forbidden when to < from or to > from + evolutions_remaining. Forward secrecy is a RED-shell discipline; BLUE has no recovery path if RED violates it. After PHASE4-N-P S5 the underlying algorithm (`ade_crypto::kes_sum::Sum6Kes::update_kes`) is BLUE-owned; per-field zeroize on Drop of consumed sub-seeds is implemented via `ZeroizingSeed` (DC-CRYPTO-08). |
| **Code** | `crates/ade_runtime/src/producer/signing.rs` (kes_update, kes_sign); `crates/ade_crypto/src/kes_sum/sum.rs` (SumKes::update_kes + ZeroizingSeed Drop) |
| **Tests** | `kes_update_chain_matches_reference`, `kes_sign_rejects_period_past_evolutions_remaining`, `kes_update_rejects_backwards_evolution`, `zeroizing_seed_drop_overwrites_bytes` |
| **CI** | `ci/ci_check_private_key_custody.sh`, `ci/ci_check_kes_sum_compatibility.sh` |

### `DC-CRYPTO-06`: Ade-native KES envelope is the sole accepted hot-signing-key envelope format‚Ä¶

_tier: derived ¬∑ status: enforced_

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | docs/clusters/PHASE4-N-O/S1.md ¬ß1; docs/active/op-ops-04-ade-native-kes-flow.md (operator spec verbatim) |
| **Requirement** | Ade-native KES envelope is the sole accepted hot-signing-key envelope format. Closed grammar `ade.kes.seed.v1`: load-bearing fields {`format`, `role`, `crypto`, `seed_32`, `period_idx`, `format_version`} are validated with `#[serde(deny_unknown_fields)]`; optional metadata {`genesis_hash`, `network_magic`, `created_at_slot`, `created_by`} is ignored but does not break load. The loader returns closed `AdeKesEnvelopeError` variants for every unsupported shape (UnknownEnvelopeFormat, WrongKeyRole, UnsupportedCryptoTag, MissingSeed32, MalformedSeed32, MalformedPeriodIdx, PeriodIdxOutOfRange, UnsupportedFormatVersion, MalformedJson). No fallback parser. No heuristic guess. Private-key bytes never appear in any error/log surface. |
| **Code** | `crates/ade_runtime/src/producer/ade_kes_envelope.rs` (parse, serialize, AdeKesEnvelopeError); `crates/ade_runtime/src/producer/keys.rs` (load_ade_kes_signing_key, write_ade_kes_envelope, KeyLoadError::AdeEnvelope) |
| **Tests** | `parse_round_trips_serialize`, `parse_round_trips_at_nonzero_period`, `parse_rejects_unknown_format`, `parse_rejects_wrong_role`, `parse_rejects_unsupported_crypto`, `parse_rejects_unsupported_format_version`, `parse_rejects_missing_seed_32`, `parse_rejects_malformed_seed_32_length`, `parse_rejects_uppercase_seed_hex`, `parse_rejects_period_idx_overflow`, `parse_accepts_period_idx_boundary`, `parse_rejects_unknown_load_bearing_field`, `parse_accepts_optional_metadata_fields`, `parse_rejects_malformed_json`, `serialize_does_not_leak_extra_fields`, `envelope_error_carries_no_seed_bytes` |
| **CI** | `ci/ci_check_kes_envelope_closed.sh` |

### `DC-CRYPTO-07`: cardano-cli's `KesSigningKey_ed25519_kes_2^6` envelope (the upstream `Sum6KES`‚Ä¶

_tier: derived ¬∑ status: enforced_

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | docs/clusters/PHASE4-N-O/S1.md ¬ß1; docs/clusters/PHASE4-N-P/S5.md; docs/active/op-ops-04-ade-native-kes-flow.md |
| **Requirement** | cardano-cli's `KesSigningKey_ed25519_kes_2^6` envelope (the upstream `Sum6KES` expanded-tree serialization, 608 bytes for a fresh key) is loadable via the Ade-owned BLUE deserializer (`ade_crypto::kes_sum::Sum6Kes::raw_deserialize_signing_key_kes`). After PHASE4-N-P S5, structurally-valid 608-byte payloads round-trip into a `KesSecret`; any other payload shape ‚Äî wrong size (32, 612, anything ‚âÝ 608), malformed sub-tree, inconsistent vk hash, leaf-all-zero, period > 63 tree shape ‚Äî fail-closes via `KeyLoadError::UnsupportedExpandedKesKeyFormat` (size mismatch) or `KeyLoadError::KesParse(KesParseError::*)` (structural defect). No fallback parser; the deserializer IS the structural validator. |
| **Code** | `crates/ade_runtime/src/producer/keys.rs` (load_kes_signing_key_skey routes 608-byte payloads through ade_crypto::kes_sum::Sum6Kes::raw_deserialize_signing_key_kes; wrong-size payloads return UnsupportedExpandedKesKeyFormat) |

| **CI** | `ci/ci_check_kes_envelope_closed.sh`, `ci/ci_check_kes_sum_compatibility.sh` |

### `DC-CRYPTO-08`: Ade-owned Sum6KES algorithm is Haskell-equivalent‚Ä¶

_tier: derived ¬∑ status: enforced_

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | docs/clusters/PHASE4-N-P/cluster.md; docs/planning/phase4-n-p-invariants.md ¬ß1 (I1, I2, I4, I6); ¬ß2 (N1, N9); docs/clusters/PHASE4-N-P/S4.md (cardano-cli ground-truth + prefix-divergence discovery) |
| **Requirement** | Ade-owned Sum6KES algorithm is Haskell-equivalent. `ade_crypto::kes_sum::Sum6Kes` is byte-identical to Haskell `cardano-base`'s `Sum6KES Ed25519DSIGN`: `derive_verification_key`, `gen_key_kes_from_seed_bytes`, `update_kes` (chain across all 64 periods), and `sign_kes` produce the same bytes as the Haskell reference for every (seed, period, msg) triple. Cross-impl validation against the cardano-cli ground-truth corpus is mechanically enforced under `#[cfg(test)]` only (3 throwaway 608-byte SKEY + VKEY pairs captured from `cardano-cli 11.0.0.0`; deserializing the SKEY through our impl produces the captured VK byte-for-byte). Note: `cardano-crypto` Rust 1.0.8 uses different `expand_seed` prefix bytes (0x00/0x01 vs Haskell's 0x01/0x02) ‚Äî Ade matches Haskell, NOT cardano-crypto Rust; this divergence is asserted explicitly in `sum6_kes_seed_expansion_diverges_from_cardano_crypto_rust_1_0_8`. After PHASE4-N-P S5, `KesSecret.inner` is the Ade-owned signing key; `cardano-crypto` is a `#[cfg(test)]` oracle only. No compatibility shim may construct an upstream `SumSigningKey` through unsafe layout assumptions, transmute, vendored pub(crate) access, or fork-only constructors (N9), enforced by `ci/ci_check_kes_sum_compatibility.sh` Guard 3. |
| **Code** | crates/ade_crypto/src/kes_sum/{mod,single,sum,hash,errors,period}.rs; `crates/ade_crypto/src/kes_sum/cardano_cli_corpus.rs` (#[cfg(test)] ground-truth corpus); `crates/ade_crypto/src/kes_sum/tests.rs` (35 unit tests) |
| **Tests** | `sum0_kes_signs_and_verifies_at_period_0`, `sum0_kes_rejects_period_1`, `sum0_kes_update_expires_after_period_0`, `sum0_kes_verify_rejects_wrong_message`, `sum1_kes_signs_at_period_0_and_period_1`, `sum6_kes_total_periods_is_64`, `sum6_kes_sizes_match_recurrence`, `sum6_kes_chain_advances_through_all_64_periods`, `sum6_kes_update_after_period_63_expires`, `sum6_kes_sign_rejects_period_64`, `sum6_kes_verify_rejects_wrong_period_signature`, `sum6_kes_seed_expansion_diverges_from_cardano_crypto_rust_1_0_8`, `sum6_kes_vk_diverges_from_cardano_crypto_rust_for_same_seed`, `cardano_cli_corpus_skey_deserializes_and_vk_matches_ground_truth`, `cardano_cli_corpus_sign_then_upstream_verifies`, `sum0_signing_key_debug_is_redacted`, `sum_signing_key_debug_is_redacted`, `zeroizing_seed_drop_overwrites_bytes` |
| **CI** | `ci/ci_check_kes_sum_compatibility.sh`, `ci/ci_check_private_key_custody.sh` |

### `DC-CRYPTO-09`: Sum6KES expanded signing-key serde and period inference‚Ä¶

_tier: derived ¬∑ status: enforced_

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | docs/clusters/PHASE4-N-P/cluster.md; docs/planning/phase4-n-p-invariants.md ¬ß1 (I3, I5); ¬ß2 (N2, N3, N4, N5); docs/clusters/PHASE4-N-P/period-from-zeroed-sum6-tree-shape-proof.md |
| **Requirement** | Sum6KES expanded signing-key serde and period inference. `raw_serialize_signing_key_kes` / `raw_deserialize_signing_key_kes` are byte-identical to Haskell's `rawSerialiseSignKeyKES` / `rawDeserialiseSignKeyKES` for `Sum6KES Ed25519DSIGN`. The on-disk format is exactly 608 bytes; any other payload size fails closed via `KesParseError::WrongPayloadSize`. `current_period` is uniquely inferable from which sub-seeds are zeroed in the tree (no heuristic; exactly one valid period or a closed parse error) ‚Äî implemented per the proof obligation at `docs/clusters/PHASE4-N-P/period-from-zeroed-sum6-tree-shape-proof.md`. Round-trip preserves period; serialize ‚Üí deserialize ‚Üí serialize yields byte-identical output for every period 0..=63. Malformed sub-trees (truncated child skey, wrong VK length at any recursion level, inconsistent vk0/vk1 hashes, leaf-all-zero) ‚Üí closed `KesParseError` variant; no best-effort guesswork. |
| **Code** | `crates/ade_crypto/src/kes_sum/period.rs` (period_from_zeroed_sum6_tree_shape); `crates/ade_crypto/src/kes_sum/sum.rs` (raw_serialize/raw_deserialize_signing_key_kes); `crates/ade_crypto/src/kes_sum/single.rs` (Sum0 leaf serde); `crates/ade_crypto/src/kes_sum/errors.rs` (KesParseError closed surface) |
| **Tests** | `sum6_raw_serialize_signing_key_kes_size_is_608`, `sum6_raw_serialize_signature_kes_size_is_448`, `sum6_skey_round_trip_at_every_period_0_to_63`, `sum6_signature_round_trip_at_every_period`, `period_from_zeroed_sum6_tree_shape_agrees_with_update_kes_chain`, `period_from_zeroed_sum6_tree_shape_rejects_leaf_all_zero`, `raw_deserialize_signing_key_kes_rejects_wrong_payload_size`, `raw_deserialize_signing_key_kes_rejects_leaf_all_zero`, `raw_deserialize_signing_key_kes_rejects_inconsistent_vk_left_at_level_6`, `raw_deserialize_signing_key_kes_rejects_inconsistent_vk_right_at_level_6`, `raw_deserialize_signature_kes_rejects_wrong_payload_size`, `cardano_cli_corpus_skey_round_trips_through_ade_serde`, `cardano_cli_corpus_skey_period_inference_is_zero`, `cardano_cli_corpus_negative_flip_one_byte_in_vk_left_fail_closed`, `cardano_cli_corpus_constants_have_expected_sizes` |
| **CI** | `ci/ci_check_kes_sum_compatibility.sh` |

### `DC-CRYPTO-10`: The RED signing shell evolves the operator KES key to the requested period before signing ‚Äî fail-closed backwards / beyond-lifetime‚Ä¶

_tier: derived ¬∑ status: enforced_

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | docs/clusters/completed/PHASE4-N-AC/cluster.md (archived at close); docs/evidence/c1-genesis-rehearsal-reproduction-README.md (item-4 C1 re-run finding) |
| **Requirement** | The RED signing shell must evolve the operator KES signing key to the requested KES period BEFORE signing, using the existing deterministic Sum6KES `update` primitive. It must fail closed if the requested period is before the key start (`EvolutionBackwards` ‚Äî a destroyed past period cannot be re-signed; forward-secrecy), beyond the key lifetime, or cannot be reached by sequential evolution (`EvolutionExhausted`, beyond `SUM6_MAX_PERIOD = 63`). The period is passed VERBATIM (never manually `¬± N` adjusted); evolution is fail-closed both directions (a backwards / beyond-lifetime request ‚Üí structured error + NO signature, never a key override). Signing stays RED (`T-KEY-01` preserved ‚Äî no signing in BLUE); the BLUE Sum6KES algorithm, KES verifier, forge eligibility, and wire rules are unchanged. |
| **Code** | `crates/ade_runtime/src/producer/producer_shell.rs` (`ProducerShell::kes_sign_header_advancing(&mut self, period, preimage)` = `kes_advance_to(period)?` then `kes_sign_header`; `kes_advance_to` ‚Üí the existing deterministic `kes_update` ‚Äî no-op at the current period, forward-evolves in window, fail-closed `Signing(EvolutionBackwards)` / `Signing(EvolutionExhausted)`); `crates/ade_node/src/produce_mode.rs` (the forge's single real KES sign ‚Äî `run_real_forge_inner` step 3 ‚Äî now calls `kes_sign_header_advancing`; on `Err(_)` it still returns the closed `CoordinatorEvent::ForgeFailed`) |
| **Tests** | `producer_shell.rs::tests::shell_kes_sign_header_advancing_evolves_then_signs` ‚Äî period > current evolves forward then signs; `‚Ä¶::shell_kes_sign_header_advancing_at_current_period_signs` ‚Äî period == current is a no-op evolution then signs (period-0 signing unchanged); `‚Ä¶::shell_kes_sign_header_advancing_backwards_fails_closed` ‚Äî period < current ‚Üí `EvolutionBackwards` + NO signature; `‚Ä¶::shell_kes_sign_header_advancing_beyond_lifetime_fails_closed` ‚Äî period beyond the key lifetime ‚Üí `EvolutionExhausted` + NO signature. (All 4 in `crates/ade_runtime/src/producer/producer_shell.rs::tests::`; all 4 resolve on disk, exactly one `fn <name>` each.) |
| **CI** | `ci/ci_check_kes_evolution_before_sign.sh` ‚Äî pins that the forge real KES sign uses `kes_sign_header_advancing` (NOT the raw `kes_sign_header` / `kes_sign_at`), that `kes_sign_header_advancing` calls `kes_advance_to(period)` VERBATIM before signing (no `period ¬± N` mutation), and that `kes_update` retains BOTH fail-closed guards (`EvolutionBackwards` + `EvolutionExhausted`); the standing `ci_check_no_signing_in_blue.sh` remains the BLUE `T-KEY-01` fence |

> **Introduced + enforced in PHASE4-N-AC (S1).** Surfaced by the item-4 C1 genesis-rehearsal re-run: the C1 rehearsal stopped reproducing once the private net aged past one KES period (slot ~249659 / `slotsPerKESPeriod` 129600 ‚Üí KES period 1), because the forge's only real KES sign required `kes.current_period() == requested` and nothing evolved the minted-at-period-0 key forward ‚Üí `KesPeriodNotCurrent { requested: 1, current: 0 }` on every leader slot (`succeeded = 0`). NOT a regression from N-U/AA/AB (the wire/serve/intersection path was healthy). Fix: the new `kes_sign_header_advancing` method evolves then signs; the BLUE Sum6KES algorithm + KES verifier are reused unchanged. Live proof (non-promotable rehearsal): with the fix Ade forged 3 period-1 blocks + self-accepted them, and the real cardano-node DOWNLOADED the period-1 header with NO KES/parse rejection (pre-fix: failed=5 / succeeded=0). Two pre-existing fail-closed INFO items handed to C2 (registry `evidence_notes`): (1) `kes_advance_to` zeroes the key on a FAILED advance ‚Äî UNREACHABLE via the forge (the `kes_period_in_window` + `kes_period_for_slot` pre-check bounds the period), fail-safe (a zero key signs nothing the peer accepts); (2) the opcert window upper bound `opcert_start + 63` can diverge from the absolute Sum6KES ceiling 63 when `opcert_start > 0` (real preprod opcerts) ‚Äî still fail-closed (`EvolutionExhausted`), but the C2 config must derive `kes_max_period` from the absolute ceiling, not `opcert_start + 63`.

### `DC-EPOCH-03`: Single-epoch forge containment on the --mode node spine: in this forge path, a‚Ä¶

The four-cell contract below is unchanged (no new test / CI / code locus for this rule ‚Äî the registry append records the composition, the enforcement lives in the existing seed-epoch gate plus the new `ci_check_forge_followed_tip_admission.sh` via `DC-NODE-15`).

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | docs/planning/phase4-n-f-g-invariants.md |
| **Requirement** | Single-epoch forge containment on the --mode node spine: in this forge path, a forge is valid only within the single recovered seed epoch. A candidate forge slot beyond the recovered seed epoch FAILS CLOSED -- it cannot be forged, served, or signed as a valid block. The seed-epoch nonce (eta0) is frozen at the recovered value; the forge apply path does NOT drive the BLUE CandidateFreeze / EpochBoundary nonce transitions (they exist in ade_core::consensus::nonce but nothing drives them on the forge path), so signing past the boundary with a stale eta0 is a peer-reject class and is forbidden, not silently attempted. Cross-epoch production (nonce roll + epoch transition driven from an epoch-aware tick + follow/durability) is a SEPARATE nonce-roll/epoch-transition cluster, NOT this one. The off-epoch slot fails closed with a structured local outcome (a fail-closed boundary for this single-epoch forge path, hardening DC-NODE-05's single-epoch cluster-scope containment for the live-serve path). |

### `DC-EVIDENCE-03`: Convergence-through-reorg transcript shape (CE-AI-6) ‚Äî ONE JSONL with a strict slot regression in the observed peer-block sequence + ‚â•1 AgreementVerdict{agreed} at the re-converged tip + 0 diverged; vacuous-until-committed‚Ä¶

The transcript is **vacuous-until-committed**: the gate `ci/ci_check_convergence_evidence_schema.sh` passes when no transcript is present (the real operator-produced transcript is pending the live pass), and asserts the shape once the `.jsonl` + `.md`-bound-sha256 manifest is committed. A boring same-tip-only run (no slot regression) is explicitly NOT sufficient. **SINGLE-BEST-PEER scope ‚Äî NOT full multi-peer Cardano ChainSel.** Status `enforced_scaffolding` (the sole such status in the registry): the gate is real + executable, the transcript it gates is not yet committed.

### `DC-EVIDENCE-04`: Closed fork-choice convergence evidence ‚Äî the live SELECT path emits a CLOSED, observe-only 10-event vocabulary (`needs_fork_choice ‚Üí lca_discovered ‚Üí candidate_fragment_built ‚Üí fork_choice_selected ‚Üí branch_fetch_started ‚Üí branch_fetch_completed ‚Üí branch_prevalidated ‚Üí fork_switch_applied | fork_switch_failed | fork_switch_superseded`); every win paired to EXACTLY ONE terminal by a bounded deterministic `fork_switch_id`; never consumed by selection/apply‚Ä¶

_tier: derived ¬∑ status: enforced_ ¬∑ _introduced_in: PHASE4-N-AO (S9)_

> **NEW in PHASE4-N-AO (S9) ‚Äî promotes the live SELECT proof from stderr diagnostics to registry-grade evidence.** Before S9 the fork-choice middle (NeedsForkChoice / LCA / win / fetch / prevalidate / apply) was visible only via temporary `FCDIAG` stderr markers (reverted) ‚Äî a committed transcript proved only the beginning (`block_received`) and end (`agreement`), leaving the actual SELECT unaudited (did Ade DISCOVER the LCA, SELECT a winner, FETCH+PREVALIDATE the branch, and APPLY the fork-switch, or merely follow one peer?). S9 adds a CLOSED observe-only convergence-evidence sequence: the 10 event discriminators EQUAL the emit-only allow-list (an unknown/added variant fails closed at the allow-list test, the `NodeSchedEvent` pattern); every field is bounded + typed (no free-form error strings ‚Äî `failure_code` is a closed enum mapping `BranchProofError`/`LcaError`; `fork_switch_id = blake2b(winning_peer ‚Äñ fork_anchor.slot ‚Äñ fork_anchor.hash ‚Äñ winner_tip.slot ‚Äñ winner_tip.hash)` hex-prefix, never free-form text). For a given `fork_switch_id`, a `fork_choice_selected{result=win}` is followed by EXACTLY ONE terminal (`applied` OR `failed` OR `superseded` ‚Äî the last when a newer win on the same fork overwrites this provisional pending before the relay loop applies it) ‚Äî never zero, never two, never dangling. **OBSERVE-ONLY:** no evidence event/type is EVER consumed by `select_best_chain` / `walk_to_durable_lca` / `apply_fork_switch` / the forge fence; a transcript write failure (flips `incomplete`, `DC-EVIDENCE-01`) cannot alter selection/apply/fence behavior. BLUE selector/walk/apply UNCHANGED.

|--------|----------|
| **Source** | `docs/planning/phase4-n-ao-ce-ao-6-live-gap.md` (S9 evidence finding) + `docs/clusters/PHASE4-N-AO/S9-closed-fork-choice-evidence.md` |

### `DC-EVIDENCE-05`: Replayable post-switch branch-continuity verdict ‚Äî a GREEN pure reducer `derive_post_switch_continuity` classifies Ade's OWN validated admitted-block lineage after a ForkChoiceWin at tip X into a closed `PostSwitchContinuity {ContinuesSelectedBranch | Diverged | BrokenLineage | DanglingForkChoiceWin | InsufficientEvidence}`; peer tip NEVER an input; replay-equivalent; the SINGLE impl behind both the hermetic replay test and the live CE-AO-6 gate‚Ä¶

_tier: derived ¬∑ status: enforced_ ¬∑ _introduced_in: PHASE4-N-AO (S10)_

> **NEW in PHASE4-N-AO (S10) ‚Äî the replayable verdict the `CN-CONS-03` release terminal is derived from.** Motivated by the 2026-06-13 scout run: a clean two-producer follow run (no switch) emitted ONLY `lagging` verdicts (peer perpetually 30‚Äì80 slots ahead), zero `agreed`, zero `diverged` ‚Äî a perfectly healthy follower the original exact-tip terminal (`DC-EVIDENCE-04`'s first form) would REJECT. Exact-tip agreement is a test-harness artifact: a live producer never pauses for the follower to touch its exact tip. S10 replaces it with a branch-continuity verdict over Ade's OWN admitted lineage. `ContinuesSelectedBranch` REQUIRES: unbroken `prev_hash` lineage from X across every post-X `block_admitted` (`admitted[i].prev_hash == admitted[i-1].hash`; the first post-switch follow block chains to `X.hash`), no `diverged` after X, and every `fork_choice_selected{win}` paired to a terminal. `prev_hash` is the admitted block's VALIDATED header field (`decoded.prev_hash` ‚Äî the same canonical parent link the S7 walk consumes via `get_block_by_hash`), NEVER peer-supplied; the peer's tip is NEVER an input. **REPLAY-EQUIVALENT:** same post-switch admitted-block bytes + same applied fork-switch point ‚Üí byte-identical `PostSwitchContinuity`. The reducer is the SINGLE implementation behind both the hermetic replay test AND the live CE-AO-6 gate (`ci_check_post_switch_convergence_window.sh` invokes the `post_switch_continuity` bin) ‚Äî no Rust/Python drift. **GREEN, observe-only:** `PostSwitchContinuity` is NEVER consumed by `select_best_chain`/`walk_to_durable_lca`/`apply_fork_switch`/`pump_block`/the forge fence; the node does not use it to select chains ‚Äî CI and `/cluster-close` use it to enforce the release gate.

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | `docs/clusters/PHASE4-N-AO/S10-post-switch-branch-continuity.md` (S10) + `docs/planning/phase4-n-ao-ce-ao-6-live-gap.md` |
| **Requirement** | A GREEN pure reducer `derive_post_switch_continuity(events) ‚Üí PostSwitchContinuity {ContinuesSelectedBranch | Diverged | BrokenLineage | DanglingForkChoiceWin | InsufficientEvidence}` (no free-form strings) classifies Ade's OWN validated admitted-block lineage after a ForkChoiceWin at X. `ContinuesSelectedBranch` requires unbroken `prev_hash` lineage from X (admitted[i].prev_hash == admitted[i-1].hash; first chains to X.hash), no `diverged` after X, every win paired to a terminal. `prev_hash` is the VALIDATED header field (`decoded.prev_hash`), never peer-supplied; peer tip never an input. Replay-equivalent (same bytes + same X ‚Üí byte-identical verdict). The reducer is the SINGLE impl behind the hermetic replay test AND the live CE-AO-6 gate. GREEN observe-only: never consumed by selection/walk/apply/pump/forge-fence. |
| **Code** | `crates/ade_node/src/post_switch_continuity.rs` (`derive_post_switch_continuity` + the closed `PostSwitchContinuity` verdict + `evaluate_release_window`, GREEN pure reducer), `crates/ade_node/src/bin/post_switch_continuity.rs` (the thin transcript‚Üíverdict bin the gate invokes), `prev_hash_hex` on `block_admitted` (`crates/ade_node/src/admission_log/{event,writer}.rs` + `convergence_evidence.rs` `emit_block_admitted`/`emit_admit_and_verdict`) sourced from `PumpTip.prev_hash` (`crates/ade_runtime/src/forward_sync/pump.rs`) + `ForkSwitchOutcome::Adopted.new_tip_prev` + the fork-switch-adopt + admission-runner emit sites in `crates/ade_node/src/node_lifecycle.rs` + `crates/ade_node/src/admission/runner.rs`.
