### `DC-LEDGER-08`: Conway cert-state accumulation is a closed, total, era-versioned transition‚Ä¶

_tier: derived ¬∑ status: enforced_

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | Cardano ledger spec (Conway CDDL certificate tags 0..18; delegation/pool state transitions); IDD fail-fast + closed-surface doctrine |
| **Requirement** | Conway cert-state accumulation is a closed, total, era-versioned transition: for each block at track_utxo, certificates decode through the era-correct closed grammar (Conway via the completed single decode_conway_certs retaining all owner payloads, tags 0..18) selected by explicit era dispatch ‚Äî never the Shelley 6-variant decoder on Conway bytes, never reduced into the 7-variant Shelley Certificate, never with payload fields dropped. Every certificate resolves to an owner-tagged disposition: it mutates B4-owned CertState (delegation/pool), or it is owner-tagged to ConwayGovState and routed out-of-mutation-scope (observed, not swallowed, not applied), or it is a structured reject (NotValidInEra for removed tags 5/6, Malformed for bad CBOR, UnsupportedUntilStateOwner only for genuinely-ownerless cases ‚Äî unreachable on the real corpus). Composite certs (tags 10/12/13) carry both a B4-owned mutation and an owner-tagged governance effect; both are represented. No certificate is flattened to neutral because there is nowhere to put it (the owner exists), decode-dropped, or apply-swallowed; a decode or apply error propagates as a structured LedgerError and halts the block transition. Incomplete or best-effort accumulation is a forbidden fail-open. (Wiring the owner-tagged ConwayGovState effects into applied governance state is PHASE4-B5, not B4.) |
| **Code** | `crates/ade_types/src/conway/cert.rs` (owner-complete ConwayCert); `crates/ade_types/src/shelley/cert.rs` (PoolRegistrationCert.owners); `crates/ade_codec/src/conway/cert.rs` (decode_conway_certs payload retention + decode_drep); `crates/ade_codec/src/shelley/cert.rs` (shared read_pool_registration_cert) ‚Äî PHASE4-B4-S1 decoder-completeness clause; `crates/ade_ledger/src/delegation.rs` (apply_conway_cert + ConwayCertAction/ConwayCertOutcome owner-tagged apply model, total over 18 tags) ‚Äî PHASE4-B4-S2 apply-totality clause |
| **Tests** | `each_tag_retains_owner_payloads`, `drep_grammar_total`, `conway_cert_action_total`, `apply_outcome_agrees_with_action`, `removed_tag_rejects_as_era_invalid`, `drep_registration_is_owner_tagged_not_applied`, `era_dispatch_conway_accumulates_via_conway_path`, `era_dispatch_shelley_accumulates_via_shelley_path`, `conway_decode_error_is_fail_closed`, `conway_unknown_tag_is_fail_closed`, `conway_removed_tag_is_fail_closed`, `conway_apply_error_is_fail_closed`, `conway_governance_cert_routed_out_of_scope`, `positive_synthetic_cert_state_accumulates`, `cert_state_replay_byte_identical`, `adversarial_no_false_accept` |
| **CI** | `ci/ci_check_forbidden_patterns.sh` |

### `DC-LEDGER-09`: Conway governance-certificate accumulation is a closed, total, era-versioned‚Ä¶

_tier: derived ¬∑ status: enforced_

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | Cardano ledger spec (Conway CDDL gov cert tags 9..18; CONWAY CERTS/GOVCERT/COMMITTEE transitions; CIP-1694); IDD fail-fast + closed-surface doctrine |
| **Requirement** | Conway governance-certificate accumulation is a closed, total, era-versioned transition into ConwayGovState: every governance-affecting Conway cert that B4 owner-tagged to ConwayGovState (vote-delegation tags 9/10/12/13 -> vote_delegations; committee tags 14/15 -> committee_hot_keys; DRep tags 16/17/18 -> drep_expiry) resolves to exactly one explicit ConwayGovState mutation or a structured reject -- never observed-and-dropped, never flattened, never with payload fields lost. B5 mutates only governance-owned fields; it does not touch B4-owned CertState and does not double-apply the delegation/pool half of composite certs (10/12/13). DRep expiry is computed only from an explicit gov-env (current epoch + drepActivity); a missing required env input is a structured fail-fast, never a defaulted expiry. A cert that cannot be applied propagates a structured LedgerError and halts the block transition; incomplete or best-effort accumulation is a forbidden fail-open. ConwayGovState becomes a deterministic function of (boundary-loaded base then replayed block-stream cert effects) rather than a frozen snapshot -- a deliberate, oracle-confirmable fingerprint migration (T-DET-01). |
| **Code** | `crates/ade_ledger/src/gov_cert.rs` (apply_conway_gov_cert: native gov dispatch over ConwayCert, total over 18 tags) ‚Äî PHASE4-B5-S2; `crates/ade_ledger/src/state.rs` (GovCertEnv + LedgerState::gov_cert_env() fail-fast) + `crates/ade_ledger/src/pparams.rs` (ConwayOnlyDepositParams.drep_activity) + `crates/ade_ledger/src/error.rs` (ValidationEnvironmentError::MissingDRepActivityParam) ‚Äî PHASE4-B5-S1; `crates/ade_ledger/src/rules.rs` (accumulate_tx_certs / process_block_certificates thread Option<ConwayGovState>, apply the gov half, carry gov_state forward through apply_block ‚Äî replaces the B4 observe-and-drop) ‚Äî PHASE4-B5-S3; `crates/ade_ledger/src/fingerprint.rs` (gov-state + drep_activity fingerprint surface) |
| **Tests** | `gov_apply_total_over_18_tags`, `composite_gov_half_applied_once_certstate_untouched_by_b5`, `drep_expiry_uses_epoch_plus_activity`, `env_free_gov_certs_need_no_env`, `drep_register_missing_env_is_fail_fast`, `drep_expiry_overflow_is_fail_closed`, `gov_apply_is_deterministic`, `gov_cert_env_present_ok`, `gov_cert_env_missing_drep_activity_is_fail_fast`, `gov_accumulation_applies_drep_registration_into_gov_state`, `gov_apply_error_halts_accumulation`, `positive_synthetic_gov_state_accumulates`, `gov_state_accumulation_replays_byte_identical`, `adversarial_drep_register_update_missing_env_rejected`, `adversarial_drep_expiry_overflow_rejected`, `adversarial_decode_layer_rejects_guard_gov_path`, `adversarial_double_resign_is_deterministic` |

### `DC-LEDGER-10`: Credential identity is faithful end-to-end: a stake/committee/DRep credential‚Ä¶

_tier: derived ¬∑ status: enforced_

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | Cardano ledger spec (Credential = key\|script across UTXOW/DELEG/GOVCERT; CIP-1694); IDD illegal-states-unrepresentable + determinism doctrine |
| **Requirement** | Credential identity is faithful end-to-end: a stake/committee/DRep credential is a closed sum over {KeyHash, ScriptHash} of a 28-byte hash, never a tag-erased Hash28. Both era certificate decoders preserve the key/script discriminant (an unknown tag is a deterministic reject); the credential type makes a discriminant-less credential unrepresentable on the BLUE authority path (no Hash28->credential coercion); CertState (registrations/delegations/rewards) and ConwayGovState (vote_delegations/committee_hot_keys/drep_expiry) key on the discriminated credential, so a key-hash and a script-hash credential sharing 28 bytes are distinct authoritative-state keys (matching cardano-node's Credential-keyed UMap/VState); and the canonical fingerprint serializes the discriminant so two states differing only in a credential's key/script tag fingerprint differently. The discriminated representation is a deliberate cert-state + gov-state fingerprint migration (T-DET-01). Default scope is Shelley+; Byron is included only if proven to have an affected credential surface. |
| **Code** | `crates/ade_types/src/shelley/cert.rs` (StakeCredential enum {KeyHash,ScriptHash} + hash()) ‚Äî OQ5-S1; `crates/ade_codec/src/shelley/cert.rs` + `crates/ade_codec/src/conway/cert.rs` (decode_stake_credential preserves the tag, rejects unknown) ‚Äî OQ5-S1; `crates/ade_ledger/src/state.rs` (ConwayGovState re-keyed to StakeCredential), gov_cert.rs, governance.rs, cert_classify.rs, rules.rs (cred.hash() boundary adapter for the Hash28-keyed stake snapshot) ‚Äî OQ5-S1; `crates/ade_ledger/src/fingerprint.rs` (write_stake_credential emits discriminant+hash; gov-map writers use it; stake-snapshot writer stays write_hash28) ‚Äî OQ5-S1; `crates/ade_testkit/src/harness/snapshot_loader.rs` (GREEN: gov-map + DRep-reg parses preserve the tag) ‚Äî OQ5-S1; `crates/ade_ledger/src/governance.rs` (committee ratification by full-credential equality, no .hash() on the committee path) + `crates/ade_ledger/src/state.rs` (ConwayGovState.committee StakeCredential-keyed) + `crates/ade_types/src/conway/governance.rs` (GovActionState.committee_votes StakeCredential) + `crates/ade_ledger/src/fingerprint.rs` (write_committee_vote_list) + `crates/ade_testkit/src/harness/snapshot_loader.rs` (parse_committee_state + parse_committee_vote_map tag-preserving) ‚Äî COMMITTEE-CRED-FIDELITY-S1; `crates/ade_types/src/conway/governance.rs` (GovActionState.drep_votes StakeCredential) + `crates/ade_ledger/src/governance.rs` (lookup_stake exact-variant DRep resolution, no OR-fallback) + `crates/ade_ledger/src/fingerprint.rs` (write_credential_vote_list, renamed from write_committee_vote_list, serves committee+drep) + `crates/ade_testkit/src/harness/snapshot_loader.rs` (parse_credential_vote_map, renamed, serves committee+drep) ‚Äî DREP-VOTE-FIDELITY-S1; `crates/ade_ledger/src/governance.rs` (EnactmentEffects.committee_changes StakeCredential-typed ‚Äî dormant, prevents committee-enactment re-collapse) ‚Äî ENACTMENT-COMMITTEE-FIDELITY-S1; `crates/ade_types/src/conway/governance.rs` (GovAction::UpdateCommittee structured {removed: BTreeSet<StakeCredential>, added: BTreeMap<StakeCredential,u64>, threshold}, replacing opaque raw bytes) + `crates/ade_ledger/src/fingerprint.rs` (write_gov_action emits the structured 5-field shape via write_stake_credential) + `crates/ade_testkit/src/harness/snapshot_loader.rs` (parse_cold_credential/_set/_epoch_map + parse_unit_interval, fail-closed on unknown tag) ‚Äî ENACTMENT-COMMITTEE-WRITEBACK-S1; `crates/ade_ledger/src/governance.rs` (apply_committee_enactment pure transition: dissolve + discriminated remove/add + quorum) + `crates/ade_ledger/src/rules.rs` (epoch-boundary apply site calls it) ‚Äî ENACTMENT-COMMITTEE-WRITEBACK-S2 |
| **Tests** | `shelley_credential_preserves_discriminant`, `conway_credential_preserves_discriminant`, `unknown_credential_tag_rejects`, `discriminant_changes_fingerprint`, `keyhash_scripthash_same_bytes_are_distinct_certstate`, `keyhash_scripthash_same_bytes_are_distinct_govstate`, `discriminant_changes_fingerprint_corpus`, `credential_accumulation_replays_byte_identical`, `committee_keyhash_scripthash_do_not_cross_resolve`, `committee_keyhash_scripthash_same_bytes_distinct`, `committee_discriminant_changes_fingerprint`, `drep_keyhash_scripthash_do_not_cross_resolve`, `drep_vote_discriminant_changes_fingerprint`, `enactment_committee_changes_keyhash_scripthash_distinct`, `update_committee_decodes_removed_added_threshold`, `update_committee_keyhash_scripthash_members_distinct`, `update_committee_decode_rejects_malformed`, `update_committee_structured_fields_change_fingerprint`, `enact_update_committee_keyhash_scripthash_distinct`, `committee_oracle_mainnet_575_576_noop_agreement` |

### `DC-LEDGER-11`: proposal_procedures MUST NOT remain an opaque byte field in the authoritative‚Ä¶

_tier: derived ¬∑ status: enforced_

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | CIP-1694 (proposal_procedure = [coin, reward_account, gov_action, anchor]); Project constitution ¬ß3 (closed semantic surfaces, T-CORE-01); DC-LEDGER-10 (downstream credential discriminant must not be re-collapsed) |
| **Requirement** | proposal_procedures MUST NOT remain an opaque byte field in the authoritative Conway tx-body shape. ConwayTxBody.proposal_procedures is Option<Vec<ProposalProcedure>>, decoded through a single closed entry point (decode_proposal_procedures) that rejects unknown gov_action tags, structural failures, empty sets, and trailing garbage deterministically; the typed form re-encodes byte-identically (PreservedCbor) for every well-formed Conway tx body. The decoder reuses the existing closed GovAction enum (preserving DC-LEDGER-10 UpdateCommittee discriminant) and the existing opaque Anchor struct. |
| **Code** | `crates/ade_codec/src/conway/governance.rs` (decode_proposal_procedures, decode_proposal_procedure, decode_gov_action, encode_proposal_procedures); `crates/ade_types/src/conway/governance.rs` (ProposalProcedure); `crates/ade_codec/src/conway/tx.rs` (typed key 20 path); `crates/ade_testkit/src/governance/proposal_procedures_replay.rs` (PP-S2 canonical synthetic corpus + replay harness) |
| **Tests** | `roundtrip_info_action_proposal`, `roundtrip_hard_fork_initiation`, `roundtrip_no_confidence`, `roundtrip_treasury_withdrawals`, `roundtrip_parameter_change`, `roundtrip_new_constitution`, `roundtrip_update_committee`, `roundtrip_multi_procedure`, `rejects_unknown_gov_action_tag`, `rejects_empty_proposal_procedures_set`, `rejects_trailing_garbage`, `rejects_truncated_proposal_procedure`, `rejects_invalid_stake_credential_in_update_committee`, `update_committee_keeps_stake_credential_discriminant`, `body_with_proposal_procedures_round_trips_through_typed_field`, `body_none_skips_proposal_procedures_key_20`, `body_and_sub_decoder_agree_on_proposal_procedures`, `canonical_corpus_decodes_to_expected_shape`, `canonical_corpus_round_trips_byte_identical`, `canonical_corpus_covers_all_gov_action_variants`, `canonical_corpus_includes_update_committee_discriminant_case` |

### `DC-LIVEMEM-01`: Live-feed bounded memory before authoritative decode/apply (operational-hardening; NOT BLUE consensus law)

_tier: derived ¬∑ status: enforced_ ¬∑ _introduced_in: PHASE4-N-F-G-E_ ¬∑ _strengthened_in: PHASE4-N-AA_

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | docs/planning/phase4-n-f-g-e-invariants.md |
| **Requirement** | Peer-driven memory on the live `--mode node` feed is bounded BEFORE authoritative decode/apply. A per-mini-protocol reassembly tail over 16 MiB fails closed with a structured `SessionError` (drop the peer); the WirePump opportunistic drain stops at 256 buffered blocks, letting the existing bounded `mpsc` (cap 64) back-pressure the pump. No silent truncation, no partial decode, no unbounded fallback. The bounds are CLOSED CONSTANTS (defensive implementation bounds, NOT Cardano semantic parameters) ‚Äî they may be tightened by a future hardening slice, but no runtime option (CLI / env / config) may disable them or set them unbounded. The cap fires before the BLUE decode path (unchanged); the verdict-decoupled `NodeBlockSource` contract, the relay-loop containment, and the served-chain handoff fence are all unchanged. |
| **Code** | `crates/ade_network/src/session/core.rs` (GREEN `MAX_REASSEMBLY_TAIL_BYTES` = 16 MiB cap + additive `SessionError::ReassemblyBufferOverflow`); `crates/ade_node/src/node_sync.rs` (RED `MAX_WIRE_PUMP_LOOKAHEAD` = 256 lookahead-depth cap); `crates/ade_runtime/src/network/mux_pump.rs` (overflow variant ‚Üí `PeerHaltReason::ChainSyncDecodeError` ‚Äî drop the peer) |
| **Tests** | `session_reassembly_tail_over_cap_fails_closed` (`crates/ade_network/src/session/core.rs:464`) ‚Äî incomplete tail over the 16 MiB cap fails closed with `ReassemblyBufferOverflow`; `session_reassembly_tail_under_cap_still_drains_complete_item` (`crates/ade_network/src/session/core.rs:502`) ‚Äî a complete item under the cap still drains intact; `wirepump_lookahead_stops_at_cap` (`crates/ade_node/src/node_sync.rs:2133`) ‚Äî the opportunistic drain stops at `MAX_WIRE_PUMP_LOOKAHEAD`; `wirepump_lookahead_cap_preserves_relay_behavior_under_normal_feed` (`crates/ade_node/src/node_sync.rs:2162`) ‚Äî the cap does not alter relay behaviour under a normal feed |
| **CI** | `ci/ci_check_live_feed_memory_bounds.sh` ‚Äî both bounds are CLOSED LITERAL constants AND not wired to CLI / env / config (the no-escape-hatch guard); exit 0 this pass |

_cross-refs: `CN-SESS-04`, `DC-SESS-06`, `DC-SYNC-01`, `DC-SYNC-02`, `DC-NODE-06`, `CN-NODE-02`. **PHASE4-N-AA strengthening (`strengthened_in += "PHASE4-N-AA"`):** `DC-SERVEMEM-01` is the symmetric **serve-side** analog of this **receive-side** bound ‚Äî the serve range cap (`MAX_SERVE_RANGE_BLOCKS` = 256) mirrors the receive-side `MAX_WIRE_PUMP_LOOKAHEAD` = 256, completing peer-driven memory/work bounding on both the inbound feed and the outbound serve. This rule's own four-cell contract (Code / Tests / CI above) is unchanged ‚Äî the strengthening is the cross-side completion, not a re-scope._

### `DC-NODE-04`: Authority-fatal halt + shutdown-resume identity: authoritative errors‚Ä¶

_tier: derived ¬∑ status: enforced_

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | docs/planning/phase4-n-k-orchestrator-binary-invariants.md ¬ß1 (I-6, I-7) |
| **Requirement** | Authority-fatal halt + shutdown-resume identity: authoritative errors (chain_write failure on a committed rollback, SnapshotDecodeError::UnknownVersion or FingerprintMismatch during bootstrap) halt the binary deterministically with a non-zero exit code ‚Äî no silent retry, no fallback decode. Clean shutdown drains the admit/write/snapshot pipeline to a quiescent point (bounded ‚Äî no waiting indefinitely for peer sessions) and writes a final snapshot via the persistent writer; restarting against the same (chaindb, snapshot store) produces a byte-identical initial (LedgerState, PraosChainDepState, ChainDb tip). Schema-version migration (snapshot v1 -> v2 upgrade tooling) is the snapshot-format lifecycle concern of DC-STORE-09, NOT a shutdown-semantics concern of this rule. This rule does NOT carry that open_obligation. |
| **Code** | `crates/ade_node/src/node.rs`, `crates/ade_node/src/main.rs` |
| **Tests** | `crates/ade_node/tests/shutdown_resume_identity.rs::shutdown_then_resume_produces_byte_identical_state`, `crates/ade_node/tests/shutdown_resume_identity.rs::shutdown_clean_exits_with_evidence`, `crates/ade_node/tests/shutdown_resume_identity.rs::cold_start_without_genesis_fails_with_generic_startup_code`, `crates/ade_node/tests/authority_fatal_decode.rs::binary_halts_on_authority_fatal_decode_error` |

### `DC-NODE-05`: Forge-slot discipline on the --mode node relay run-loop. A forge is attempted‚Ä¶

_tier: derived ¬∑ status: enforced_ ¬∑ _introduced_in: PHASE4-N-F-E ¬∑ strengthened_in: PHASE4-N-F-F, PHASE4-N-F-G-A, PHASE4-N-AE, PHASE4-N-AH, PHASE4-N-AI_

> **Strengthened in PHASE4-N-AE (2026-06-07).** The forge-slot discipline (at-most-once-per-slot, never a past slot, subordinate to the sync spine) is now further gated by the AE forge-on-followed-tip admissibility classifier (`DC-NODE-15`): in the recover‚Üífollow ForgeTick arm the forge fires ONLY when `durable_servable_tip == followed_peer_tip` and the `recovered.tip` forge-base fallback is removed ‚Äî so the forge tick stays subordinate to the spine AND builds only on a peer-adoptable parent. The four-cell contract below is unchanged (the AE strengthening's enforcement lives in `ci_check_forge_followed_tip_admission.sh` via `DC-NODE-15` / `DC-CONS-24`).

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | docs/planning/phase4-n-f-e-invariants.md |
| **Requirement** | Forge-slot discipline on the --mode node relay run-loop. A forge is attempted at most once per SlotNo and never for a slot <= the last forged slot (no past or duplicate forge). The current slot is derived ONLY through the clock seam: RED observes wall-clock (SystemClock), GREEN converts via millis_to_slot over the SystemStart anchor + EraSchedule slot length -- only SlotNo crosses the seam (no SystemTime/Instant/float past the RED observation boundary). The forge tick advances NO durable tip and admits/serves/gossips nothing -- it is subordinate to the sync spine, whose run_node_sync -> pump_block path remains the sole durable tip-advance authority; a forged block is a local self-accept artifact only. For a fixed recovered state, ordered block feed, injected clock tick schedule, and shutdown schedule, the forge-attempt sequence and forged block bytes are byte-identical across runs (replay-equivalent). Leadership eligibility is NOT decided in the loop or the GREEN planner (whose forge input is a content-blind Due\|NotDue) -- it stays in BLUE inside forge_one_from_recovered. Single-epoch this cluster: an unsupported slot fails closed / skips with a structured local outcome (cluster-scope containment, not permanent behavior). |
| **Code** | `crates/ade_node/src/node_lifecycle.rs`, `crates/ade_node/src/run_loop_planner.rs` |
| **Tests** | `plan_loop_step_forge_precedence_table_is_total`, `forge_slot_guard_none_is_due`, `forge_slot_guard_at_most_once_per_slot`, `forge_slot_guard_rejects_past_slot`, `relay_loop_forge_slot_derived_via_clock_seam`, `relay_loop_forge_tick_attempts_forge_advances_no_tip`, `relay_loop_without_producer_material_matches_nfd_relay`, `relay_loop_forge_two_runs_byte_identical`, `forge_tick_rotated_kes_period_skips_no_retroactive_sign`, `forge_tick_off_epoch_slot_fails_closed_local` |
| **CI** | `ci/ci_check_loop_planner_closed.sh`, `ci/ci_check_node_run_loop_containment.sh`, `ci/ci_check_genesis_consistency_fixture_present.sh` |

> **Strengthened in PHASE4-N-F-G-A.** S1 / S4 ‚Äî the forge-slot discipline is now genesis-consistency-proven (S1 pinning harness against the committed reference fixture) and epoch-hardened: the off-epoch fail-closed guard (`forge_epoch_admission`) sits inside the fenced `forge_one_from_recovered`, before leadership / KES signing. Containment is byte-unchanged.

### `DC-NODE-06`: Self-accept -> serve handoff on the --mode node relay spine (sibling serve‚Ä¶

_tier: derived ¬∑ status: enforced_ ¬∑ _introduced_in: PHASE4-N-F-G-B ¬∑ strengthened_in: PHASE4-N-F-G-C, PHASE4-N-U_

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | docs/planning/phase4-n-f-g-invariants.md; docs/clusters/completed/PHASE4-N-U/cluster.md (S3 supersession) |
| **Requirement** | Self-accept -> serve handoff on the --mode node relay spine (sibling serve task, shape B). Only a BLUE self-accepted forged artifact may enter the sibling served-chain serve task: the handoff carries a typed, constructor-fenced artifact whose ONLY provenance is a ForgeSucceeded outcome (CN-FORGE-01 emits ForgeSucceeded only when BLUE self_accept accepts the forged block against its pre-forge base). The serve task MUST NOT accept raw forged bytes, a failed forge output (ForgeNotLeader / ForgeFailed), a self-declared acceptance flag, or a peer-verdict substitute. Served-chain mutation happens ONLY in the sibling serve authority via the single ServedChainHandle::push_atomic authority; the block-fetch response preserves the self-accepted forged block bytes as the payload and applies the single CN-WIRE-08 tag-24 envelope authority (no parallel serializer). The relay-loop body performs NO serve / admit / gossip / block-fetch / durable-tip mutation -- the handoff from the relay loop to the sibling serve task is a typed channel send of a constructor-fenced self-accepted artifact, not served-chain mutation and not block-fetch serving, so the relay-loop containment gate (ci_check_node_run_loop_containment.sh) stays SEMANTICALLY UNCHANGED (this cluster may ADD a served-chain handoff gate but MUST NOT relax containment). Peer acceptance is proven ONLY by the peer's validation log through ba02_evidence::correlate, never by Ade's self-accept / ForgeSucceeded / any wire-success signal (RO-LIVE-06). |
| **Code** | `crates/ade_node/src/node_lifecycle.rs` (`run_node_serve_task` -> `ServedChainSource::DurableChainDb` over `Arc<dyn ChainDb>` ‚Äî N-U S3 evolved spine; the G-B push sibling + `serve_gate_admits` + handoff channel retired), `crates/ade_node/src/node_sync.rs`, `crates/ade_runtime/src/network/served_chain_projection.rs` (`ChainDbServedSource` ‚Äî the durable-provenance serve source), `crates/ade_runtime/src/network/serve_dispatch.rs` (`ServedChainSource`). _HISTORICAL (G-B/G-C, superseded by N-U S3 ‚Äî now `--mode produce` only, CN-PROD-04):_ `crates/ade_runtime/src/producer/served_chain_handle.rs`, `crates/ade_ledger/src/producer/served_chain.rs` |

| **CI** | `ci/ci_check_served_chain_handoff_fence.sh` _(N-U S3 / `60deecf3`: REPOINTED to fence the evolved durable-provenance serve ‚Äî node-spine serve sources ONLY `ServedChainSource::DurableChainDb`; no retired non-durable ingress ‚Äî `push_atomic` / `served_chain_admit` / `ServedChainHandle` / `SelfAcceptedHandoff` channel; exit 0)_, `ci/ci_check_node_run_loop_containment.sh` _(co-bound; containment semantically unchanged; exit 0)_, `ci/ci_check_served_chain_projection.sh` _(N-U S3 NEW: the node-spine serve is a read-only projection of the durable ChainDb)_ |

### `DC-NODE-07`: Node-spine live serve-to-peer (--mode node serves the G-B self-accepted ServedChainView‚Ä¶

_tier: derived ¬∑ status: enforced_ ¬∑ _introduced_in: PHASE4-N-F-G-H_

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | docs/planning/phase4-n-f-g-h-invariants.md |
| **Requirement** | `--mode node` can serve the G-B self-accepted `ServedChainView` to real peers through the single shared ChainSync + BlockFetch serve path, using the configured network magic, **outside** `run_relay_loop` ‚Äî with **no second serve authority or serializer**. The only blocks served are the BLUE self-accepted `AcceptedBlock`s reachable through the G-B `ServedChainView` (fed solely by the sibling self-accept‚Üíserve push task, `DC-NODE-06`). A sibling listener + serve-dispatch task (spawned outside the relay loop, mirroring the G-B push task) reuses the existing N2N serve machinery and the BLUE `producer_chain_sync_serve` + `producer_block_fetch_serve` (+ `producer_chain_sync_advance_tip`) ‚Äî serving **both** the ChainSync header advertisement (a follower discovers the served tip, `DC-CONS-18`) **and** the BlockFetch body (the follower fetches the served block by hash, `DC-CONS-17`), under the closed server-agency reply surface (`CN-PROTO-06`) and the deterministic/total session reducers (`DC-PROTO-07`, `DC-PROTO-08`). No parallel tag-24 serializer (the single `CN-WIRE-08` envelope authority); no serve / `push_atomic` / served-chain mutation inside `run_relay_loop` (containment `CN-NODE-02` stays semantically unchanged); reuses the existing `--listen` flag (no new `--mode node` flag; S1 path-fidelity fence stays green); **not** switched to `--mode produce`. Wiring the serve is **not** a peer-acceptance claim: acceptance is proven only by the peer's validation log through `ba02_evidence::correlate` (`RO-LIVE-06`), and `RO-LIVE-01` / `RO-LIVE-06` do **not** flip at this cluster's implementation close. |
| **Code** | `crates/ade_runtime/src/network/serve_dispatch.rs` (S1: the single shared serve-dispatch core ‚Äî `dispatch_server_frame_event_to_outbound` + `install_server_peer_state` / `remove_server_peer_state` + `ServerPeerStates` + `DispatchError`, extracted verbatim from `produce_mode`; OQ1 resolved ‚Äî extracted, not duplicated ‚Üí no second serve authority); `crates/ade_node/src/node_lifecycle.rs` (S2: `run_node_serve_task` ‚Äî the request-driven serve sibling `tokio::spawn`ed **outside** `run_relay_loop` on the `On` arm when `--listen` is supplied + `bind_serve_listener` + the closed `ServeStartError`; retains the `ServedChainView` instead of discarding it ‚Äî the only new wiring); `crates/ade_network/src/handshake/version_table.rs` (S2b: `n2n_supported_for_magic` ‚Äî the configured-magic serve version table; the lone additive BLUE *function*, no struct/enum); `crates/ade_network/src/chain_sync/server.rs` (`producer_chain_sync_serve` + `producer_chain_sync_advance_tip` ‚Äî reused BLUE, unchanged); `crates/ade_network/src/block_fetch/server.rs` (`producer_block_fetch_serve` ‚Äî reused BLUE, unchanged); `crates/ade_runtime/src/producer/served_chain_handle.rs` (`ServedChainHandle` / `ServedChainView` ‚Äî reused GREEN) |
| **Tests** | `node_spine_serve_loopback_follower_fetches_self_accepted_block` ‚Äî hermetic loopback: a follower over a real socket ChainSync-discovers the served header then BlockFetch-fetches the self-accepted block body from the `--mode node` spine (`crates/ade_node/tests/node_spine_serve_loopback.rs`); `node_serve_start_failure_is_surfaced_not_silent` ‚Äî a listener bind fault surfaces as the closed `ServeStartError`, never a silent no-op (`crates/ade_node/tests/node_spine_serve_loopback.rs`); `n2n_supported_for_magic_produces_configured_magic` ‚Äî the serve version table advertises the configured network magic (`crates/ade_network/src/handshake/version_table.rs`); `node_c1_serve_live` ‚Äî env-gated (`ADE_LIVE_C1_SERVE=1`) operator harness; skipped in CI; `NoEvidence` panics and writes nothing (`crates/ade_node/tests/node_c1_serve_live.rs`) |

### `DC-NODE-08`: `--mode node` MAY forge the genesis-successor (FIRST) block from the recovered base when both tips are None‚Ä¶

_tier: derived ¬∑ status: enforced_ ¬∑ _introduced_in: PHASE4-N-F-G-J_

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | `docs/planning/phase4-n-f-g-j-genesis-successor-prevhash-invariants.md`; cluster docs `docs/clusters/PHASE4-N-F-G-J/` (`cluster.md`, `S3-position-validation-genesis-forge.md`, `S4-node-spine-cold-start-reachability.md`) |
| **Requirement** | `--mode node` MAY forge the genesis-successor (FIRST) block from the recovered authoritative base when `ChainDb::tip()` AND the recovered tip (`recovered.tip`) are BOTH `None`, but ONLY when ALL hold: (a) the explicitly WarmStart-recovered/imported seed-epoch lineage is present (the recovered `SeedEpochConsensusInputs` + anchor lineage), never an unanchored / from-genesis-file-constructed or stale base; (b) `ForgeIntent::On` with complete operator key material; (c) the feed state is forge-eligible under the `CN-NODE-04` closed split (`no_block_available` \| `clean_empty`), never an ineligible / ambiguous (`unknown_disconnected`) or error state; (d) the slot/epoch/KES/leader guards pass (`DC-EPOCH-03` single-epoch containment + the BLUE leader check + KES-period/opcert); and (e) the forged first block carries `PrevHash::Genesis` (CBOR null per `CN-WIRE-09`) and flows through `self_accept` ‚Üí `SelfAcceptedHandoff` (`DC-NODE-06`) ‚Üí `ServedChainView` (`DC-NODE-07`). The recovered lineage gates PERMISSION to forge from the genesis-successor position; it is NOT the source of the prev_hash bytes, which are structurally null. The first-block reachability fires EXACTLY ONCE; once a durable tip exists, `block_number > 0` takes the normal `selected_tip` path with `PrevHash::Block`. The durable tip advances ONLY through the accepted path, never from forge scheduling alone; the forge base is the recovered surface only (`CN-CINPUT-03` / `DC-CINPUT-02b`); no `RO-LIVE-01`/`06` flip. The eligibility signal is general (forge-configured + valid recovered base), never a private-only / C1-only flag. |
| **Code** | `crates/ade_node/src/node_sync.rs` (`forge_header_position` ‚Äî GREEN single cold-start convention: `None` ‚áí block 0 + `PrevHash::Genesis`, `Some` ‚áí `last_block_no+1` + `Block`, malformed-height edge fails closed as `NodeForgeError::RecoveredTipMissingBlockNo`; `forge_one_from_recovered(selected_tip: Option<&ChainTip>)` routes the cold-start ctx into the SAME `run_real_forge` S3 proved); `crates/ade_node/src/node_lifecycle.rs` (`may_cold_start_forge` ‚Äî GREEN cold-start permission: no tip + recovered lineage + forge-eligible feed; the `LoopStep::ForgeTick` arm passes `selected_tip.as_ref()` and gates the both-`None` genesis forge); `crates/ade_node/src/forge_intent.rs` (`ForgeIntent::On` precondition) |

### `DC-NODE-09`: `--mode node` serve-listener lifetime is decoupled from feed end ‚Äî it terminates only on shutdown / fatal serve error‚Ä¶

_tier: derived ¬∑ status: enforced_ ¬∑ _introduced_in: PHASE4-N-F-G-K_

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | `docs/clusters/PHASE4-N-F-G-K/cluster.md` |
| **Requirement** | Once `--mode node` has spawned a `--listen` serve task (`run_node_serve_task`) over a `ServedChainView`, the end of the upstream feed (the relay loop returning ‚Äî e.g. a clean feed-end `HaltCleanly` with the operator shutdown watch still false) alone MUST NOT terminate that serve task. The serve listener's lifetime is owned by the node lifecycle owner: it terminates ONLY on (a) explicit node shutdown (the operator shutdown watch), (b) a fatal serve error (a post-bind accept fault), or (c) lifecycle-owner cancellation. The serve task stays read-only over `ServedChainView` (fed only by forge ‚Üí self_accept ‚Üí `SelfAcceptedHandoff` ‚Üí `push_atomic`, `DC-NODE-06`/`DC-NODE-07`); it holds no ChainDb / WAL / forge handle, so extending its lifetime grants AVAILABILITY, not authority. The process-termination guarantee is PRESERVED (moved from feed-end stop to the lifecycle owner, never removed): operator shutdown ends BOTH the relay loop and the serve task. No serve of bytes outside `ServedChainView`; no durable tip advance; no peer-block admission; no `RO-LIVE` flip; no unbounded never-terminating serve. |
| **Code** | `crates/ade_node/src/node_lifecycle.rs` (`run_node_lifecycle_inner` On-arm: the `--listen` serve task is spawned with `shutdown.clone()` ‚Äî the operator shutdown watch ‚Äî NOT a dedicated feed-end stop channel; the post-`run_relay_loop` `node_serve_stop.send(true)` flip is REMOVED; `node_serve_handle` is awaited and ends only on shutdown / fatal serve error. `run_node_serve_task` ‚Äî the serve loop ‚Äî is UNCHANGED: it breaks on its shutdown watch, a fatal accept error, and events-channel close, and takes only `(TcpListener, ServedChainView, network_magic, watch::Receiver<bool>)`) |
| **Tests** | `crates/ade_node/tests/node_spine_serve_loopback.rs`: `serve_task_outlives_feed_end_and_serves_late_fetch`, `serve_task_terminates_on_shutdown_no_hang`, `node_spine_serve_loopback_follower_fetches_self_accepted_block`, `node_serve_start_failure_is_surfaced_not_silent`. (4 named; all resolve on disk.) |
| **CI** | `ci/ci_check_node_serve_lifetime.sh` (NEW ‚Äî pins that the serve listener's lifetime is independent of the feed source's end; serve outlives feed-end, terminates on shutdown / fatal serve error) |

### `DC-NODE-10`: Forge-successor position (block_no, prev_hash) is read from the evolved admitted spine state, not the stale WarmStart baseline‚Ä¶

_tier: derived ¬∑ status: enforced_ ¬∑ _introduced_in: PHASE4-N-F-G-Q_

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | `docs/clusters/PHASE4-N-F-G-Q/cluster.md` |
| **Requirement** | After the feed validation/admission advances the node spine (a block ingested ‚Üí `state.receive` evolved), the next forge MUST derive the successor header position ‚Äî `block_no` (and the `chain_dep`/`ledger` it self-accepts against) ‚Äî from the EVOLVED admitted node-spine state (`state.receive`: the evolved `chain_dep` + ledger), NOT the stale WarmStart baseline (`recovered.chain_dep` / `recovered.ledger`). The successor `block_no` = the evolved `chain_dep.last_block_no + 1`; the `prev_hash` = the durable selected tip's hash. `RecoveredTipMissingBlockNo` is reserved for a genuinely malformed recovered state and MUST NOT fire for a feed-advanced tip. No guessed `block_no`, no `unwrap_or(1)`, no synthetic numbering. The genesis-successor cold-start (BOTH tips `None` ‚Üí block 0 + `PrevHash::Genesis`) is UNCHANGED (`DC-NODE-08`). The seed-epoch PoolDistr + eta0 (`DC-CINPUT-02b` / `DC-CINPUT-03`) are per-epoch and unchanged ‚Äî valid for the in-epoch successor; cross-epoch is off-epoch fail-closed (`DC-EPOCH-03`). NARROW: selects the evolved admitted chain state for the forge; no other forge-semantics change, no durable-recovery / WAL change (the ChainBreak-on-restart is a SEPARATE N-U durability concern). |
| **Code** | `crates/ade_node/src/node_lifecycle.rs` (the relay-loop forge call threads the evolved `state.receive.chain_dep` + `state.receive.ledger` into `forge_one_from_recovered` ‚Äî NOT the recovered baseline); `crates/ade_node/src/node_sync.rs` (`forge_one_from_recovered(recovered, live_chain_dep, live_ledger, selected_tip, ‚Ä¶)` ‚Äî `forge_header_position` + the self-accept ctx read `live_chain_dep`/`live_ledger`; `recovered` supplies only the seed-epoch PoolDistr + the off-epoch guard) |
| **Tests** | `crates/ade_node/src/node_sync.rs`: `forge_successor_reads_evolved_spine_block_no_not_stale_baseline_g_q`, `forge_one_from_recovered_cold_start_is_block_zero_genesis`. (2 named; all resolve on disk.) |
| **CI** | `ci/ci_check_forge_successor_evolved_spine.sh` (NEW ‚Äî pins that the successor forge position is sourced from the evolved admitted spine, not the stale recovered tip) |

### `DC-NODE-11`: Stable served block 0 ‚Äî monotone serve-gate mechanism SUPERSEDED by serve-as-projection (PHASE4-N-U); invariant preserved + strengthened (now survives restart)‚Ä¶

_tier: derived ¬∑ status: enforced_ ¬∑ _introduced_in: PHASE4-N-F-G-R ¬∑ strengthened_in: PHASE4-N-U_

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | `docs/clusters/PHASE4-N-F-G-R/cluster.md`; `docs/clusters/PHASE4-N-U/S3-serve-as-durable-chain-projection.md` (mechanism supersession) |
| **Requirement** | Once `--mode node` has self-accepted and served a genesis-successor block at `block_no` 0, a follower MUST see a STABLE block 0 (no block-0-replaces-block-0 churn) ‚Äî never B-without-A history. **PHASE4-N-U supersedes the G-R monotone serve-gate MECHANISM** (`serve_gate_admits` over the in-memory `ServedChainView` accumulator) with **serve-as-projection** (`DC-NODE-13`): own-forged blocks are now durably admitted (`DC-NODE-12`) and the durable chain is **extend-only** (`DC-CONS-23`), so it holds exactly one block 0 by construction; the served view PROJECTS the durable ChainDb (`ChainDbServedSource`) and serves that stable, coherent chain WITHOUT a monotone gate. The stability invariant is PRESERVED and STRENGTHENED ‚Äî it now also survives restart (the durable ChainDb is recovered by `T-REC-05`; the in-memory accumulator was not). NARROW (unchanged): no synthetic numbering; the served block is still self-accepted (no serve of unvalidated bytes). |
| **Code** | `crates/ade_runtime/src/network/served_chain_projection.rs` (`ChainDbServedSource` ‚Äî PHASE4-N-U S3 serve-as-projection over the durable ChainDb provides the stable/coherent served chain; the durable chain is extend-only so it holds exactly one block 0); `crates/ade_node/src/node_lifecycle.rs` (`run_node_serve_task` serves the durable projection; `serve_gate_admits` + the `ServedChainView` accumulator RETIRED); `crates/ade_ledger/src/receive/{reducer,admitted}.rs` + `block_validity` (extend-only durable admit ‚Äî `DC-CONS-23` ‚Äî rejects a re-mint block 0). HISTORICAL (G-R, superseded): `node_lifecycle` `serve_gate_admits` monotone-`block_no` gate + `crates/ade_ledger/src/producer/served_chain.rs` `ServedChainSnapshot` |

| **CI** | `ci/ci_check_served_chain_projection.sh` (`ci_script` REPOINTED from the RETIRED `ci_check_served_chain_stability.sh` ‚Äî the projection gate fences serve-as-projection + the retirement: no `serve_gate_admits` / `.push_atomic(` / `ServedChainHandle::new(` in `node_lifecycle`) |

### `DC-NODE-12`: Own-forged durable admit chokepoint ‚Äî a forged block becomes durable ONLY via the same pump_block admit chokepoint received blocks use‚Ä¶

_tier: derived ¬∑ status: enforced_ ¬∑ _introduced_in: PHASE4-N-U ¬∑ strengthened_in: PHASE4-N-AH, PHASE4-N-AI_

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | `docs/planning/phase4-n-u-forged-block-durability-invariants.md` |
| **Requirement** | A self-accepted forged block may become part of the durable chain ONLY by being submitted to the same durable admit chokepoint as received blocks (`run_node_sync ‚Üí pump_block` / `forward_sync AdmitPlan::durable`): `StoreBlockBytes ‚Üí AppendWal ‚Üí AdvanceTip`, durable-before-tip, behind the BLUE admit authority (`decode ‚Üí validate_and_apply_header ‚Üí block_validity`, extend-only). The forge has NO second tip-advance path and performs NO direct tip mutation ‚Äî it submits a self-accepted artifact as an admit INPUT. The bytes admitted durably (`StoreBlockBytes` + WAL) are byte-identical to the bytes `self_accept` validated ‚Äî no re-encode / reserialize / reconstruct between `self_accept` and durable admit; the served projection must expose those same bytes when serving the durable block (I-10). SUPERSEDES the `DC-NODE-05` containment consequence "a forged block is a local self-accept artifact only" while PRESERVING `DC-NODE-05`'s deeper invariant: the forge tick advances no durable tip DIRECTLY, and `pump_block` remains the sole durable tip-advance authority. |
| **Code** | `crates/ade_node/src/node_sync.rs` (`admit_forged_block_durably` ‚Äî the fenced RED driver ‚Üí `pump_block`; feeds `accepted().as_bytes()` with no re-encode); `crates/ade_node/src/node_lifecycle.rs` (the ForgeTick arm admits the self-accepted handoff via the driver before the G-R serve handoff); `crates/ade_runtime/src/forward_sync/{reducer,pump}.rs` (`pump_block` / `AdmitPlan::durable` ‚Äî reused; advances `state.receive` + the durable ChainDb together so the next forge builds N+1) |
| **Tests** | `crates/ade_node/tests/forge_succeeds.rs`: `forge_tick_durable_admit_advances_tip`, `forge_successor_builds_block_1_from_durable_tip`, `forged_admit_bytes_byte_identical_to_self_accept`. (3 named; all resolve on disk.) |
| **CI** | `ci/ci_check_forged_durable_admit_via_pump.sh` (NEW ‚Äî fences the driver: routes through `pump_block`, no re-encode, no fork-choice, no manual tip advance), `ci/ci_check_node_run_loop_containment.sh` (EXTENDED in place ‚Äî allow-lists the 2nd fenced tip-advancer `admit_forged_block_durably` + still forbids direct `pump_block`/`put_block`/`AdvanceTip`/rollback in the loop body) |

### `DC-NODE-13`: Served view is a durable-chain projection ‚Äî the ChainView served to followers is a deterministic projection of the durable adopted chain‚Ä¶

_tier: derived ¬∑ status: enforced_ ¬∑ _introduced_in: PHASE4-N-U_ ¬∑ _strengthened_in: PHASE4-N-AA_

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | `docs/planning/phase4-n-u-forged-block-durability-invariants.md`; `docs/clusters/PHASE4-N-U/S3-serve-as-durable-chain-projection.md` |
| **Requirement** | The ChainView served to followers (ChainSync header advertisement + BlockFetch body) is a deterministic PROJECTION of the durable adopted chain ‚Äî including any feed-ingested predecessor ‚Äî not an independent accumulator. Once own-forged blocks are durably admitted (`DC-NODE-12`), the served view follows the durable chain so a follower can fetch coherent history (the durable chain says A ‚Üí B; the served view serves A and B, never B without A). SUPERSEDES the PHASE4-N-F-G-R monotone serve-gate workaround (which gated an accumulator) with serve-as-projection. |
| **Code** | `crates/ade_runtime/src/network/served_chain_projection.rs` (`ChainDbServedSource` ‚Äî RED read-only projection adapter implementing `ServedHeaderLookup` + `ServedRangeLookup` over `&dyn ChainDb`: `next_after`/`intersect`/`tip`/`range_bytes` read the durable ChainDb via `iter_from_slot`/`get_block_by_hash`/`tip`, `decode_block` for `block_no`/era, `block_header_bytes` for the header, `stored.bytes` served verbatim); `crates/ade_runtime/src/network/serve_dispatch.rs` (`ServedChainSource` enum `{Snapshot|DurableChainDb}`; the single dispatch authority reads either source ‚Äî `DC-NODE-07` preserved); `crates/ade_node/src/node_lifecycle.rs` (`run_node_serve_task` dispatches with `ServedChainSource::DurableChainDb` over the durable ChainDb; the G-R push sibling + `serve_gate_admits` retired); `crates/ade_ledger/src/block_validity/header_input.rs` (`block_header_bytes` ‚Äî the DC-CONS-18 header authority exposed for raw durable bytes; `accepted_block_header_bytes` delegates) |
| **Tests** | `crates/ade_node/tests/node_spine_serve_loopback.rs`: `served_view_projects_durable_chain` (follower block-fetches the durable block via the projection, byte-identical, DC-CONS-17), `follower_fetches_coherent_history_incl_ingested_predecessor` (durable A‚ÜíB ‚áí `next_after` walk None‚ÜíA‚ÜíB‚ÜíNone + `RequestRange[A,B]` = StartBatch,Block(A),Block(B),BatchDone, never B without A), `served_view_retires_accumulator` (empty durable chain serves nothing ‚Äî `RequestNext` parks `AwaitReply`, no phantom accumulator). Unit tests in `served_chain_projection.rs` pin the empty-store + range-boundary contract. (3 named; all resolve on disk.) |
| **CI** | `ci/ci_check_served_chain_projection.sh` (NEW ‚Äî fences the projection: reuses `block_header_bytes`, no parallel splitter, no re-encode; and the retirement: no `serve_gate_admits` / `.push_atomic(` / `ServedChainHandle::new(` in `node_lifecycle`) |

_PHASE4-N-AA strengthening (`strengthened_in += "PHASE4-N-AA"`): the serve-as-projection is now also **bounded** ‚Äî `ChainDbServedSource` reads the durable chain via the S1 hash-free capped primitives (`range_bytes_capped` / `last_block_bytes`) under `MAX_SERVE_RANGE_BLOCKS` = 256 (`DC-SERVEMEM-01`), so a follower can never drive an unbounded range read or per-block hash scan through the projection. The projection's own enforcement (Code / Tests / CI above) is unchanged; this is an additive resource bound on the read path, not a relaxation._

### `DC-NODE-14`: Every claimed forge parent must be servable or peer-intersectable in the durable served lineage‚Ä¶

_tier: derived ¬∑ status: enforced_ ¬∑ _introduced_in: PHASE4-N-AE_

> **NEW in PHASE4-N-AE.** PARTIAL after AE.A (followed-tip lineage clause), ENFORCED after AE.B (recovered-anchor clause). Root cause confirmed LIVE (CE-A5): the relay rejected `HeaderEnvelopeError (UnexpectedBlockNo (BlockNo 19) (BlockNo 0))` and fell back to Origin because the forged successor's parent was a snapshot-only point with NO servable `StoredBlock`. Fix = **Option B (FindIntersect-ONLY, proof-gated):** `ChainDbServedSource::intersect` projects the `prev_hash` of the EARLIEST servable `StoredBlock` (the forge parent) as a FindIntersect point IFF a real servable successor exists; it NEVER serves bytes for it (`get_block_by_hash`/`serve_range` stay empty ‚Üí BlockFetch refuses structurally; no synthetic `StoredBlock`). A recover-only anchor with no successor ‚Üí no projection (fail-closed).

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | `docs/clusters/PHASE4-N-AE/cluster.md`; `docs/planning/phase4-n-ae-slice-a-invariants.md`; `docs/planning/c2-local-discovered-gaps.md` |
| **Requirement** | Every claimed forge parent must be servable or peer-intersectable in the durable served lineage. A `--mode node` forge may only build on a parent a Haskell peer can FindIntersect: the followed peer tip (a durably-stored `StoredBlock` written by `pump_block`, AE.A) or a recovered anchor made intersectable (AE.B). The served chain must expose that parent as an intersect point from which the peer rolls forward onto the forged successor; the recovered snapshot anchor is never served as a chain head a peer cannot intersect. |
| **Code** | `crates/ade_runtime/src/network/served_chain_projection.rs` (`ChainDbServedSource::intersect`/`next_after`/`tip` over the durable ChainDb ‚Äî read-only, reused; AE.B: `intersect` projects the `prev_hash` of the earliest servable `StoredBlock` as a FindIntersect-ONLY point iff a real servable successor exists, never serving bytes for it); `crates/ade_node/src/node_lifecycle.rs` (the forge-on-followed-tip gate gives the projection an intersectable parent); `crates/ade_ledger/src/block_validity/header_input.rs` (`DecodedBlock.prev_hash` exposed ‚Äî already parsed ‚Äî for the FindIntersect-only proof) |

### `DC-NODE-15`: Forge admissibility requires the durable servable tip to equal the followed peer tip‚Ä¶

_tier: derived ¬∑ status: enforced_ ¬∑ _introduced_in: PHASE4-N-AE ¬∑ strengthened_in: PHASE4-N-AH_

> **NEW in PHASE4-N-AE (AE.A, 2026-06-06).** The `--mode node` ForgeTick `recovered.tip` forge-base fallback is removed: the forge base is the durable servable tip (`ChainDb::tip()`; the recovered snapshot anchor is NEVER a forge base). A closed GREEN classifier returns `CaughtUp` iff BOTH tips are present AND hash AND block_no are equal, else `NotCaughtUp{reason}`. The followed-peer-tip signal is a forge-ADMISSIBILITY input ONLY ‚Äî it may PREVENT a forge but never reaches `select_best_chain`/`chain_selector`/`fork_choice` (gate (d) static-grep enforced).

| **Requirement** | A `--mode node` forge is admissible ONLY when `durable_servable_tip == followed_peer_tip` (hash AND block_no); otherwise it fails closed with a typed structured refusal `ForgeRefused::NotCaughtUp { local_servable_tip, followed_peer_tip, reason }` ‚Äî no forge, no state transition, tip unchanged (distinct from a forge Failed). The recovered anchor (`recovered.tip`) is NEVER a forge base. The followed-peer-tip signal is a forge-ADMISSIBILITY input only: it may PREVENT a forge but may not select, replace, reorder, or prefer chains. |

### `DC-NODE-16`: Receive idempotency ‚Äî a re-announced block already durably present byte-identically is a no-op at the durable-admit chokepoint; a different block at/before the last-applied slot stays fail-closed‚Ä¶

_tier: derived ¬∑ status: enforced_ ¬∑ _introduced_in: PHASE4-N-AE_

> **NEW in PHASE4-N-AE.F (2026-06-07) ‚Äî the post-CE-A5 echo fix.** After the CE-A5 relay `AddedToCurrentChain` Ade's forged block 17 (slot 421), it RE-ANNOUNCED that block over Ade's follow link. The unchanged BLUE header authority correctly rejected `SlotBeforeLastApplied{last=421,attempted=421}` ‚Äî a CORRECT fail-closed, but it terminated the run (exit 43) AFTER the adoption. Fix: `pump_block`, immediately after `decode_block`, queries `db.get_block_by_hash(&decoded.block_hash)`; on a hit whose `stored.slot == decoded.header_input.slot` it returns `Ok(None)` BEFORE the RollForward/BlockDelivered reducer steps ‚Äî no validation, no WAL append, no tip change. The skip is gated on HASH equality vs the durable store (NEVER slot alone): a DIFFERENT block (different hash) at/before the last-applied slot returns `None` here and falls through to the unchanged BLUE authority, staying fail-closed. RED chokepoint only; NO BLUE change (`get_block_by_hash` is a DETERMINISTIC durable-store query, so the gate introduces no new reducer input and the BLUE authority is untouched). No skip-past, no fork-choice ‚Äî `DC-CONS-03` untouched; the no-op appends nothing to the WAL, so `T-REC-05` / `DC-WAL-02` warm-start replay-equivalence is preserved.

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | `docs/clusters/PHASE4-N-AE/slices/AE.F.md`; `docs/planning/phase4-n-ae-f-echo-idempotency-invariants.md`; `docs/evidence/phase4-n-ae-ce-a5-relay-adoption.md` |
| **Requirement** | Receive idempotency: a peer-delivered block already durably present byte-identically in the ChainDb (same slot, same hash) is an idempotent no-op at the durable-admit chokepoint (`pump_block`) ‚Äî no validation step, no WAL append, no tip change; the post-state is identical and replay-equivalent. A DIFFERENT block (different hash) at/before the last-applied slot is NOT short-circuited: it reaches the unchanged BLUE header authority and fails closed (`SlotBeforeLastApplied` / `BlockNoOutOfOrder`). The skip is gated on HASH equality vs the durable store, never slot alone; no skip-past, no fork-choice (`DC-CONS-03` untouched). |
| **Code** | `crates/ade_runtime/src/forward_sync/pump.rs` (`pump_block` ‚Äî the hash-exact `get_block_by_hash(&decoded.block_hash)` already-have gate at `pump.rs:102`, placed BEFORE the BLUE chokepoint reducer `forward_sync_step`; on `Some(stored)` AND `stored.slot == decoded.header_input.slot` it returns `Ok(None)` with no reducer step and no WAL append) |
| **Tests** | `crates/ade_runtime/src/forward_sync/pump.rs::tests::pump_block_reannounced_block_is_idempotent_noop` (CE-F1 ‚Äî re-pump ‚Üí `Ok(None)`; chain-dep last_slot / WAL length / ChainDb tip unchanged), `crates/ade_runtime/src/forward_sync/pump.rs::tests::pump_block_different_block_at_or_before_tip_still_fails_closed` (CE-F2 ‚Äî a different lower-slot block ‚Üí `SlotBeforeLastApplied`, NOT short-circuited), `crates/ade_node/src/node_sync.rs::tests::run_node_sync_survives_reannounced_block_in_feed` (CE-F4 ‚Äî `run_node_sync` over `[block, same-block]` completes, admits exactly once, no exit-43). (3 named; all resolve on disk.) |
| **CI** | `ci/ci_check_receive_idempotency.sh` (PHASE4-N-AE.F ‚Äî NEW; fences (1) the gate queries the durable store by HASH `get_block_by_hash(&decoded.block_hash)`, (2) the `return Ok(None)` no-op is gated by that hash hit, (3) the gate PRECEDES the BLUE reducer `forward_sync_step` so a hit runs no reducer step / no WAL append, (4) slot-consistency `stored.slot == decoded.header_input.slot`) |

### `DC-NODE-17`: `followed_peer_tip` advances ONLY from a real observed peer ChainSync advertisement (incl. the self-adoption echo case); a RED forge-admissibility observation only ‚Äî never mutates tip/WAL/ledger, never reaches fork-choice‚Ä¶

_tier: derived ¬∑ status: declared_ ¬∑ _introduced_in: TBD_

> **NEW (DECLARED, observation-only) in PHASE4-N-AF (2026-06-07).** Rung-1 Finding B surfaced a sole-producer stall: Ade forged + got block N adopted by the relay, but `followed_peer_tip` never advanced to N, so the `DC-NODE-15` admissibility gate stayed `NotCaughtUp` and Ade forged exactly one block per recover. DC-NODE-17 was the candidate fix ‚Äî recognize catch-up to Ade's OWN adopted block via the peer's re-announcement and forge the successor. **OQ-1 (c2t4 live, 2026-06-07) DISPROVED it as the fix:** the relay does NOT re-announce Ade's own adopted block over the follow link (Ade forged + got block 12 adopted ‚Äî relay `AddedToCurrentChain` blockNo=12 ‚Äî but `followed_peer_tip` stayed at 11; no `TipUpdate(12)`; then the link EOF'd). The pump DOES emit `TipUpdate` on every `RollForward` (verified live for block 11); there is simply no `RollForward(12)`. DC-NODE-17 is therefore **RETAINED as a SAFETY/OBSERVATION invariant ONLY** ‚Äî IF the peer advertises a tip, the RED signal must reflect it (never local inference) ‚Äî and is **NOT** the sustained-forge stall fix. The actual fix is `DC-NODE-18` (single-producer successor forge extends the adopted durable spine WITHOUT a relay echo). This rule has no enforcing tests/code/CI today (`tests = []`, `ci_script = ""`, `code_locus` is a CANDIDATE pending OQ-1, which resolved NEGATIVE); its enforcement preconditions (no WAL append / no durable-tip mutation / no ledger mutation / no fork-choice influence / no `DC-NODE-15` bypass / committed live evidence the peer re-announces Ade's block) remain UNMET. Open secondary diagnostic OQ-KA (follow-link keep-alive ‚Üí possible delayed self-echo) is non-blocking and does NOT drive DC-NODE-18.

| **Requirement** | `followed_peer_tip` advances ONLY from a real observed peer ChainSync advertisement of the peer's selected tip (including the self-adoption echo case, where the advertised block is already durably held by Ade ‚Äî the relay re-announcing Ade's own just-adopted block). The advance is a RED scheduling observation of the peer's real selection: it updates forge ADMISSIBILITY only (`DC-NODE-15`) and must NEVER mutate the durable tip / WAL / ledger (`DC-NODE-16` idempotency preserved; replay-neutral) and NEVER reach chain selection / fork-choice (`DC-CONS-03` stays the follow authority). NOT a chain-selection rule; a RED observation rule for forge admissibility only. |

### `DC-NODE-18`: Single-producer extend-own-durable-spine ‚Äî after initial peer catch-up AND an explicit RED venue-adoption certificate, an explicitly single-producer Ade may forge the next successor on its OWN durable adopted spine without a relay echo‚Ä¶

_tier: derived ¬∑ status: enforced_ ¬∑ _introduced_in: PHASE4-N-AF ¬∑ strengthened_in: PHASE4-N-AH_

> **NEW in PHASE4-N-AF (S1, 2026-06-07) ‚Äî the Rung-1 Finding B fix, introduced after OQ-1 disproved `DC-NODE-17`-as-fix.** Since the relay does NOT re-announce Ade's own adopted block, sole-producer Ade cannot rely on a follow-link echo to re-arm the `DC-NODE-15` gate. Instead: after initial peer catch-up against a real peer tip (`DC-NODE-15`) AND an explicit RED venue-adoption certificate for Ade's first successor ‚Äî operator/harness-supplied, naming the adopted own tip, matched by **chain-point identity (hash + block_no), slot ignored, NEVER inferred from self-admit** ‚Äî single-producer Ade may forge the next successor on its OWN durable adopted spine WITHOUT a relay echo. A successor is adoptable by induction (it extends an already-adopted parent; the relay is a pure follower). The forge mode is an explicit 4-state enum `ForgeMode` (`InitialCatchupRequired ‚Üí CaughtUpToPeerTip ‚Üí FirstOwnBlockServed ‚Üí SingleProducerExtendOwnDurableSpine`; no booleans). **A gate-APPLICABILITY refinement, NOT a fork-choice weakening:** valid ONLY while the venue is explicitly declared single-producer (`VenueRole::SingleProducer`; default `Unknown` runs the VERBATIM prior `DC-NODE-15` path); the followed-peer-tip signal still may not select/replace/reorder/prefer chains; multi-producer behaviour stays with chain-selection authority (`DC-CONS-03`). Fails closed to a typed `ForgeRefused::SingleProducerFenceViolation { reason, durable_tip, followed_peer_tip, observed_peer_tip, venue_role }` on each fence condition. **BLUE UNCHANGED** ‚Äî `pump_block` durable admission stays authoritative + idempotent (`DC-NODE-16`); ledger/chain_dep/WAL unchanged; successor construction derives from the evolved admitted spine (`DC-NODE-10`/`DC-CONS-24`); chain selection (`DC-CONS-03`) stays the sole follow/fork authority. **SCOPE BOUNDARY (live-proven core ONLY):** asserts the successor-extension-after-adoption-certificate authority; does NOT assert sustained production past k, relay ImmutableDB settlement, follow-link liveness, or forge-loop continuation after a follow-link EOF ‚Äî those are deferred to `DC-NODE-19`.

| **Source** | `docs/planning/single-producer-extend-own-spine-invariants.md`; `docs/clusters/PHASE4-N-AF/cluster.md`; `docs/clusters/PHASE4-N-AF/S1-single-producer-extend-own-spine.md` |
| **Requirement** | Successor extension after an explicit adoption certificate (single-producer, single successor). A successor is adoptable by induction. > **Strengthened in PHASE4-N-AH (`strengthened_in += "PHASE4-N-AH"`).** The PHASE4-N-AF certificate-promotion mechanism this rule introduced is **superseded as forge authority** by `DC-NODE-20`: the run-4 live finding showed the cert-promotion-into-extend raced and lost to the follow-link EOF (the cert had leaked from evidence into forge-loop authority), so N-AH makes the post-self-admit forge base the LOCAL durable `ChainDb::tip` (no cert read; the `FirstOwnBlockServed` cert-wait intermediate is folded out of the `ForgeMode` enum, now 3-state) and **removes the cert entirely** from `ade_node` (`DC-NODE-21`). The CORE invariant this rule asserts ‚Äî an explicitly single-producer Ade extends its OWN durable adopted spine WITHOUT a relay echo ‚Äî is **preserved and strengthened** (it now ENTERS the extend state via a local self-admit, and survives warm-start via `DC-NODE-22`); the `Code`/`Tests`/`CI` rows above describe the AS-INTRODUCED PHASE4-N-AF surface and are superseded in part by the `DC-NODE-20`/`21`/`22` rows below (the cert parser is now deleted).

### `DC-NODE-19`: Single-producer forge-loop continuation after follow-link EOF ‚Äî in the certified extend state, a structural feed-EOF must NOT by itself terminate the forge loop‚Ä¶

_tier: derived ¬∑ status: declared_ ¬∑ _introduced_in: TBD ¬∑ strengthened_in: PHASE4-N-AH_

> **NEW (DECLARED) at /invariants (PHASE4-N-AG framing, 2026-06-08).** CE-AF-6b, deferred from `DC-NODE-18`. In an explicitly declared single-producer venue (`VenueRole::SingleProducer`) that has ALREADY entered the `DC-NODE-18`/`DC-NODE-20` extend state, a `LoopState::Ending` caused SOLELY by a structural feed EOF (the Ade‚Üírelay follow link closing/draining) MUST NOT by itself terminate the forge loop ‚Äî the loop continues forging successors on its OWN certified durable spine (each admitted via `pump_block`, `DC-NODE-12`). The continuation is FENCED to the certified single-producer run and FAILS CLOSED on any of 7 conditions (not single-producer / not in the extend mode / operator shutdown / forge-validity bounds fail / a competing chain observed / relay-producing evidence / cert absent-or-malformed). It RELOCATES the loop's termination authority off feed-liveness onto explicit operator shutdown / fatal error (the same move `DC-NODE-09` made for the serve-listener), while PRESERVING `DC-NODE-05` (the forge advances no durable tip directly; `run_node_sync ‚Üí pump_block` stays the SOLE durable tip-advance authority; available feed work still drains via `SyncOnce` before any `ForgeTick`). **HONEST STATUS (NOT a gap):** kept `declared`/partial ‚Äî the loop-continuation gate `ci_check_single_producer_loop_continuation.sh` landed (N-AG) and `strengthened_in += "PHASE4-N-AH"` records that the proven extend state now survives warm-start, but the registry holds the rule `declared` (`tests = []`, `ci_script = ""`) because the full slice contract (the GREEN `plan_loop_step` 5th-input 32-case totality gate + the certified-run continuation fence + replay-equivalence over post-EOF forged successors + a committed sustained-past-k live transcript) was re-homed to PHASE4-N-AH CE-AH-6 on the `DC-NODE-20` path. Not overclaimed. `DC-CONS-03` explicitly untouched.

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | `docs/planning/single-producer-loop-continuation-after-feed-eof-invariants.md` (CE-AF-6b; OQ-19-1/2/5/6) |
| **Requirement** | In a `VenueRole::SingleProducer` venue already in `ForgeMode::SingleProducerExtendOwnDurableSpine`, a `LoopState::Ending` caused SOLELY by structural feed EOF MUST NOT by itself terminate the forge loop; the loop continues forging successors on its OWN certified durable spine (each via `pump_block`). FAILS CLOSED (no continuation; verbatim `HaltCleanly` / typed refusal) on any of: not single-producer; not in the extend mode; operator shutdown requested; forge-validity bounds fail (off-epoch `DC-EPOCH-03` / beyond forecast horizon `DC-CONS-09` / KES-period invalid); a competing chain observed before EOF; relay-producing evidence; the venue certificate absent/malformed. A real shutdown or fatal source failure exits via `Err`/fail-fast and is NEVER continued. A loop-lifecycle refinement, NOT a fork-choice change ‚Äî `DC-CONS-03` stays the sole follow/fork authority. |
| **Code** | _(declared ‚Äî `code_locus` is a CANDIDATE pending the full slice: `crates/ade_node/src/run_loop_planner.rs` (`plan_loop_step` 5th closed `VenuePolicy` input ‚Äî the 32-case total table), `crates/ade_node/src/node_lifecycle.rs` (`run_relay_loop_with_sched` threads the venue policy + restructures the Idle-under-feed-end wait), `crates/ade_node/src/node_sync.rs` (the venue/mode/cert continuation fence reuses `single_producer_forge_decision` / `SingleProducerFenceReason`). ### `DC-NODE-20`: Local selected durable chain forge-base authority ‚Äî after self-admit, the next forge base is Ade's LOCAL durable `ChainDb::tip`, NOT `followed_peer_tip` and NOT the cert (rung-1 single-producer)‚Ä¶

_tier: derived ¬∑ status: enforced_ ¬∑ _introduced_in: PHASE4-N-AH ¬∑ strengthened_in: PHASE4-N-AI_

> **Strengthened in PHASE4-N-AI (rung-2 wiring).** The `DC-NODE-20` rung-1 SingleProducer fail-closed arm is now the explicit `VenueRole::SingleProducer` consequent of the shared venue-blind detector + venue-split resolver (`DC-NODE-23`/`24`): a peer-origin competing candidate in a SingleProducer venue still FAILS CLOSED (byte-unchanged behaviour), while a Participant venue routes the validated header into BLUE `select_best_chain`. The four-cell contract below is unchanged; the strengthening is the resolver split that preserves this arm verbatim. See `DC-NODE-23`/`24`/`28`.

> **NEW in PHASE4-N-AH (S1, 2026-06-08) ‚Äî the run-4 live-finding fix.** Ade forged block 11, a real Haskell relay ADOPTED it, but Ade returned `no_tip_available` every subsequent tick because the `proceed_to_forge` gate required `durable_servable_tip == followed_peer_tip` ‚Äî which fails the instant Ade self-admits a block the non-producing relay does not re-announce ‚Äî and the only escape (the `DC-NODE-18` cert-promotion into extend mode) raced and lost to the follow-link EOF. **The cert had leaked from evidence into forge-loop authority.** S1 makes the forge base Ade's LOCAL SELECTED DURABLE TIP (`ChainDb::tip`) under a 6-condition fence (single-producer; NO competing block observed on the canonical receive stream since catch-up ‚Äî an OBSERVED-FEED fence, NOT fork-choice; relay non-producing; admitted via `pump_block`; spine contiguous/servable; no fork-choice required ‚Äî mechanically DERIVED from the observed-feed fence). The `FirstOwnBlockServed` cert-wait intermediate is FOLDED OUT of the authority path: the transition is DIRECT `(CaughtUpToPeerTip + self-admit valid own block via pump_block + the fence) ‚áí SingleProducerExtendOwnDurableSpine{current_tip = ChainDb::tip}`, with NO cert read (`ForgeMode` is now 3-state). `DC-NODE-15` REMAINS the INITIAL catch-up gate (durable == followed before the first own-forge); `DC-NODE-20` supersedes ONLY the repeated post-self-admit re-check. In rung 1 "selected" is DEGENERATE (no competing candidate ‚áí local ChainDB head = selected tip); **rung 2 MUST replace this with real fork-choice (`DC-CONS-03`, untouched here).** Removing the RED cert/timing from the authority path makes the post-self-admit forge MORE deterministic / replay-equivalent (`T-REC-03`/`05` extended).

### `DC-NODE-21`: Adoption certificate is rung-1 evidence-only, never forge authority ‚Äî the cert parser is fully DELETED from `ade_node`‚Ä¶

_tier: derived ¬∑ status: enforced_ ¬∑ _introduced_in: PHASE4-N-AH_

> **NEW in PHASE4-N-AH (S2, 2026-06-08).** The file-based operator adoption certificate is a rung-1 RED EVIDENCE-ONLY shim. It MAY prove relay adoption for the transcript / bounty bundle, but MUST NEVER control forge-base selection (`DC-NODE-20` derives the forge base from the local durable ChainDB tip) or any durable authority, and MUST NEVER appear in multi-producer, preprod, or production forge paths. S2 FULLY DELETED the `VenueAdoptionCertificate` type + the `read_adoption_cert` / `parse_hex32` parsers + the `--adoption-cert-path` CLI flag from `ade_node` ‚Äî **the cert parser is GONE, not just demoted.** Separated from `DC-NODE-20` (OQ-20-3) because "cert is evidence-only, never authority" is independently enforceable and needs a hard rung-2 removal boundary ‚Äî folding it into `DC-NODE-20` would make it easier for the shim to creep back into later slices as authority. **Hard follow-up:** it must be replaced/removed before rung 2 / preprod; the cert can never become chain-selection or durable authority.

S4b's GREEN `warm_start_forge_mode(venue_role, recovered_tip, replayed_anchor_block_no)` re-enters `SingleProducerExtendOwnDurableSpine{current_tip = ChainDb::tip}` for a single-producer venue whose recovered tip is ABOVE the replay anchor (`recovered_tip.block_no > replayed_anchor_block_no` ‚áî recovery replayed ‚â• 1 own block ‚Äî a local continuation spine), WITHOUT a fresh followed-peer catch-up; every other case FAILS CLOSED to `InitialCatchupRequired`. This is the warm-start analog of `DC-NODE-20`. `DC-CONS-03` (rung-2 fork-choice) is untouched; `pump_block` remains the SOLE durable admit authority (`DC-NODE-05`/`12` ‚Äî this rule only sets the forge MODE / reads the recovered tip; it admits nothing).

### `DC-NODE-23`: Shared receive-side fork-choice detector (rung-2) ‚Äî a peer candidate is classified ONCE, venue-blind, by a pure total predicate over (durable_tip, candidate_header_summary)‚Ä¶

_tier: derived ¬∑ status: enforced_ ¬∑ _introduced_in: PHASE4-N-AI_

> **NEW in PHASE4-N-AI (S2, the venue-blind detector).** A peer-origin candidate that is NOT already part of Ade's admitted durable spine / own-served lineage ‚Äî including but not limited to a header that does not build on `ChainDb::tip` ‚Äî is classified ONCE by a pure total predicate `(durable_tip, candidate_header_summary) ‚Üí ReceiveDisposition {AlreadyHave | LinearExtend | RefuseSingleProducer | NeedsForkChoice}`. A duplicate / already-known peer echo is `AlreadyHave`, **never** a competing candidate merely because it is not a fresh extension. Observes no venue, no wall-clock, no network state ‚Äî the SINGLE classification point that both the SingleProducer fail-closed arm (`DC-NODE-20`) and the Participant fork-choice arm (`DC-NODE-24`) consume. It never selects, reorders, or prefers chains (that is `select_best_chain` / `DC-CONS-03`).

|--------|----------|
| **Source** | `docs/planning/phase4-n-ai-live-fork-choice-invariants.md` (I-5) |
| **Requirement** | A peer-origin candidate not already known as part of Ade's admitted durable spine / own-served lineage is classified ONCE, venue-blind, by a pure total predicate over `(durable_tip, candidate_header_summary)` ‚Üí `{AlreadyHave | LinearExtend | RefuseSingleProducer | NeedsForkChoice}`. A duplicate / already-known peer echo is `AlreadyHave`, never a competing candidate. The predicate observes no venue, no wall-clock, no network state; it never selects / reorders / prefers chains (that stays `DC-CONS-03`). It is the single classification point consumed by both `DC-NODE-20` (SingleProducer) and `DC-NODE-24` (Participant). |

### `DC-NODE-24`: Venue-split fork-choice resolver (rung-2) ‚Äî SingleProducer fails closed (DC-NODE-20, byte-unchanged); Participant routes the validated header into BLUE select_best_chain‚Ä¶

The four-cell contract below is byte-unchanged; the strengthening is the live exercise, not a re-scope.
>
> **NEW in PHASE4-N-AI (S2, the venue-split resolver).** The `DC-NODE-23` detector's non-spine consequent (`NeedsForkChoice`) is gated by venue and TOTAL over the closed venue set: `VenueRole::SingleProducer ‚áí` **fail closed** (the `DC-NODE-20` rung-1 behaviour, **byte-unchanged** ‚Äî never adopt a peer candidate); `VenueRole::Participant ‚áí NeedsForkChoice ‚áí` the existing `ade_runtime::consensus::chain_selector` orchestrator (`process_stream_input ‚Üí BLUE select_best_chain`, `DC-CONS-03`). Venue input is explicit and **fail-safe** ‚Äî an undeclared / unknown venue takes the conservative SingleProducer refuse arm. In Participant mode the peer's VALIDATED header summary (post `validate_and_apply_header`) becomes a candidate; a raw `followed_peer_tip` signal MUST NOT reach `select_best_chain`.

### `DC-NODE-25`: Live fork-choice durable application authority (rung-2) ‚Äî a ChainSelected/RolledBack outcome is applied ONLY via the already-enforced lockstep / materialize / pump_block authorities; a win is provisional until BODIES validate‚Ä¶

_tier: derived ¬∑ status: enforced_ ¬∑ _introduced_in: PHASE4-N-AI_ ¬∑ _strengthened_in: PHASE4-N-AO_

> **Strengthened in PHASE4-N-AO (`strengthened_in += PHASE4-N-AO`).** Under the SELECT cluster, the live durable-apply authority drives the fork-switch adoption (`DC-NODE-37`) ‚Äî the reused lockstep/materialize/`pump_block` path applies the `RolledBack`+`ChainSelected`, no second apply path. The four-cell contract below is byte-unchanged; the strengthening is the live exercise, not a re-scope.
>
> **NEW in PHASE4-N-AI (S3, the apply driver).** A `ChainSelected` / `RolledBack` outcome from the `chain_selector` orchestrator is applied to the durable stores ONLY via the existing enforced authorities: the lockstep receive reducer (`DC-CONS-20` ‚Äî ChainDb + LedgerState + PraosChainDepState advanced / rolled-back as ONE structural transition) + `materialize_rolled_back_state` (`CN-STORE-07`) for the rollback target + `pump_block` (`DC-NODE-05`/`12`) for roll-forward. **NO second apply path, NO second durable tip-advance path, NO second rollback-materialize path.** A fork-choice win is PROVISIONAL: the chain is durably adopted ONLY when its BODIES validate and apply through `pump_block` (no header-only tip advance). A `TiebreakerLossKeepCurrent` outcome makes no durable change.

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | `docs/planning/phase4-n-ai-live-fork-choice-invariants.md` (I-2, I-3, I-4, I-11) |
| **Requirement** | A `ChainSelected` / `RolledBack` orchestrator outcome is applied to the durable stores ONLY via the enforced authorities ‚Äî lockstep receive reducer (`DC-CONS-20`) + `materialize_rolled_back_state` (`CN-STORE-07`) + `pump_block` (`DC-NODE-05`/`12`). No second apply / tip-advance / materialize path. A fork-choice win is provisional: durable adoption happens ONLY when the BODIES validate through `pump_block` ‚Äî no header-only tip advance. A `TiebreakerLossKeepCurrent` makes no durable change. |
| **Code** | `crates/ade_node/src/node_lifecycle.rs` (the RED apply driver) over `crates/ade_ledger/src/receive/reducer.rs` (`DC-CONS-20` lockstep) + `crates/ade_ledger/src/rollback/*` (`materialize_rolled_back_state` / `commit_rollback`, `CN-STORE-07`) + `crates/ade_runtime/src/forward_sync/pump.rs` (`pump_block`, `DC-NODE-05`/`12`). | **Tests** | `crates/ade_node/tests/apply_driver_ai_s3.rs`: `apply_rolledback_rolls_back_and_appends_wal_record_after_commit` (a RolledBack outcome rolls back via the materialize authority + appends the WAL rollback record AFTER commit), `apply_chain_selected_invalid_body_fails_via_pump_no_advance` (an invalid body fails through `pump_block` with NO tip advance ‚Äî the win is provisional), `apply_chain_selected_without_block_bytes_fails_closed` (a header-only selection fails closed ‚Äî no header-only tip advance). ### `DC-NODE-26`: Decision/durable reconciliation (rung-2) ‚Äî after any applied receive decision the orchestrator selector.current_tip EQUALS the durable ChainDb::tip‚Ä¶

_tier: derived ¬∑ status: enforced_ ¬∑ _introduced_in: PHASE4-N-AI_ ¬∑ _strengthened_in: PHASE4-N-AO_

> **Strengthened in PHASE4-N-AO (`strengthened_in += PHASE4-N-AO`).** Under the SELECT cluster, decision/durable reconciliation spans the live fork-switch (the orchestrator `current_tip` reconciles to the post-switch durable `ChainDb::tip`). The four-cell contract below is byte-unchanged; the strengthening is the live exercise, not a re-scope.
>
> **NEW in PHASE4-N-AI (S3, the reconciliation backstop).** After any applied receive decision, the `chain_selector` orchestrator's `selector.current_tip` EQUALS the durable `ChainDb::tip` (and the orchestrator `chain_dep` equals the durable `PraosChainDepState`). The in-memory decision state never diverges from the persisted authority: the orchestrator decides, the durable lockstep path applies, and the two are reconciled EVERY decision. No applied decision leaves the selector ahead of, behind, or forked from the durable spine.

### `DC-NODE-27`: Rollback+reselection replay-equivalence (rung-2) ‚Äî a live rollback is durably recorded by a version-gated WalEntry::RollBack marker that re-invokes the existing rollback authority on replay; byte-identical recovery‚Ä¶

_tier: derived ¬∑ status: enforced_ ¬∑ _introduced_in: PHASE4-N-AI_ ¬∑ _strengthened_in: PHASE4-N-AO_

> **Strengthened in PHASE4-N-AO (`strengthened_in += PHASE4-N-AO`).** Under the SELECT cluster, the `WalEntry::RollBack{ForkChoiceWin}` marker is CONSTRUCTED live for the first time by the fork-switch (`DC-NODE-37`) ‚Äî same marker, re-invoked on replay, no second rollback implementation. The four-cell contract below is byte-unchanged; the strengthening is the live exercise, not a re-scope.
>
> **NEW in PHASE4-N-AI (S1, OQ-1 RESOLVED ‚Üí A).** The ordered live receive-event sequence (RollForward headers, RollBackward points, body deliveries) replayed against the same bootstrap anchor + durable log produces a BYTE-IDENTICAL durable tip + ledger fingerprint + PraosChainDepState ‚Äî **INCLUDING any rollback+reselection.** A live rollback is recorded durably (append-only, canonical bytes ‚Äî `CN-WAL-01`) such that replay re-invokes the SAME materialize / reducer authority (`CN-STORE-07` / `DC-CONS-20`) at that point; the durable record is **NOT a second rollback implementation.** No implicit live-only rollback: a rollback that happened live MUST be reproducible on recovery (`T-REC-03`/`05`, `DC-CONS-06`/`22`). **OQ-1 RESOLVED ‚Üí A** (a version-gated `WalEntry::RollBack` marker re-invoking the existing rollback / materialize authority on replay; option B WAL-tail reconciliation rejected). This is the SOLE new BLUE authority this cluster.

| **Requirement** | The ordered live receive-event sequence replayed against the same anchor + durable log yields a BYTE-IDENTICAL durable tip + ledger fp + PraosChainDepState, INCLUDING any rollback+reselection. ### `DC-NODE-28`: No forge across unresolved re-selection (rung-2) ‚Äî once a candidate is NeedsForkChoice in a Participant venue, forging is DISABLED until the outcome is durably applied+reconciled or rejected‚Ä¶

_tier: derived ¬∑ status: enforced_ ¬∑ _introduced_in: PHASE4-N-AI_ ¬∑ _strengthened_in: PHASE4-N-AO_

> **Strengthened in PHASE4-N-AO (`strengthened_in += PHASE4-N-AO`).** Under the SELECT cluster, the no-forge fence covers the live fork-switch / `MissingBridge` window (`DC-NODE-39`). The four-cell contract below is byte-unchanged; the strengthening is the live exercise, not a re-scope.
>
> **NEW in PHASE4-N-AI (S4b, the producer race fence).** Once a peer-origin candidate is classified `NeedsForkChoice` (`DC-NODE-23`) in a Participant venue, forging is DISABLED until the fork-choice outcome is either (a) durably applied and reconciled (`DC-NODE-25`/`26`) or (b) rejected with durable state unchanged. The forge base is **NEVER** selected from a stale pre-resolution `ChainDb::tip` while a decision is pending ‚Äî a producer tick that fires during a pending decision **fails closed** (typed `ForgeRefused`), never forges on the old local tip. A producer race fence DISTINCT from `pump_block` durable admit, rollback replay, or selector / durable reconciliation, so it carries its OWN evidence. Prevents stale local authority leaking into block production. Derived tier with a true-tier authority consequence.

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | `docs/planning/phase4-n-ai-live-fork-choice-invariants.md` (I-12) |
| **Requirement** | Once a candidate is `NeedsForkChoice` (`DC-NODE-23`) in a Participant venue, forging is DISABLED until the outcome is (a) durably applied + reconciled (`DC-NODE-25`/`26`) or (b) rejected with durable state unchanged. The forge base is NEVER selected from a stale pre-resolution `ChainDb::tip` while a decision is pending; a producer tick during a pending decision fails closed (typed `ForgeRefused`), never forging on the old local tip. |

Reuses `DC-NODE-05` forge-slot discipline + `DC-CONS-13` forge purity; no new BLUE. |
| **Tests** | `crates/ade_node/tests/live_fork_choice_ai_s4bii.rs`: `pending_reselection_forge_refusal_gate` (a producer tick during a pending decision fails closed, never forges on the stale tip), `participant_rollback_beyond_k_fails_closed_clears_pending` (a beyond-k Participant rollback fails closed and clears the pending state), `singleproducer_rollback_refused_by_run_node_sync` (the SingleProducer venue refuses a peer rollback at the loop level).
