### `DC-NODE-29`: Live rollback target canonical binding (rung-2; AI-S6 H-1 remediation) ‚Äî a peer RollBackward target is bound against the durable ChainDb pre-commit; peer slot MUST equal the stored slot for the hash, else fail closed before any mutation‚Ä¶

_tier: derived ¬∑ status: enforced_ ¬∑ _introduced_in: PHASE4-N-AI_ ¬∑ _strengthened_in: PHASE4-N-AO_

> **Strengthened in PHASE4-N-AO (`strengthened_in += PHASE4-N-AO`).** Under the SELECT cluster, the canonical pre-commit rollback-target slot+hash binding is the FORK-ANCHOR binding for the SELECT (`DC-NODE-37`/`38`) ‚Äî never peer-supplied. The four-cell contract below is byte-unchanged; the strengthening is the live exercise, not a re-scope.
>
> **NEW in PHASE4-N-AI (S6 ‚Äî the H-1 cluster-close security remediation).** For a peer `RollBackward(point)` on the live Participant path, the rollback target MUST be resolved against the durable `ChainDb` and use the STORED chain point (stored slot + hash) as the SOLE authority. The peer-supplied slot MUST equal the stored slot for that hash; on any mismatch (or unknown hash, or Origin) the path **fails closed with a typed error BEFORE `commit_rollback`, BEFORE `WalEntry::RollBack`, BEFORE any ChainDb / LedgerState / PraosChainDepState mutation.** No rollback target may be built from mixed peer/local authority (peer-supplied slot + locally-verified hash). Reconciliation (`DC-NODE-26`) remains the post-apply backstop but is NOT the only defense. **Closes H-1** (cluster-close security review): a Byzantine peer's `RollBackward` naming a real in-chain hash with an arbitrary lower slot would otherwise truncate the durable chain to a peer-chosen depth and brick the node ‚Äî reconciliation caught the mismatch only AFTER disk mutation; pre-commit canonical binding rejects it with zero durable mutation.

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | `docs/clusters/PHASE4-N-AI/S6-rollback-target-slot-hash-binding.md` (H-1 remediation) |
| **Requirement** | For a peer `RollBackward(point)` on the live Participant path, the rollback target is resolved against the durable `ChainDb` using the STORED chain point (slot + hash) as the SOLE authority; the peer-supplied slot MUST equal the stored slot for that hash. On mismatch / unknown-hash / Origin the path fails closed with a typed error BEFORE `commit_rollback`, BEFORE `WalEntry::RollBack`, BEFORE any ChainDb / LedgerState / PraosChainDepState mutation. No mixed peer/local-authority target. Reconciliation (`DC-NODE-26`) is the post-apply backstop, NOT the only defense. |
| **Code** | `crates/ade_node/src/node_lifecycle.rs` (`run_participant_sync` RollBack arm) over `crates/ade_runtime/src/chaindb` `get_block_by_hash`. RED shell binding; reuses the enforced rollback authorities (`CN-STORE-07` / `DC-CONS-20`); no new BLUE. |
| **Tests** | `crates/ade_node/tests/live_fork_choice_ai_s4bii.rs`: `rollback_slot_hash_mismatch_fails_before_mutation` (a peer slot ‚âÝ the stored slot for the hash fails closed BEFORE any durable mutation ‚Äî the H-1 attack), `participant_rollback_applies_durably` (a canonically-bound target applies durably), `participant_rollback_to_unknown_point_fails_closed` (an unknown hash / Origin fails closed). (3 named; all resolve on disk.) |
| **CI** | `ci/ci_check_rollback_target_canonical_binding.sh` (PHASE4-N-AI ‚Äî NEW, 62 lines on disk; fences the pre-commit canonical target binding ‚Äî stored-point-as-sole-authority, peer-slot-must-equal-stored-slot, fail-closed-before-mutation, no mixed peer/local authority). |

### `DC-NODE-30`: Participant-path convergence evidence emission ‚Äî the live `--mode node --participant-venue` rollback-follow path emits the closed AgreementVerdict vocabulary to a dedicated `--convergence-evidence-path` JSONL as a GREEN side-output; never authority‚Ä¶

_tier: derived ¬∑ status: enforced_ ¬∑ _introduced_in: PHASE4-N-AJ_

> **NEW in PHASE4-N-AJ (the CE-AI-6 bridge).** Closes the bridge gap: the rollback-follow (node) path previously emitted NO agreement evidence while `--mode admission` ignored rollbacks, so the convergence-through-reorg transcript (CE-AI-6) could not be produced. PHASE4-N-AJ makes `run_participant_sync` emit `BlockReceived` for EACH peer block considered (before drop/admit/refuse), `BlockAdmitted` per `pump_block` admit, and `AgreementVerdict = verdict::derive(outcome, observed_peer_tip)` ‚Äî each carrying `consensus_inputs_fingerprint_hex` ‚Äî to a dedicated `--convergence-evidence-path` sink. Emit-only GREEN side-output of already-authoritative outcomes: **never** gates admission, **never** triggers/parameterizes a rollback, **never** influences fork-choice, **never** mutates the durable chain. `pump_block` stays the sole roll-forward admit; `apply_chain_event` the sole rollback authority; `classify_receive` unchanged. A write failure is non-fatal to authority (the sink is distinct from the authoritative WAL) but **poisons** the transcript (`EvidenceEmitResult::FailedAndPoisoned`) so it is marked incomplete/unusable for CE-AI-6 ‚Äî never a silent partial that later passes the gate. No path supplied ‚áí no file and node behaviour byte-unchanged. **NO new evidence enum; NO BLUE change** (evidence-only span ‚Äî first BLUE-empty cluster since the G-N window). `CN-CONS-03` was NOT flipped; CE-AI-6 is now PRODUCIBLE + mechanically checkable, but the flip is the follow-on operator pass only.

| **Source** | `docs/planning/phase4-n-aj-participant-convergence-evidence-invariants.md` ¬ß1 (I-AJ-1) + ¬ß7 (D-1/D-2/D-3) |
| **Requirement** | The live `--mode node --participant-venue` rollback-follow path emits the existing closed AgreementVerdict vocabulary to a dedicated `--convergence-evidence-path` JSONL as a deterministic GREEN side-output of already-authoritative outcomes: `BlockReceived` for EACH peer block considered (before drop/admit/refuse), `BlockAdmitted` per `pump_block` admit, `AgreementVerdict = verdict::derive(outcome, observed_peer_tip)`, each carrying `consensus_inputs_fingerprint_hex`. MUST NOT become authority ‚Äî never gates admission, triggers/parameterizes a rollback, influences fork-choice, or mutates the durable chain. Emit-only on Diverged. ### `DC-NODE-31`: Recovered-anchor live-follow start authority ‚Äî after recovery from a non-Origin bootstrap anchor, the recovered store PERSISTS the bootstrap anchor point and resolves the live-follow FindIntersect START from it (anchor, not Origin); replay-equivalent; fail-closed‚Ä¶

_tier: derived ¬∑ status: enforced_ ¬∑ _introduced_in: PHASE4-N-AK_

> **NEW in PHASE4-N-AK (AK-S1).** Remediates a live recover‚Üífollow regression: a bare-anchor recovery previously resolved the live-follow start to Origin (block 0), so the FindIntersect handshake never matched the peer's chain. PHASE4-N-AK persists the bootstrap anchor POINT (slot, hash) as replayable recovery provenance bound to the recovered anchor fingerprint, and resolves the live-follow start tip from it. **Resolution order = servable `ChainDb` tip ‚Üí persisted recovered anchor point (non-Origin + provenance-bound) ‚Üí Origin/None only if the recovered store is truly Origin/cold-start.** A non-Origin recovered store whose anchor-point record is missing / malformed / fingerprint-mismatched **FAILS CLOSED before live follow starts.** The persisted anchor point is the durable restart authority ‚Äî NOT CLI re-supply (CLI seed-point is first-run input only). Does not change `ChainDb::tip()` semantics and does not synthesize a servable block. AI-S4a `RollBackward(Origin)` fail-close unchanged. The wire-pump consumer (`spawn_live_wire_pump_source`) is UNCHANGED. **Extends `T-REC-05`** to the recovered tip surface: same recovered store + same WAL ‚áí same anchor point ‚áí same `BootstrapState.tip` ‚áí same FindIntersect start.

| **Requirement** | After recovery from a non-Origin bootstrap anchor, the recovered store persists the bootstrap anchor point (slot, hash) as replayable recovery provenance bound to the recovered anchor fingerprint; on warm-start, `BootstrapState` resolves the live-follow start tip from that persisted anchor point whenever `ChainDb` has no servable post-anchor block. ### `DC-NODE-32`: Recovered-anchor rollback boundary on the single-producer live-follow path ‚Äî `run_node_sync` accepts a peer `RollBackward` binding EXACTLY (slot AND hash) to the persisted recovered anchor as an idempotent no-op; every non-anchor/Origin rollback fails closed‚Ä¶

_tier: derived ¬∑ status: enforced_ ¬∑ _introduced_in: PHASE4-N-AK_

> **NEW in PHASE4-N-AK (AK-S2 ‚Äî completes the live follow).** After recovery to a bare bootstrap anchor and `DC-NODE-31`'s FindIntersect-at-anchor start, the peer's post-intersection `RollBackward(anchor)` must be accepted so the single-producer follow loop can catch up. PHASE4-N-AK makes `run_node_sync` accept a peer `RollBackward` whose target binds EXACTLY (slot AND hash) to the persisted recovered anchor point (`DC-NODE-31` / `BootstrapState.tip`) as an **idempotent NO-OP boundary rewind: no WAL, no ChainDb mutation, no ledger mutation, no cursor.** The anchor is a recovery snapshot boundary, NOT a stored servable block, and is NEVER synthesized into one (`ChainDb::tip()` / `last_block_bytes` / serve never return it). `RollBackward(Origin)` still fails closed (AI-S4a unchanged); every non-anchor, non-Origin rollback fails closed; the accepted point must bind to the PERSISTED anchor on slot AND hash, never peer-supplied alone. The anchor point consumed by `run_node_sync` is the single authority (`BootstrapState.tip`), threaded in ‚Äî NEVER re-read from the store inside the loop. The first forward block after the anchor admits through the EXISTING sole `pump_block` path (AK-S2 adds NO forward-link code). **Recover‚Üífollow on the single-producer path is replay-equivalent** (extends `T-REC-05`/`DC-NODE-31` to the follow). **SCOPE (deliberately narrow):** does NOT add general stored-block rollback-follow on the single-producer path, and does NOT touch the participant path (`run_participant_sync` ‚Äî a separate follow-on obligation).

The anchor is a recovery-snapshot boundary, never a stored servable block, never synthesized into one. `RollBackward(Origin)` fails closed (AI-S4a); every non-anchor non-Origin rollback fails closed; the accepted point must bind to the PERSISTED anchor on slot AND hash, never peer-supplied alone. ### `DC-NODE-33`: Participant-path recovered-anchor rollback boundary ‚Äî `run_participant_sync` accepts a peer `RollBackward` binding EXACTLY (slot AND hash) to the persisted recovered anchor as an idempotent no-op (the participant MIRROR of `DC-NODE-32`); every non-anchor/Origin rollback falls through to the unchanged DC-NODE-29 fail-closed resolution‚Ä¶

_tier: derived ¬∑ status: enforced_ ¬∑ _introduced_in: PHASE4-N-AL_

> **NEW in PHASE4-N-AL ‚Äî the participant MIRROR of `DC-NODE-32`.** N-AK fixed the bare-anchor recover‚Üífollow rollback no-op for the SINGLE-PRODUCER path (`run_node_sync`) and explicitly deferred the PARTICIPANT path (`run_participant_sync`) as "OQ #4 ‚Äî a separate follow-on." CE-AI-6 runs the participant path, so it was blocked: a bare-anchor participant recover halted at the relay's standard post-`IntersectFound` `RollBackward(anchor)` (`get_block_by_hash(anchor) ‚Üí None ‚Üí UnexpectedRollback`) before admitting any block. PHASE4-N-AL makes `run_participant_sync` accept a peer `RollBackward` whose target binds EXACTLY (slot AND hash) to the persisted recovered anchor (`state.recovered_anchor`, set in the forge-ON arm at `node_lifecycle.rs:563`) as an **idempotent NO-OP** ‚Äî evaluated BEFORE the unchanged DC-NODE-29 stored-block resolution; no `commit_rollback`, no `WalEntry::RollBack`, no ChainDb/ledger/chain_dep mutation, no cursor, no `pending_reselection`. `RollBackward(Origin)` still fails closed (AI-S4a); every non-anchor rollback falls through to the UNCHANGED DC-NODE-29 stored-block authority; the accepted point binds to the PERSISTED anchor on slot AND hash, never peer-supplied alone. The first forward block after the no-op admits through the EXISTING `pump_block`. **Recover‚Üífollow on the participant path is replay-equivalent.** **SCOPE:** the participant recovered-anchor rollback-to-intersection case ONLY; `DC-NODE-32` (single-producer) is NOT broadened ‚Äî `DC-NODE-33` is a distinct sibling. Does NOT prove CE-AI-6 reorg convergence / full ChainSel (a separate induced-reorg pass).

### `DC-NODE-34`: Peer-identity restoration (SELECT foundation) ‚Äî the live receive path carries the origin peer identity end-to-end (`AdmissionPeerEvent.peer ‚Üí NodeSyncItem ‚Üí participant loop`) so per-peer candidate tracking is possible; provenance-only, byte-identical single-peer follow‚Ä¶

_tier: derived ¬∑ status: enforced_ ¬∑ _introduced_in: PHASE4-N-AO (S1)_

> **NEW in PHASE4-N-AO (S1) ‚Äî the SELECT foundation.** PHASE4-N-AI single-best-peer FOLLOW flattened peer identity into one merged feed; multi-candidate SELECT needs to know WHICH peer a candidate came from. S1 carries the origin peer identity end-to-end: `AdmissionPeerEvent (peer: String) ‚Üí NodeSyncItem ‚Üí run_participant_sync` ‚Äî the `NodeBlockSource ‚Üí NodeSyncItem` conversion (which formerly DISCARDED the peer at `node_sync.rs` `from_wire_pump`/`next_item`) now threads the peer label. **Restoration is provenance-only:** a single-peer FOLLOW run admits + replays BYTE-IDENTICALLY to the pre-restoration baseline, and identity restoration MUST NOT alter selection, admission, rollback, or evidence-verdict semantics. The aggregator that CONSUMES the identity is `DC-NODE-35` (latent until S3). `NodeSyncItem` is a transient feed type (not persisted / hashed) ‚Äî no canonical-type or replay obligation. RED/GREEN feed shape; NO BLUE change.

### `DC-NODE-35`: BLUE-safe candidate construction ‚Äî a `CandidateFragment` fed to BLUE `select_best_chain` is derived ONLY from Ade's OWN `validate_and_apply_header` output, never a peer-trusted minted summary, never a raw `followed_peer_tip`; the load-bearing S2 entry gate‚Ä¶

_tier: derived ¬∑ status: enforced_ ¬∑ _introduced_in: PHASE4-N-AO (S2)_

> **NEW in PHASE4-N-AO (S2) ‚Äî THE load-bearing gate that keeps the cluster from becoming look-over-the-peers-shoulder.** A `CandidateFragment` fed to BLUE `select_best_chain` (`DC-CONS-03`) MUST be derived ONLY from Ade's OWN validated headers (`validate_and_apply_header` output ‚Äî the `chain_selector::process_header_arrival` validate-then-fragment pattern), NEVER a peer-trusted minted `ValidatedHeaderSummary` (the `ade_core_interop::follow` shape, which MUST NOT cross into BLUE or any authority path) and NEVER a raw `followed_peer_tip`. Byte authority: hash-critical protocol paths use preserved original wire bytes; internal candidate comparison/proof surfaces use project-canonical bytes. Peer identity (`DC-NODE-34`) is preserved on each candidate. Candidate-set ordering MUST be deterministic. Malformed / missing candidate data fails closed. **No live `select_best_chain` call may be introduced until candidate construction proves these five properties** (the cluster's load-bearing S2 entry gate). The aggregator's TCB color is RESOLVED by this proof ‚Äî the easier color MUST NOT be picked to dodge it.

### `DC-NODE-36`: Live single-selector dispatch ‚Äî the participant `NeedsForkChoice` arm (formerly fail-closed) routes the aggregated candidate SET to the SINGLE existing BLUE `select_best_chain` (`DC-CONS-03`); routed-to, NEVER duplicated; no second selector / parallel preference / density ordering / operator heuristic‚Ä¶

_tier: derived ¬∑ status: enforced_ ¬∑ _introduced_in: PHASE4-N-AO (S3)_

> **NEW in PHASE4-N-AO (S3) ‚Äî wires the `NeedsForkChoice` consequent PHASE4-N-AI left fail-closed.** `DC-NODE-24` intended a Participant ‚Üí `select_best_chain` dispatch; S3 delivers it. The live participant `NeedsForkChoice` arm (formerly `Err(UnexpectedRollback)` in `run_participant_sync`) routes the aggregated candidate SET to the SINGLE existing BLUE `select_best_chain` ‚Äî **routed-to, NEVER duplicated: no second selector, no parallel preference, no density ordering, no operator heuristic.** The selected tip is arrival-order-independent over the live multi-peer set (the live analog of the `CN-CONS-01` permutation proof). A `TiebreakerLossKeepCurrent` outcome makes NO durable change. Only validated candidate summaries (`DC-NODE-35`) reach `select_best_chain`; a raw `followed_peer_tip` never does. The production `select_best_chain` was byte-unchanged through N-AI (the `fork_choice.rs` touch there was a `cfg(test)` arrival-order proof) ‚Äî S3 calls it LIVE for the first time.

### `DC-NODE-37`: Fork-switch never-abandon (SELECT primary invariant; the H-1 class at fork-choice scale) ‚Äî never commit a rollback of the durable chain until the replacement branch's bodies are FETCHED, LINKED, and VALIDATED; a failed/lying/incomplete branch leaves ChainDb+LedgerState+PraosChainDepState UNCHANGED‚Ä¶

_tier: derived ¬∑ status: enforced_ ¬∑ _introduced_in: PHASE4-N-AO (S4)_

> **NEW in PHASE4-N-AO (S4) ‚Äî the security-critical slice; the H-1 truncation class (PHASE4-N-AI AI-S6 / `DC-NODE-29`) generalized from a peer `RollBackward` to an Ade-initiated reselection.** When `select_best_chain` picks a winner that forks BELOW Ade's current durable tip, Ade MUST NEVER commit a rollback of its durable chain until the replacement branch's bodies are FETCHED, LINKED, and VALIDATED as a complete candidate branch (block-fetched via `BlockFetch RequestRange` anchor‚Üítip from the winning peer; the fork anchor canonically bound to Ade's durable STORED slot+hash per `DC-NODE-29`, never peer-supplied / mixed authority). A failed / lying / Byzantine / incomplete replacement branch leaves ChainDb + LedgerState + PraosChainDepState UNCHANGED. Adoption then proceeds ONLY via the already-enforced authorities: `RolledBack(fork_anchor)` through `materialize_rolled_back_state` (`CN-STORE-07`) + the lockstep receive reducer (`DC-CONS-20`), then `ChainSelected(body) √ó N` through `pump_block` (`DC-NODE-05`/`12`) ‚Äî a fork-choice win is PROVISIONAL, durably adopted ONLY when its BODIES validate+apply (no header-only tip advance). The reselection is recorded as the durable append-only `WalEntry::RollBack{ForkChoiceWin}` and is replay-equivalent (`DC-NODE-27`, extended ‚Äî NOT a second rollback implementation). No forge across the pending reselection (`DC-NODE-28`). **Its own focused per-cluster security review (S4 is the expected HIGH surface).**

| **Source** | `docs/planning/phase4-select-multicandidate-fork-choice-invariants.md` (FC-5/FC-6/FC-7) + `docs/clusters/PHASE4-N-AO/cluster.md` |

A failed/lying/incomplete branch leaves ChainDb+LedgerState+PraosChainDepState UNCHANGED. ### `DC-NODE-38`: Live multi-block fork-anchor discovery ‚Äî `walk_to_durable_lca` walks a competing branch's preserved parent links back to a DURABLE STORED fork anchor within k (BLOCK DEPTH), over a self-binding per-peer branch cache; the LCA is the ChainDb stored slot+hash ONLY (`DC-NODE-29`); over-k / gap / no-LCA / self-binding-violation / lying-parent all fail closed‚Ä¶

_tier: derived ¬∑ status: enforced_ ¬∑ _introduced_in: PHASE4-N-AO (S7)_

> **NEW in PHASE4-N-AO (S7) ‚Äî the live-geometry gap CE-AO-6 surfaced.** Before S7 a live multi-block competing branch failed closed (`UnexpectedRollback`) because its immediate parent is an intermediate block on the competing branch Ade never stored ‚Äî SELECT only worked for 1-deep forks. A live competing branch is now eligible for SELECT only when Ade walks its preserved parent links back to a DURABLE STORED fork anchor within k (BLOCK DEPTH, not slot distance), then validates the COMPLETE intermediate header chain from that anchor (S2 `validate_and_apply_header`) BEFORE selection. **The per-peer branch cache is NOT authority** ‚Äî only an indexed memory of received, preserved headers; each entry self-binds (`key_hash == re-derived header block hash`, `entry.slot == header.slot`, `entry.prev_hash == header.prev_hash`) or the branch fails closed. The last-common-ancestor is the fork anchor, authoritative ONLY when ChainDb confirms slot AND hash (`DC-NODE-29`) ‚Äî never the competing block's immediate parent, never peer-supplied, never slot-only, never hash-only. The walk is k-bounded by BLOCK DEPTH (traversed-header count ‚â§ k AND `current_tip_block_no ‚àí lca_block_no ‚â§ k`; no slot subtraction); over-k / branch-gap / no-durable-LCA / cache-self-binding-violation / lying-parent-link all fail closed with no durable mutation. A 1-deep fork degenerates to the prior single-step behavior.

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | `docs/planning/phase4-n-ao-ce-ao-6-live-gap.md` + `docs/clusters/PHASE4-N-AO/S7-lca-anchor-walk.md` |
| **Requirement** | A live competing branch is eligible for SELECT only when Ade walks its preserved parent links back to a DURABLE STORED fork anchor within k (BLOCK DEPTH), then validates the COMPLETE intermediate header chain (S2) BEFORE selection. The per-peer branch cache is evidence only; each entry self-binds (key==re-derived hash, slot, prev_hash) or fails closed. The LCA is the ChainDb stored slot+hash ONLY (`DC-NODE-29`) ‚Äî never the immediate parent, peer-supplied, slot-only, or hash-only. k-bounded by block depth (traversed ‚â§ k AND tip_bno ‚àí lca_bno ‚â§ k). Over-k / gap / no-LCA / self-binding-violation / lying-parent all fail closed, no durable mutation. 1-deep degenerates to the prior single step. |
| **Code** | `crates/ade_node/src/lca_walk.rs` (`walk_to_durable_lca` ‚Äî the k-bounded-by-block-depth LCA walk over the self-binding per-peer branch cache; the durable-anchor check via `chaindb.get_block_by_hash`), `crates/ade_node/src/node_lifecycle.rs` (`dispatch_competing_fork_choice` ‚Äî owns the per-peer branch cache + drives the walk), `crates/ade_node/src/candidate_aggregator.rs` (`build_candidate_fragment`, REUSED multi-header), `crates/ade_node/src/selector_state.rs` (`LcaError` ‚Äî the closed walk-failure type). (8 named; all resolve on disk.) |
| **CI** | `ci/ci_check_lca_anchor_walk.sh` (PHASE4-N-AO ‚Äî NEW, present + executable, names `DC-NODE-38`; fences the 1-deep regression, the multi-block LCA walk, missing-intermediate, older-than-k by block depth, lying-parent-link, cache-self-binding-violation, arrival-order permutation, and S4 body-mismatch-before-commit). _Live: CE-AO-6 (2026-06-12 diverged + the FLIP runs) exercised the walk resolving forks of depth 1‚Äì7 at the durable anchor; transcripts OUTSIDE-REPO._ |

### `DC-NODE-39`: Post-ForkChoiceWin forward-follow continuity ‚Äî after adoption at tip X, admit the winning peer's descendants in PARENT-LINK ORDER (each via validated `prev_hash == prior tip`) OR fail closed with a structured `MissingBridge`; never silently skip a bridge and stall; `MissingBridge` PRESERVES the durable chain byte-unchanged and HOLDS the forge fence‚Ä¶

_tier: derived ¬∑ status: enforced_ ¬∑ _introduced_in: PHASE4-N-AO (S11)_

> **NEW in PHASE4-N-AO (S11) ‚Äî the robustness half of `CN-CONS-03`.** Convergence is not "Ade can complete once" (S10/run-2 proved capability) but "Ade reliably continues on the selected branch or fails closed structurally". Run-1 surfaced the hole: Ade adopted cn2@298, received 388 but missed the bridge ~340, and stalled fail-closed-but-no-progress. After a ForkChoiceWin adoption at tip X, Ade must continue receiving and admitting the winning peer's descendants in PARENT-LINK ORDER (X ‚Üí X+1 ‚Üí X+2, each via validated `prev_hash == prior tip`), OR fail closed with a STRUCTURED missing-bridge reason; it must NOT silently skip a required bridge and stall behind the winning branch. A descendant whose parent link Ade has not validated is never admitted (no peer-claimed bridging ‚Äî the parent must be in Ade's validated store / proven branch). On a genuinely missing bridge (peer serves X+2 without X+1) the post-switch admit path emits a closed `MissingBridge` discriminant, PRESERVES the current durable chain byte-unchanged (no rollback, no admit, no adoption ‚Äî `MissingBridge` is never a rollback target / candidate anchor / fence-clear reason), HOLDS the forge fence (`pending_missing_bridge.is_none()` is now a fence-resolve precondition), and refuses the silent no-op. The hold is HOLD-until-progress: a real `LinearExtend` admit (`pump_block Some`) or a proven fork-switch adoption clears it. **REPLAY-EQUIVALENT.**

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | `docs/planning/phase4-n-ao-ce-ao-6-live-gap.md` (run-1 root-cause finding) + `docs/clusters/PHASE4-N-AO/S11-post-forkchoicewin-forward-follow.md` |
| **Requirement** | After a ForkChoiceWin at X, admit winning-peer descendants in PARENT-LINK ORDER (each via validated `prev_hash == prior tip`) OR fail closed with a STRUCTURED `MissingBridge`; never silently skip a bridge and stall. A descendant whose parent link Ade has not validated is never admitted (no peer-claimed bridging). On a genuine missing bridge, the path emits a closed `MissingBridge`, PRESERVES the durable chain byte-unchanged (`MissingBridge` is never a rollback target / candidate anchor / fence-clear reason), HOLDS the forge fence, and refuses the silent no-op. HOLD-until-progress: a real `LinearExtend` admit or a proven fork-switch adoption clears it. Replay-equivalent. |
| **Code** | `crates/ade_node/src/node_lifecycle.rs` (post-switch follow state + `apply_fork_switch` intersect re-point + the fail-closed `MissingBridge` decision; `pending_missing_bridge` as a fence-resolve precondition), `crates/ade_node/src/lca_walk.rs` (`walk_to_durable_lca` `BranchGap`), `crates/ade_node/src/node_sync.rs` (`classify_receive`), `crates/ade_runtime/src/admission/wire_pump.rs` (RollForward serve/follow). BLUE `select_best_chain` / `apply_fork_switch` adoption authority UNCHANGED. |

(7 named; all resolve on disk.) |
| **CI** | `ci/ci_check_missing_bridge_fail_closed.sh` (PHASE4-N-AO ‚Äî NEW, present + executable, names `DC-NODE-39`; fences the parent-link-order admit, the structured `MissingBridge` on a genuine gap, the durable-chain-unchanged + fence-hold, and the HOLD-until-progress clear). |

### `DC-NODE-40`: Rolled-back branch evidence retention for the LCA walk ‚Äî Ade's OWN rolled-back blocks are retained as walk-visible EVIDENCE (k-bounded by block depth, hash-keyed `BTreeMap`, self-binding); NEVER durable authority / rollback target / LCA anchor; closes the `MissingBridge` OVER-FIRE on loser-branch blocks‚Ä¶

_tier: derived ¬∑ status: enforced_ ¬∑ _introduced_in: PHASE4-N-AO (S13)_

> **NEW in PHASE4-N-AO (S13) ‚Äî closes the Fault-1 `MissingBridge` OVER-FIRE.** The 2026-06-13 S11 floor-fires-live grind showed a converging run emit 23 `missing_bridge` events ALL from the LOSER cn1, all `branch_gap`, with cn1 block_no fully CONSECUTIVE 9‚Üí37 (Ade received the entire branch). Root: cn1 bno10‚Äì14 `LinearExtend`-admitted pre-switch, rolled back on cn2 adoption, never in the competing-only S7 cache ‚Üí the walk for cn1 bno15+ hits the rolled-back bno14 ‚Üí `BranchGap`. For a follower this is harmless; for a PRODUCER it is a liveness denial (normal competitor traffic after a fork-switch would intermittently hold the forge fence). Rolled-back blocks MAY now be retained as walk-visible EVIDENCE: k-bounded (block depth), hash-keyed (`BTreeMap`, never HashMap-iterated for semantic ordering), self-binding (map key == re-derived block hash; a mismatch fails closed, `CacheSelfBindingViolation`). They NEVER become durable authority, a rollback target, or the LCA anchor, and NEVER bypass S2 header validation or S4 body prevalidation. The durable LCA remains the ChainDb stored slot+hash ONLY (`DC-NODE-29`); the retention merely lets `walk_to_durable_lca` traverse non-durable INTERMEDIATE headers ‚Äî exactly the blocks Ade itself rolled back during a ForkChoiceWin adoption ‚Äî until it reaches a real durable ancestor. `MissingBridge` (`DC-NODE-39`) is then reserved for a GENUINE gap (neither durable nor cache nor retention has the bridge ‚Äî Fault 2). **REPLAY-EQUIVALENT:** same rollback + same retained set ‚Üí same walk verdict.

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | `docs/planning/phase4-n-ao-ce-ao-6-live-gap.md` (S11 Fault-1 finding) + `docs/clusters/PHASE4-N-AO/S13-rolled-back-branch-evidence-retention.md` |
| **Requirement** | Rolled-back blocks MAY be retained only as walk-visible EVIDENCE: k-bounded (block depth), hash-keyed (`BTreeMap`, never HashMap-iterated), self-binding (key == re-derived hash; mismatch ‚Üí `CacheSelfBindingViolation` fail closed). NEVER durable authority / rollback target / LCA anchor; NEVER bypass S2/S4. The durable LCA stays ChainDb stored slot+hash ONLY (`DC-NODE-29`); retention lets the walk traverse Ade's OWN rolled-back intermediate headers until a real durable ancestor. `MissingBridge` reserved for a genuine gap. Replay-equivalent (same rollback + retained set ‚Üí same verdict). |
| **Code** | a `BTreeMap<Hash32, CachedHeader>` rollback-retention cache OWNED in `crates/ade_node/src/node_lifecycle.rs` `ForgeActivation` (cross-iteration, alongside `pending_fork_switch`/`pending_missing_bridge` ‚Äî NOT a `run_participant_sync` local), populated in `apply_fork_switch` BEFORE the `ChainEvent::RolledBack` apply (walk old_tip‚Üífork_anchor+1 via `ChainDb decode_block`, insert self-bound key==block_hash + k-bounded retain by `security_param.0`), consulted by `crates/ade_node/src/lca_walk.rs` `walk_to_durable_lca` on a per-peer-cache miss (`cache.get(h).or_else(|| retention.get(h))`). (6 named; all resolve on disk.) |

### `DC-NODE-41`: Missing-bridge range re-fetch for winner-descendant recovery ‚Äî when the WINNING peer presents a descendant whose parent chain is missing, Ade actively re-fetches X+1..descendant via `BlockFetch RequestRange` to that winning peer and admits IN PARENT-LINK ORDER through `pump_block`, OR remains fail-closed with a structured `MissingBridge`; byte-only; winning-peer-only; bounded-retry‚Ä¶

_tier: derived ¬∑ status: enforced_ ¬∑ _introduced_in: PHASE4-N-AO (S14)_

> **NEW in PHASE4-N-AO (S14) ‚Äî the active-recovery half the passive `DC-NODE-39` floor cannot cover.** ChainSync delivers each block once and never re-sends, so the `DC-NODE-39` floor alone cannot recover a bridge ChainSync already streamed past ‚Äî a winning-peer descendant that arrived before its never-received bridge strands Ade fail-closed forever (run-1's stall). When a post-ForkChoiceWin WINNING peer (the peer Ade just adopted from) presents a descendant whose parent chain is missing, Ade must EITHER (a) actively re-fetch the missing range from the adopted tip to that descendant via `BlockFetch RequestRange(X+1..descendant)` to that winning peer and admit it IN PARENT-LINK ORDER through `pump_block` (each body parent-link + body-hash validated before admit; X+1 then X+2 ‚Ä¶ then the descendant), OR (b) remain fail-closed with a structured `MissingBridge` (closed failure code). It must NOT passively stall forever, and must NOT admit out of order. The re-fetch is byte-only (`BlockFetch` transports bytes, NOT truth ‚Äî a lying/short/unservable range leaves the structured hold, no admit, no mutation), targets ONLY the winning peer (a non-winning-peer gap takes the unchanged floor path ‚Äî no fetch spam on loser orphans), is bounded-retry (deterministic, no spin), and clears the hold + fence ONLY on real admitted progress. **S14 is RECOVERY, not selection:** S3 (`select_best_chain`, `DC-CONS-03`) already decided the winner; S14 never decides a branch wins. `pump_block` remains the sole admit (BLUE unchanged); the `BlockFetch` byte machinery is reused from S6 (`prefetch_branch_bodies`). **REPLAY-EQUIVALENT:** same served range ‚Üí same admitted post-state.

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | `docs/planning/phase4-n-ao-ce-ao-6-live-gap.md` (S11 Fault-2 finding) + `docs/clusters/PHASE4-N-AO/S14-missing-bridge-range-refetch.md` |
| **Requirement** | When the WINNING peer presents a descendant whose parent chain is missing, Ade EITHER (a) re-fetches X+1..descendant via `BlockFetch RequestRange` to that winning peer and admits in parent-link order through `pump_block` (each body parent-link + body-hash validated; X+1 then X+2 ‚Ä¶ then the descendant), OR (b) remains fail-closed with a structured `MissingBridge`. Never passively stall forever; never admit out of order. Byte-only (a lying/short range leaves the hold, no admit/mutation); winning-peer-only (no fetch spam on loser orphans); bounded-retry; clears hold+fence ONLY on real admitted progress. Recovery, not selection ‚Äî `pump_block` is the sole admit (BLUE unchanged). Replay-equivalent. |
| **Code** | `crates/ade_node/src/fork_switch.rs` (closed `RangeRefetchOutcome{Admitted|Unavailable|ShortRange|BodyHeaderMismatch|ParentLinkMismatch|ValidationFailed}` + `as_str`, `RangeRefetch`/`PostSwitchFollow` types, `MAX_RANGE_REFETCH_ATTEMPTS` + `range_refetch_should_retry` bounded-retry RED policy, `PrefetchedBranchBodies::ordered_for_peer`), `crates/ade_node/src/node_lifecycle.rs` (`recover_missing_range` ‚Äî `pump_block` sole admit, per-block `block_admitted` evidence; `dispatch_competing_fork_choice` walk-fail arm sets `pending_range_refetch` ONLY for a winning-peer descendant ahead of the durable tip; the relay loop drives a staleness-guarded bounded-retry `prefetch_branch_bodies(S6, byte-only) ‚Üí recover_missing_range`, clearing the hold ONLY on `RangeRefetchOutcome::Admitted`), closed `range_refetch_started`/`completed` events in `crates/ade_node/src/admission_log/{event,writer}.rs` + emit in `convergence_evidence.rs`. BLUE validation/select/apply/`pump_block` UNCHANGED. |

(6 named; all resolve on disk.) |

### `DC-PROD-03`: Producer chain-forward continuity + replay. The GREEN ChainEvolution linear‚Ä¶

_tier: derived ¬∑ status: enforced_

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | docs/planning/phase4-n-t-invariants.md ¬ß3, ¬ß4 (R1, R3); docs/clusters/PHASE4-N-T/cluster.md ¬ß1.5, ¬ß7 |
| **Requirement** | Producer chain-forward continuity + replay. The GREEN ChainEvolution linear typestate threads each forge's post-state (post-ledger, post-chain_dep, new tip) into the next forge's base; forging against a stale base is structurally unrepresentable (advance consumes self). advance obtains the post-state from BLUE block_validity and the AcceptedBlock token from BLUE self_accept against identical inputs (same pre-forge base, forged bytes, era_schedule, ledger_view); if the two authorities disagree it returns ChainEvolutionError::AuthorityMismatch and does not advance. ChainEvolution never constructs AcceptedBlock directly. For a fixed (bootstrap seed, canonical slot-sequence, KES/VRF/cold keys) the chain-evolution series (block_number, prev_hash, post-ledger fingerprint, post-chain_dep) and the forged block bytes are byte-identical across runs (in-memory two-run; no on-disk replay corpus ‚Äî durability deferred to N-U). |

### `DC-PROTO-01`: Protocol state machines have deterministic transitions

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|

### `DC-PROTO-06`: BLUE mini-protocol transitions are pure functions of (canonical prior state‚Ä¶

_tier: derived ¬∑ status: declared_

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | Project constitution ¬ß2; PHASE4-N-A invariants ¬ß7 decision 1 (docs/active/PHASE4-N-A_invariants.md) |

### `DC-PROTO-10`: Chain-sync server FindIntersect cursor ‚Äî after IntersectFound(point) the read cursor IS that point; next RequestNext serves next_after(point), never block 0‚Ä¶

_tier: derived ¬∑ status: enforced_ ¬∑ _introduced_in: PHASE4-N-AE_

> **NEW in PHASE4-N-AE (AE.E, 2026-06-07) ‚Äî the actual CE-A5 closer.** Across four prior CE-A5 reruns the real Haskell relay rejected `HeaderEnvelopeError (UnexpectedBlockNo (BlockNo N) (BlockNo 0))`: the FindIntersect handler resolved the intersect (the relay's own tip) and replied `IntersectFound`, but never set `last_announced`, so the next `RequestNext` served `next_after(None)` = block 0. `ChainDbServedSource::intersect`/`next_after` were verified CORRECT on the live store; the defect was the SERVER not threading the resolved intersect into the cursor. Fix: `state.last_announced = Block‚ÜíSome((slot,hash)) | Origin‚ÜíNone`. Origin-sync clients were unaffected (None is correct for them) ‚Äî why earlier producer-serve clusters (N-G) passed. With the fix, a real cardano-node 11.0.1 relay `AddedToCurrentChain` Ade's forged block (CE-A5 manifest).

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | `docs/clusters/PHASE4-N-AE/slices/AE.E.md`; `docs/evidence/phase4-n-ae-ce-a5-relay-adoption.md` |
| **Requirement** | After the producer chain-sync server answers `IntersectFound(point)`, its read cursor (`last_announced`) IS that point ‚Äî the next `RequestNext` serves `next_after(point)` (the successor the client rolls forward onto), never `next_after(None)` (the chain start). A non-Origin intersect that left the cursor unset would serve block 0 to a client whose read pointer is its own tip, which the client rejects as `UnexpectedBlockNo(tip_block_no + 1)(0)`. An Origin intersect keeps the cursor `None` (serve from the chain start, correct). |
| **Code** | `crates/ade_network/src/chain_sync/server.rs` (`producer_chain_sync_serve` FindIntersect handler ‚Äî sets `state.last_announced = match &point { Point::Block { slot, hash } => Some((*slot, hash.clone())), Point::Origin => None }` from the matched intersect point, at `server.rs:266`) |
| **Tests** | `crates/ade_network/src/chain_sync/server.rs::tests::producer_chain_sync_serve_find_intersect_sets_cursor_then_rolls_forward_past_it` (FindIntersect at a non-tip block ‚Üí cursor set ‚Üí next `RequestNext` RollForwards the successor, not block 0). (1 named; resolves on disk.) |
| **CI** | _(no dedicated CI gate ‚Äî test-enforced; `ci_script = ""` in the registry)_. **Enforcement gap, surfaced honestly:** the cursor-threading invariant is proven by the regression test above but has NO dedicated `ci/ci_check_*.sh` gate. Candidate follow-on: a gate fencing that the FindIntersect arm sets `last_announced` from the matched point (mirroring the existing chain-sync-server closure gates). _Not blocking ‚Äî the live CE-A5 adoption + the regression test cover it; recorded so the next slice can close it._ |

### `DC-PUMP-01`: Wire pump emits AdmissionPeerEvent::{Block, TipUpdate, Disconnected} only. It‚Ä¶

The four-cell contract below is unchanged.

The verdict remains the GREEN reducer's sole output (memory [[feedback-evidence-reducers-are-green-not-authority]] + ¬¨P-C3 no RED-derived verdicts). |

### `DC-PUMP-02`: A closed authority event on every chain-sync reply carrying a Tip ‚Äî `TipUpdate` for IntersectFound / IntersectNotFound / RollForward; the DISTINCT `AdmissionPeerEvent::RollBackward` for RollBackward‚Ä¶

_tier: derived ¬∑ status: enforced_ ¬∑ _strengthened_in: PHASE4-N-AN_

> **Strengthened in PHASE4-N-AN (gate triage, `89facbea`, CI-script + registry only ‚Äî NO source change).** The "closed event per reply" invariant is refined to record the AI-S4a split: the `RollBackward` arm emits the DISTINCT `AdmissionPeerEvent::RollBackward` (the closed fork-choice / durable-rollback signal carrying the peer's post-rollback tip), NOT a generic `TipUpdate`. `strengthened_in += PHASE4-N-AN`; the gate `ci/ci_check_admission_wire_pump_closure.sh` was updated to assert the `RollBackward` arm emits `AdmissionPeerEvent::RollBackward` (and the other three arms `tip_update`). The per-reply-closed-event invariant is preserved ‚Äî the `RollBackward` reply's closed event is simply its own variant.

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | docs/planning/phase4-n-m-c-operator-pass-invariants.md ¬ß1 (I-C7); refined for PHASE4-N-AI AI-S4a in the PHASE4-N-AN gate triage |
| **Requirement** | A CLOSED authority event is emitted on every chain-sync reply carrying a Tip: `TipUpdate` for IntersectFound / IntersectNotFound / RollForward; the DISTINCT `AdmissionPeerEvent::RollBackward` for RollBackward (AI-S4a ‚Äî a rollback is NEVER represented as a `TipUpdate` only; it is the closed fork-choice / durable-rollback signal carrying the peer's post-rollback tip). The runner's next `verdict::derive` / fork-choice call sees the freshest peer comparison input. |
| **Code** | `crates/ade_runtime/src/admission/wire_pump.rs` (handle_chain_sync: the IntersectFound / IntersectNotFound / RollForward arms call `tip_update`; the RollBackward arm emits `AdmissionPeerEvent::RollBackward` ‚Äî the distinct AI-S4a fork-choice signal ‚Äî before any other action) |
| **Tests** | `admission::wire_pump::tests::pump_emits_tip_update_and_request_next_on_intersect_found_no_block_fetch`, `admission::wire_pump::tests::pump_emits_tip_update_on_intersect_not_found`, `admission::wire_pump::tests::rollforward_drives_block_fetch_then_request_next` (the distinct `RollBackward` event is additionally exercised by the AI-S4a / AK-S2 rollback tests under `DC-NODE-23` / `DC-NODE-32` / `DC-NODE-33` and asserted structurally by the CI gate) |
| **CI** | `ci/ci_check_admission_wire_pump_closure.sh` (PHASE4-N-AN: the gate now asserts the four chain-sync arms each emit their closed authority event ‚Äî `IntersectFound`/`IntersectNotFound`/`RollForward` ‚Üí `AdmissionPeerEvent::TipUpdate`; `RollBackward` ‚Üí `AdmissionPeerEvent::RollBackward`) |

### `DC-PUMP-03`: Wire-pump keep-alive client ‚Äî `run_admission_wire_pump` runs the N2N keep-alive CLIENT (mini-protocol 8) on a cadence STRICTLY under the peer timeout, advancing the REUSED BLUE `ade_network::keep_alive` state machine; WIRE-ONLY (no `AdmissionPeerEvent`)‚Ä¶

_tier: derived ¬∑ status: enforced_ ¬∑ _introduced_in: PHASE4-N-AM_

> **NEW in PHASE4-N-AM (AM-S1).** The admission wire pump (`run_admission_wire_pump` ‚Äî the SOLE per-peer pump, `CN-PUMP-01`) now runs the N2N keep-alive CLIENT (mini-protocol 8): a `tokio::select!` cadence arm (`KEEP_ALIVE_CADENCE = 20s`, STRICTLY under the peer's ~97s keep-alive timeout) sends `KeepAliveMessage::KeepAlive(cookie)` (Initiator) via the EXISTING outbound `OutboundFrame` path, advancing the REUSED BLUE `ade_network::keep_alive` state machine (`ClientIdle ‚Üí ServerHasAgency{cookie}`); on the inbound `MsgResponseKeepAlive(cookie')` `handle_keep_alive` advances the SAME state machine (`ServerHasAgency{cookie} + Server ‚Üí ClientIdle`, validating `cookie' == cookie`). **WIRE-ONLY:** the keep-alive client produces NO canonical input, NO WAL entry, and NO `AdmissionPeerEvent` (Block / TipUpdate / RollBackward / Disconnected) ‚Äî it never affects admission, the durable chain, fork-choice, the convergence-evidence vocabulary, replay-equivalence, or any BLUE state (the `DC-PUMP-01` emit-set stays unwidened). MUST NOT: redefine the BLUE keep-alive grammar (reuse `ade_network::keep_alive` + `::codec::keep_alive`); use a cadence ‚â• the peer timeout; send a new `MsgKeepAlive` while one is in flight (respect `ServerHasAgency` agency); starve/reorder the chain-sync or block-fetch flow; dispatch a keep-alive frame as a chain-sync/block-fetch event; silently swallow a grammar violation (fail closed via `AdmissionWirePumpError::KeepAlive` ‚Äî drop the peer); use rand / wall-clock for the cookie (monotonic `u16` counter); implement a keep-alive SERVER/responder (client only ‚Äî the responder is a CE-AM-LIVE-gated follow-on). With the client running, a live participant AND single-producer follow sustains past the ~97s keep-alive deadline ‚Äî the prerequisite that makes the CE-AI-6 induced-reorg convergence capture (the N-AN live evidence) runnable. **SCOPE:** the keep-alive client ONLY; does NOT add multi-peer ChainSel, does NOT flip `CN-CONS-03`, does NOT broaden `CN-PUMP-01` / `DC-PUMP-01` / `DC-PUMP-02` (cross-refs, preserved).

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | `docs/planning/phase4-n-am-wire-pump-keepalive-sustain-invariants.md` + `docs/clusters/completed/PHASE4-N-AM/cluster.md` (planning + cluster docs; no normative-doc anchor in `.idd-config.json` `normative_docs` ‚Äî the established N-series live-wire pattern, surfaced here, not a new gap) |
| **Requirement** | The admission wire pump runs the N2N keep-alive CLIENT (mini-protocol 8) on a cadence STRICTLY under the peer's keep-alive timeout, sending `KeepAliveMessage::KeepAlive(cookie)` (Initiator) via the EXISTING outbound path and advancing the REUSED BLUE `ade_network::keep_alive` state machine; the inbound `MsgResponseKeepAlive(cookie')` advances the SAME state machine validating `cookie' == cookie`. WIRE-ONLY: the keep-alive client emits NO `AdmissionPeerEvent`, no canonical input, no WAL entry ‚Äî it never affects admission/chain/fork-choice/replay/BLUE state (the `DC-PUMP-01` emit-set stays unwidened). MUST reuse (never redefine) the BLUE keep-alive grammar; cadence < peer timeout; respect `ServerHasAgency` (no overlapping in-flight MsgKeepAlive); fail closed via `AdmissionWirePumpError::KeepAlive`; monotonic `u16` cookie (no rand/wall-clock); CLIENT only. |
| **Code** | `crates/ade_runtime/src/admission/wire_pump.rs` (`run_admission_wire_pump` ‚Äî the keep-alive client: a `tokio::select!` cadence arm `tokio::time::interval(KEEP_ALIVE_CADENCE)` / `KEEP_ALIVE_CADENCE = 20s` sends `MsgKeepAlive` Initiator under the peer timeout via the existing `OutboundFrame` path; `handle_keep_alive` validates the echoed cookie on the inbound `DeliverPeerFrame{KeepAlive}`; wire-only ‚Äî emits no `AdmissionPeerEvent`; new `AdmissionWirePumpError::KeepAlive` fail-closed variant); `crates/ade_network/src/keep_alive/transition.rs` (BLUE `keep_alive_transition` ‚Äî REUSED, unchanged); `crates/ade_network/src/codec/keep_alive.rs` (BLUE `KeepAliveMessage` codec ‚Äî REUSED, unchanged) |
| **Tests** | `crates/ade_runtime/src/admission/wire_pump.rs` (`admission::wire_pump::tests`): `wire_pump_sends_keep_alive_on_quiescent_cadence` (CE-AM-1 ‚Äî under `#[tokio::test(start_paused)]` virtual time, the production select! emits a real proto-8 `MsgKeepAlive` over a loopback mux during inbound quiescence, no `AdmissionPeerEvent`), `wire_pump_keep_alive_response_validates_cookie_no_event` (CE-AM-2 ‚Äî the echoed cookie advances the BLUE state machine, emits no event), `wire_pump_keep_alive_cookie_mismatch_fails_closed` (CE-AM-3 ‚Äî cookie mismatch / unsolicited-ClientIdle response / undecodable payload all ‚Üí `AdmissionWirePumpError::KeepAlive` fail-closed). (3 named; all resolve on disk.) |
| **CI** | `ci/ci_check_keep_alive_wire_only.sh` (NEW, PHASE4-N-AM ‚Äî the keep-alive client is WIRE-ONLY: `handle_keep_alive` is defined exactly once and drives the BLUE `keep_alive_transition` over a `decode_keep_alive_message` (consumes the peer's `MsgResponseKeepAlive`); its body constructs NO `AdmissionPeerEvent` (returns `Result<(), KeepAliveError>`, no event channel); the cadence tick enqueues an `OutboundFrame` on `AcceptedMiniProtocol::KeepAlive` via `encode_keep_alive_message` and synthesizes NO semantic event; the pump REUSES the BLUE `ade_network::keep_alive` grammar ‚Äî does not redefine the state machine or message type in the RED pump file). _Live: CE-AM-LIVE PASSED (2026-06-11, frozen c2-testnet relay, magic 42) ‚Äî the keep-alive client SUSTAINED the link 152s (vs the prior ~96s EOF): 7 `MsgKeepAlive` on the ~20s cadence, 7 `MsgResponseKeepAlive` cookies VALIDATED, 0 grammar failures, 0 idle-EOF. NOT a CE-AI-6 claim (no reorg in the sustain run); transcript OUTSIDE-REPO (competition-secrecy / no-credential-leak discipline)._ |

### `DC-PUMP-04`: Multi-peer wire-pump fairness ‚Äî each peer's `run_admission_wire_pump` feeds its OWN bounded lane; a deterministic configured-order `fair_merge` (round-robin, one item per peer per round) gives each active peer bounded delivery opportunity; backpressure is PER-PEER, never global starvation; the RED merge order MUST NOT decide fork-choice‚Ä¶

_tier: derived ¬∑ status: enforced_ ¬∑ _introduced_in: PHASE4-N-AO (S8)_

> **NEW in PHASE4-N-AO (S8) ‚Äî the gap the S7 live retry surfaced.** The S7 live retry CE-AO-6 observed 46 blocks all from one peer, 0 from the other, despite both connected: a single continuously-producing peer monopolised the shared bounded mpsc and starved the other peer's pump ‚Äî so the competing peer's branch never reached the participant dispatch and live multi-candidate SELECT could not fire. A Byzantine/hot peer could thereby SUPPRESS a competing honest branch from fork-choice purely by out-producing into the shared feed (a liveness/eclipse-flavoured denial of the SELECT input, NOT a safety break ‚Äî the node still fails closed). When multiple peers are connected to the participant receive path, no connected peer may be STARVED by another continuously-producing peer. Each peer's `run_admission_wire_pump` task feeds its OWN bounded queue (per-peer channel); a fair merge over a DETERMINISTIC order DERIVED FROM the configured `--peer` order (an explicit `Vec`, never HashMap/HashSet iteration, never scheduler timing) gives each active peer bounded delivery opportunity (round-robin, one item per peer per round); backpressure is PER-PEER (a hot peer fills its own bounded queue and self-blocks), NEVER global starvation; a disconnected peer's lane is retired in place WITHOUT reordering the remaining peers. **The merge order is RED scheduling discipline ONLY** ‚Äî it may affect delivery OPPORTUNITY but MUST NOT decide fork-choice: `select_best_chain` stays arrival-order independent (`CN-CONS-01`), peer identity is preserved through the merge (`DC-NODE-34`), and the merged stream the consumer reads is unchanged in shape (one peer-attributed `NodeSyncItem::Block` sequence). **NOTE:** the 2026-06-13 instrumented repro overturned the original "channel starvation" diagnosis ‚Äî the real blocker was an evidence MISLABEL (`emit_block_received` used a fixed first-peer label, fixed in `6846d252`); S8 stays correct + proven (a cleaner per-peer-lane arch) but was NOT the blocker.

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | `docs/planning/phase4-n-ao-ce-ao-6-live-gap.md` (S7-retry finding) + `docs/clusters/PHASE4-N-AO/S8-multi-peer-wire-pump-fairness.md` |
| **Requirement** | When multiple peers are connected to the participant receive path, no connected peer may be STARVED by another continuously-producing peer. Each peer's `run_admission_wire_pump` feeds its OWN bounded lane; a fair merge over a DETERMINISTIC configured-`--peer`-order (an explicit `Vec`, never HashMap/HashSet iteration, never scheduler timing) gives each active peer bounded delivery opportunity (round-robin, one item per peer per round); backpressure is PER-PEER, never global starvation; a disconnected lane is retired in place without reordering the rest. The RED merge order may affect delivery OPPORTUNITY but MUST NOT decide fork-choice: `select_best_chain` stays arrival-order independent (`CN-CONS-01`), peer identity preserved (`DC-NODE-34`), the merged stream unchanged in shape. |
| **Code** | `crates/ade_node/src/fair_merge.rs` (`fair_merge` ‚Äî per-peer bounded lanes + the deterministic round-robin merge over the configured-order rotating cursor; closed-lane retire-in-place; no HashMap/wall-clock/rand; RED-only), `crates/ade_node/src/node_lifecycle.rs` (`spawn_live_wire_pump_source` ‚Äî per-peer bounded channels feeding the single `WirePump` rx via `fair_merge`; the shared-channel fan-in is GONE). `run_admission_wire_pump` (per-peer pump) + `NodeBlockSource::WirePump`/`next_item` UNCHANGED. BLUE selector UNCHANGED. |
| **Tests** | `crates/ade_node/src/fair_merge.rs`: `hot_peer_cannot_starve_quiet_peer` (per-peer backpressure, not global starvation), `closed_lane_removed_without_reordering_remaining_peers`, `peer_identity_preserved_through_merge` (the peer label survives the merge). (3 named; all resolve on disk; plus the deterministic-peer-order-from-config + single-peer-unchanged tests in the 6-test fairness suite.) |
| **CI** | `ci/ci_check_wire_pump_fairness.sh` (PHASE4-N-AO ‚Äî NEW, present + executable, names `DC-PUMP-04`; fences hot-peer-no-starve, per-peer-backpressure-not-global, peer-identity-through-merge, deterministic-peer-order-from-config, closed-lane-removed-without-reorder, single-peer-unchanged). _The FULL live multi-peer SELECT assertions stay on the CE-AO-6 live retry ‚Äî synthetic fairness tests do NOT pretend to prove live two-producer fork-choice convergence._ |

### `DC-SERVEMEM-01`: Peer-driven serve range work is bounded ‚Äî the `--mode node` serve path never materializes an unbounded range or a per-block hash-index scan (operational-hardening; NOT a Cardano semantic parameter)

_tier: derived ¬∑ status: enforced_ ¬∑ _introduced_in: PHASE4-N-AA_ ¬∑ _strengthened_in: PHASE4-N-AB_

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | `docs/clusters/completed/PHASE4-N-AA/cluster.md` (cluster doc archived to `completed/` at close); the PHASE4-N-U cross-slice security review (MEDIUM finding ‚Äî peer-driven serve resource amplification) |
| **Requirement** | Peer-driven serve range work is bounded. The `--mode node` serve path MUST NOT materialize an unbounded chain range, perform per-block full-index (hash) scans, or read more than `MAX_SERVE_RANGE_BLOCKS` blocks for a single peer request. Oversized ranges fail closed (‚Üí wire `NoBlocks`) BEFORE unbounded storage/CPU work. The cap is a defensive implementation bound (`MAX_SERVE_RANGE_BLOCKS` = 256, symmetric with the receive-side `MAX_WIRE_PUMP_LOOKAHEAD` / `DC-LIVEMEM-01`), NOT a Cardano semantic parameter, and cannot be disabled at runtime (no CLI / env / config escape). |
| **Code** | `crates/ade_runtime/src/chaindb/mod.rs` (S1 ‚Äî the `ChainDb` trait declares the bounded, hash-free read primitives `range_bytes_capped(from, to, max) -> CappedSlotRange` (‚â§ `max` `(slot, bytes)` ascending, `truncated` flag, NO hash-index scan) + `last_block_bytes() -> Option<(SlotNo, Vec<u8>)>` (O(log N) tip, no full iteration)); `crates/ade_runtime/src/chaindb/types.rs` (`CappedSlotRange { blocks, truncated }`); `crates/ade_runtime/src/chaindb/persistent.rs` + `crates/ade_runtime/src/chaindb/in_memory.rs` (S1 impls ‚Äî both guard the inverted range `from > to` ‚Üí empty, no panic / overflow); `crates/ade_runtime/src/network/served_chain_projection.rs` (S2 ‚Äî `ChainDbServedSource` `range_bytes` / `next_after` / `tip` read the bounded primitives, apply the `MAX_SERVE_RANGE_BLOCKS` cap, and derive each block's hash from its bytes via the single BLUE `decode_block` authority; the closed `ServeRangeOutcome { Served \| Empty \| CapExceeded \| ReadError }` fails closed ‚Äî every non-`Served` variant ‚Üí wire `NoBlocks`) |
| **Tests** | S1 contract ‚Äî generic `<D: ChainDb>` bodies run against BOTH impls via `run_contract_tests` (`crates/ade_runtime/src/chaindb/contract.rs::tests::in_memory_passes_contract` + the `run_contract_tests` invocation in `crates/ade_runtime/src/chaindb/persistent.rs`): `‚Ä¶/contract.rs::range_bytes_capped_returns_at_most_max` (10-block range, cap 3 ‚Üí exactly 3 + `truncated`), `‚Ä¶::range_bytes_capped_within_cap_not_truncated`, `‚Ä¶::range_bytes_capped_respects_bounds` (inclusive `[from,to]`), `‚Ä¶::range_bytes_capped_bytes_byte_identical` (served bytes == stored bytes verbatim), `‚Ä¶::last_block_bytes_returns_highest_slot`, **`‚Ä¶::range_bytes_capped_inverted_range_is_empty`** (inverted + extreme-endpoint `from > to` ‚Üí empty, no panic). S2 serve (`served_chain_projection.rs` `#[cfg(test)]`): `serve_range_over_cap_fails_closed` (> cap ‚Üí `CapExceeded`), `serve_range_empty_window_is_empty_not_capexceeded` (genuinely-empty ‚âÝ cap), `serve_range_undecodable_in_range_fails_closed`, **`serve_range_inverted_range_fails_closed`**. Within-cap real-bytes parity (real forged blocks): `crates/ade_node/tests/node_spine_serve_loopback.rs::served_view_projects_durable_chain`, `‚Ä¶::follower_fetches_coherent_history_incl_ingested_predecessor`. (The registry `DC-SERVEMEM-01.tests` array names **12**; all **12** resolve on disk ‚Äî exactly one `fn <name>` each ‚Äî including the two inverted-range tests `range_bytes_capped_inverted_range_is_empty` (S1) + `serve_range_inverted_range_fails_closed` (S2). **0 unappended; 0 open registry reconciliations** ‚Äî the `tests`/`code_locus` reconciliations surfaced at the N-AA pass were RESOLVED in commit `e9cd60fc`.) |
| **CI** | `ci/ci_check_serve_range_bounded.sh` (NEW ‚Äî fails the build if the serve path uses the unbounded `iter_from_slot` (full-range `Vec` + per-block `SLOT_BY_HASH` scan) or O(N) `chaindb.tip()`, if `MAX_SERVE_RANGE_BLOCKS` is not a fixed literal / gains a CLI-env-config escape, or if a second hash authority / `SLOT_BY_HASH` reference appears on the serve path; non-vacuous ‚Äî pre-S2 HEAD tripped Guards 2/3, S2 has 0 such calls) |

_registry‚Üîdisk: **0 drift, 0 open reconciliations** at HEAD `c6e7fafe`. The registry `DC-SERVEMEM-01.tests` array carries all **12** on-disk tests and the `code_locus` reads `chaindb/mod.rs` + `chaindb/types.rs` (+ `persistent.rs` + `in_memory.rs` + `served_chain_projection.rs`); every cited test leaf-fn resolves on disk (exactly one each) and every cited locus exists. (Pinned historical N-AA-delta snapshot: at the N-AA pass the `tests` array listed 10 of 12 and the `code_locus` cited `chaindb/contract.rs`; BOTH were RESOLVED in commit `e9cd60fc`, the PHASE4-N-AA grounding-doc refresh.)_

_PHASE4-N-AB strengthening (`strengthened_in += "PHASE4-N-AB"`): the bounded serve read path can now also **transmit** a large in-range block. Pre-N-AB the serve was bounded on the READ side (this rule), but the GREEN session reducer's `handle_outbound` + `encode_inner_frame` both errored above `MAX_PAYLOAD` = 65535 ‚Äî so a within-cap block larger than one mux SDU could be read but not sent. `CN-SESS-05` adds the outbound segmentation (split into ordered `<= MAX_PAYLOAD` frames, fail closed above `MAX_OUTBOUND_PAYLOAD_BYTES` = 16 MiB), making the bounded serve end-to-end functional. This rule's own four-cell contract (Code / Tests / CI above) is unchanged ‚Äî the strengthening is the transmit-side completion, not a re-scope of the read-path bound._

### `DC-SNAPSHOT-01`: ServedChainHandle::push_atomic is deterministic in its argument order: the‚Ä¶

_tier: derived ¬∑ status: enforced_

| Aspect | Location |

Replay-equivalence anchor for the broadcast ‚Üí serve path. |
| **Code** | `crates/ade_runtime/src/producer/served_chain_handle.rs` (push_atomic uses send_modify with served_chain_admit ‚Äî the established broadcast_to_served drain-and-admit determinism carries through); `crates/ade_runtime/src/producer/broadcast_to_served.rs` (existing determinism tests cover the underlying invariant; push_atomic is a thin closure around the same primitive) |

### `DC-STORE-09`: Snapshot bytes carry a closed u32 version tag (initial == 1) and the source‚Ä¶

### `DC-SYNC-01`: During network forward-sync, a block's preserved wire bytes and its WAL entry‚Ä¶

_tier: derived ¬∑ status: enforced_

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | docs/clusters/PHASE4-N-Y/S2-network-forward-sync.md; S6-torn-write-recovery-reconciliation.md |
| **Requirement** | During network forward-sync, a block's preserved wire bytes and its WAL entry MUST be durable before the chain tip advances to it, and admission is chokepoint-only (decode -> validate_and_apply_header -> block_validity -> fork-choice). The GREEN forward-sync lifecycle reducer emits a closed SyncEffect set; AdvanceTip is constructible only after StoreBlockBytes+AppendWal (private AdmitPlan, single durable() emit site), and the RED pump fail-closes (TipBeforeDurable) on any out-of-order apply. Because tip is derived from stored blocks, recovery reconciles the chaindb to the WAL tail so a torn put_block/wal-append crash cannot incorporate an un-WAL'd orphan (S6). |
| **Code** | crates/ade_runtime/src/forward_sync/{reducer,pump}.rs; `crates/ade_runtime/src/recovery/restart.rs` (WAL-tail reconciliation) |
| **Tests** | `forward_sync_wal_and_bytes_precede_tip_advance`, `forward_sync_replay_two_runs_byte_identical`, `forward_sync_admission_through_chokepoints`, `recovery_torn_put_block_before_wal_append_drops_orphan`, `node_sync_pump_advances_recoverable_tip`, `node_sync_fails_closed_on_undecodable_block`, `node_sync_kill_then_warm_start_recovers_same_tip` |
| **CI** | `ci/ci_check_forward_sync_chokepoint_only.sh`, `ci/ci_check_node_sync_via_pump.sh` |

### `DC-TXV-05`: For each era, required_signers(state, tx_body) is a closed, explicit‚Ä¶

_tier: derived ¬∑ status: enforced_

### `DC-TXV-06`: For each era, the certificate-deposit classification map(state, cert) is a‚Ä¶

_tier: derived ¬∑ status: enforced_

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | Cardano ledger spec (Conway CDDL certificate tags 0..18; UTXO deposit/refund accounting); IDD fail-fast + closed-surface doctrine |
| **Requirement** | For each era, the certificate-deposit classification map(state, cert) is a closed, total, era-versioned function: every certificate variant resolves to exactly one of new_deposit(coin) \| refund(coin) \| neutral \| explicit_reject, with the coin sourced from the cert (Conway explicit-deposit variants, tags 7/8) or the protocol parameter (legacy variants, tags 0/1). An unrecognized cert tag, malformed cert CBOR, or undecodable withdrawals field is a deterministic reject, never a silent neutral. State-dependent cases that cannot be accounted (e.g. pool re-registration charged as a new deposit) reject with a structured UnsupportedStateDependentDepositAccounting error rather than guessing. Incomplete classification is a forbidden false-accept path feeding the value-conservation equation. |
| **Code** | `crates/ade_codec/src/conway/cert.rs` (decode_conway_certs, closed ConwayCert grammar); `crates/ade_codec/src/error.rs` (CodecError::UnknownCertTag); `crates/ade_types/src/conway/cert.rs` (ConwayCert, CertDisposition, DepositEffect, CoinSource); `crates/ade_ledger/src/cert_classify.rs` (classify); `crates/ade_ledger/src/error.rs` (UnsupportedStateDependentDepositAccounting); corpus/conway_certs/{classification_table.md,tags.json} |
| **Tests** | `decode_total_over_tags_0_18`, `unknown_cert_tag_is_codec_error`, `removed_tag_5_6_is_not_valid_in_conway`, `malformed_cert_cbor_rejected`, `decode_is_replay_deterministic`, `class_mapping_is_total`, `legacy_unregistration_unresolved_is_unsupported_state_dependent`, `legacy_unregistration_resolves_recorded_deposit`, `pool_reregistration_is_neutral`, `pool_new_registration_charges_pool_deposit` |
| **CI** | `ci/ci_check_conway_cert_classification_closed.sh` |

### `DC-VAL-05`: A Valid block yields evolved (LedgerState', PraosChainDepState'); an Invalid‚Ä¶

_tier: derived ¬∑ status: enforced_

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | IDD explicit-total-transition doctrine; Cardano ledger spec |
| **Requirement** | A Valid block yields evolved (LedgerState', PraosChainDepState'); an Invalid block yields the unchanged input states plus a structured reason. No partial or in-place mutation occurs on the invalid path. |
| **Code** | crates/ade_ledger/src/block_validity/ (closed verdict taxonomy: Valid carries evolved-state stats, Invalid carries structured reason; PHASE4-B1-S3), `crates/ade_ledger/src/block_validity/transition.rs` (Valid returns evolved (ledger', chain_dep'); Invalid returns input clones; PHASE4-B1-S4) |
| **Tests** | `invalid_block_leaves_state_unchanged`, `valid_block_evolves_both_states` |
| **CI** | `ci/ci_check_consensus_closed_enums.sh` |

### `DC-VAL-06`: Every crypto-input, field-size, and structural check on the authority path‚Ä¶

_tier: derived ¬∑ status: enforced_

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | Cardano ledger spec (mandatory witness/field checks); IDD fail-fast doctrine |
| **Requirement** | Every crypto-input, field-size, and structural check on the authority path rejects (produces Invalid) on wrong size or shape and never silently skips. The pattern `if X.len() == K { check } else { skip }` is forbidden in BLUE validation; size checks go through a helper that returns an error. No defined-but-unwired check and no tautological (value-compared-to-itself) guard may stand in for a real check. |
| **Code** | `crates/ade_ledger/src/block_validity/verdict.rs` (FieldKind/FieldError closed fail-closed field taxonomy; PHASE4-B1-S3); `crates/ade_core/src/consensus/kes_check.rs` (expect_size fail-closed header crypto-field guard; PHASE4-B1-S5); `crates/ade_testkit/src/validity/adversarial.rs` (M1 truncated VRF proof, M3 flipped KES sig, M4 slot-beyond-horizon adversarial mutators exercising the fail-closed checks; PHASE4-B1-S7); `crates/ade_ledger/src/tx_validity/witness.rs` (wrong-size vkey/sig ‚Üí MalformedWitnessField via from_bytes, never skipped); `crates/ade_ledger/src/tx_validity/required_signers.rs` (unresolvable input / malformed certs\|withdrawals\|voters CBOR ‚Üí structured RequiredSignerError, never silent skip; PHASE4-B2-S1); `crates/ade_ledger/src/conway.rs` (check_conway_coin_conservation: closed coin-level preservation-of-value check wired into validate_conway_state_backed ‚Äî closes the state-backed fail-open gap where outputs+fee != inputs was accepted at track_utxo=true; PHASE4-B2-S4); `crates/ade_testkit/src/tx_validity/adversarial.rs` (GREEN witness/value/input mutators driving tx_validity fail-closed; PHASE4-B2-S4) |
| **Tests** | `expect_size_rejects_wrong_length`, `praos_malformed_kes_sig_rejected`, `no_mutation_is_ever_valid`, `each_mutation_maps_to_expected_class`, `wrong_size_signature_rejected`, `wrong_size_vkey_rejected`, `unresolvable_input_is_fail_fast`, `unresolvable_collateral_input_is_fail_fast`, `conway_conservation_full`, `conservation_early_out_removed`, `adversarial_imbalanced_via_deposit`, `adversarial_imbalanced_via_withdrawal`, `adversarial_unknown_cert_tag_rejects_as_decode`, `adversarial_removed_tag_rejects_as_era_invalid`, `adversarial_truncated_withdrawals_rejects_as_decode`, `adversarial_state_dependent_unaccountable_rejects`, `adversarial_no_false_accept`, `adversarial_verdicts_replay_byte_identical`, `trailing_bytes_after_cert_array_rejected`, `huge_array_count_rejects_without_overallocating` |
| **CI** | `ci/ci_check_consensus_closed_enums.sh` |

Two guards on every LedgerView query: (a) Queried epoch != canonical.epoch_no ‚Üí return None (BLUE then fails closed via MissingConsensusInput). (b) Block slot outside [epoch_start_slot, epoch_end_slot] ‚Üí runner intercepts before admit and emits AdmissionHalted { reason: CrossEpochUse } (DC-ADMIT-11). No ambient default view; no cross-epoch silent use. |

### `DC-WAL-02`: WAL fingerprint-chain integrity: every WalEntry::AdmitBlock has prior_fp ==‚Ä¶

_tier: derived ¬∑ status: enforced_ ¬∑ _strengthened_in: PHASE4-N-M-A, PHASE4-N-Y, PHASE4-N-AE_

> **Strengthened in PHASE4-N-AE (AE.C, 2026-06-07).** The FIRST-ENTRY clause (`prior_fp == anchor's initial_ledger_fingerprint`) is now enforced on the LIVE recover‚Üífollow path. The CE-A5 live run found `node_lifecycle` seeding the follow `ForwardSyncState.prior_fp` with `Hash32([0u8;32])` (zero) instead of `fingerprint(&state.ledger).combined` ‚Äî so the first followed `AdmitBlock`'s `prior_fp` was 0, not the recovered ledger-tip `post_fp`, and a recover‚Üífollowed store failed warm-start (ChainBreak@1, exit 42). Fixed at BOTH lifecycle sites (forge-off + forge-on). The `verify_chain` authority was NOT loosened ‚Äî only the LIVE seed was corrected to feed it the right first `prior_fp`. **This strengthening closes the prior `_(no CI script ‚Äî gap)_`:** the new `ci_check_recover_follow_wal_lineage.sh` fences the live seed.

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | docs/planning/phase4-n-m-ledger-seed-invariants.md ¬ß1 (I-A5) |
| **Requirement** | WAL fingerprint-chain integrity: every WalEntry::AdmitBlock has prior_fp == previous entry's post_fp (or anchor's initial_ledger_fingerprint for the first entry). WalStore::verify_chain walks the WAL + asserts the chain holds. Verify failure is authority-fatal at the binary boundary. |
| **Code** | `crates/ade_ledger/src/wal/store_trait.rs`, `crates/ade_ledger/src/wal/replay.rs`. **PHASE4-N-AE.C live-seed fix:** `crates/ade_node/src/node_lifecycle.rs` (the recover‚Üífollow path seeds the follow `ForwardSyncState.prior_fp` from `fingerprint(&state.ledger).combined`, the recovered ledger-tip post_fp, at both the forge-off and forge-on lifecycle sites ‚Äî NOT zero). |
| **Tests** | `crates/ade_runtime/src/wal/file_wal_store.rs::tests::file_wal_store_verify_chain_passes_then_catches_break`, `crates/ade_ledger/src/wal/replay.rs::tests::replay_from_anchor_catches_chain_break`, `crates/ade_runtime/tests/wal_replay_from_anchor.rs::wal_replay_from_anchor_rejects_chain_break`. **PHASE4-N-AE.C (live recover‚Üífollow path):** `crates/ade_node/src/node_sync.rs::tests::recover_follow_zero_seed_chainbreaks` (reproduces the zero-seed ChainBreak@1), `crates/ade_node/src/node_sync.rs::tests::recover_follow_kill_warm_start_chains_from_ledger_fp` (proves the fix ‚Äî first followed `prior_fp` == recovered ledger-tip post_fp), `crates/ade_node/src/node_sync.rs::tests::recover_follow_two_runs_byte_identical`. (6 named; all resolve on disk.) |
| **CI** | `ci/ci_check_recover_follow_wal_lineage.sh` (PHASE4-N-AE.C ‚Äî NEW; fences the live recover‚Üífollow seed of the first `prior_fp` from the recovered ledger fingerprint, without loosening `verify_chain`). _Prior `_(no CI script ‚Äî gap)_` is now closed._ |

### `DC-WAL-04`: Forged-block WAL chain integrity + no-orphan recovery‚Ä¶

_tier: derived ¬∑ status: enforced_ ¬∑ _introduced_in: PHASE4-N-U_

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | `docs/planning/phase4-n-u-forged-block-durability-invariants.md` |
| **Requirement** | A forged `AdmitBlock` WAL entry's `prior_fp` MUST equal the current durable `post_fp` (the `BootstrapAnchor`'s `initial_ledger_fingerprint` for a genesis-successor block 0; the previous entry's `post_fp` otherwise). A forged block that would `ChainBreak` (`prior_fp` mismatch) is rejected fail-closed (authority-fatal). The WAL binds the EXACT canonical self-accepted bytes (no re-encode; I-10). Warm-start recovery reconciles durable block storage and the WAL tail so a torn forge-admit crash leaves no un-WAL'd forged orphan at or ahead of the durable tip. |
| **Code** | `crates/ade_ledger/src/wal/*` (`WalEntry::AdmitBlock` `prior_fp`/`post_fp` + `verify_chain` ‚Äî reused, no new variant); `crates/ade_node/src/node_sync.rs` (`admit_forged_block_durably ‚Üí pump_block` appends the forged `AdmitBlock` with `prior_fp = state.prior_fp`); `crates/ade_node/src/node_lifecycle.rs` (`warm_start_recovery` WAL-tail reconciliation: `rollback_to_slot(wal_tail_slot)` before warm-start) |
| **Tests** | `crates/ade_node/tests/forge_succeeds.rs`: `forged_admit_wal_prior_fp_chains` (the forged `AdmitBlock`'s `prior_fp` chains from the anchor `initial_ledger_fingerprint` and the forged WAL verifies from it). `crates/ade_node/src/node_lifecycle.rs`: `warm_start_drops_orphan_block_above_wal_tail` (no-orphan recovery ‚Äî a torn `StoreBlockBytes`-before-`AppendWal` crash leaves no un-WAL'd orphan at or ahead of the durable tip). (2 named; both resolve on disk.) |
| **CI** | `ci/ci_check_forged_durable_admit_via_pump.sh` (the S1 driver gate fences the chaining clause; the S2 no-orphan recovery clause is test-enforced via `warm_start_drops_orphan_block_above_wal_tail`) |

## CN ‚Äî Classification-Table Constraint-Network Invariants (`classification_table.md`)

Constraint-network invariants from the classification table ‚Äî closed wire grammars, surface-reduction chokepoints, single-authority constraints, and the closed-enum / closed-vocabulary fences that keep the attack surface bounded.

_119 rules._

### `CN-ADMIT-01`: Single admission-mode entry authority: exactly one pub fn in‚Ä¶

_tier: release ¬∑ status: enforced_

No second entry point; no per-call fallback. The runner composes N-M-A seed-import + bootstrap_anchor::mint + seed_to_snapshot + bootstrap_initial_state warm-start + N-L n2n_dialer + per-AdmittedBlock loop + WalStore::append + verdict::derive + admission_log emit. |

### `CN-CINPUT-01`: The seed-epoch consensus inputs (epoch, active-slots coefficient, total active‚Ä¶

_tier: constraint ¬∑ status: enforced_

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | docs/clusters/PHASE4-N-F-A/cluster.md; A1-seed-epoch-consensus-inputs-type.md |
| **Requirement** | The seed-epoch consensus inputs (epoch, active-slots coefficient, total active stake, and the per-pool active-stake + registered VRF keyhash distribution) persisted as Ade recovered state MUST be a single closed canonical type (SeedEpochConsensusInputs) with a SOLE encoder/decoder pair. The codec is deterministic CBOR, BTreeMap-ordered (no HashMap), version-gated (decode rejects any version != SEED_CINPUT_SCHEMA_VERSION fail-closed), and byte-canonical (a structurally valid but non-canonically-encoded buffer is rejected, not silently re-canonicalized). No second encoder/decoder for this type may exist. |

### `CN-CINPUT-02`: The SeedEpochConsensusInputs sidecar MUST be populated ONLY on the‚Ä¶

_tier: constraint ¬∑ status: enforced_

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | docs/clusters/PHASE4-N-F-A/cluster.md; A2-bootstrap-population-containment.md; A3a-wal-provenance-entry.md |
| **Requirement** | The SeedEpochConsensusInputs sidecar MUST be populated ONLY on the verified-bootstrap composition path (genesis_bootstrap / mithril_bootstrap), through the anchor-fp-keyed SnapshotStore surface (put_seed_epoch_consensus_inputs), built via the GREEN merge (merge_seed_epoch_consensus_inputs) and the A1 sole encoder. The forge-time consensus-inputs path (produce_mode / import_live_consensus_inputs / pool_distr_view_from_consensus_inputs / --consensus-inputs-path) MUST NOT build or put the sidecar, nor append its WAL provenance. Enforced by a data-flow-resistant containment gate (global call-site scan, not a bypassable RHS grep). This does NOT forbid diagnostic import of LiveConsensusInputsCanonical (fixtures / pinning tests / first-run verified-bootstrap extraction may still exist); it forbids that import from populating, proving, or substituting for the recovered sidecar on any bounty-primary path. NOTE: this rule constrains POPULATION + the forge-time fence only; it does NOT assert that the producer CONSUMES the recovered surface ‚Äî producer consumption is deferred to PHASE4-N-F-C and no registry rule is introduced for it in this close. |
| **Code** | `crates/ade_runtime/src/genesis_bootstrap.rs`; `crates/ade_runtime/src/mithril_bootstrap.rs`; `crates/ade_runtime/src/seed_consensus_merge.rs`; `crates/ade_runtime/src/seed_consensus_provenance.rs`; ci/ci_check_consensus_input_provenance.sh |
| **Tests** | `bootstrap_persists_anchor_keyed_seed_consensus_inputs`, `bootstrap_seed_inputs_merge_fails_closed_on_missing_vrf_or_stake`, `snapshot_store_keyed_sidecar_is_disjoint_from_slot_snapshots` |
| **CI** | `ci/ci_check_consensus_input_provenance.sh` |

### `CN-CINPUT-03`: Consume-side anti-laundering fence: on the node-lifecycle forge path the‚Ä¶

_tier: constraint ¬∑ status: enforced_

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | docs/clusters/PHASE4-N-F-C/cluster.md; L5-produce-from-recovered-state.md |
| **Requirement** | Consume-side anti-laundering fence: on the node-lifecycle forge path the leadership view MUST be projected from the recovered SeedEpochConsensusInputs surface (PoolDistrView::from_seed_epoch_consensus_inputs over the recovered BootstrapState) and MUST NOT be built from a forge-time operator bundle. No SeedEpochConsensusInputs value may be CONSTRUCTED on the production forge path (no shape-swap of an operator bundle into the recovered-surface type), and the forge-time consensus-input tokens (import_live_consensus_inputs / pool_distr_view_from_consensus_inputs / --consensus-inputs-path) MUST NOT appear in the node-sync/forge driver. Enforced by a data-flow-resistant containment gate (guard (d) of ci_check_consensus_input_provenance.sh: positive recovered- projection grep + negative bundle/cold-token grep + no-literal-construction fence over the comment/test-stripped run_node_sync/forge body), not a bypassable RHS grep. |
| **Code** | `crates/ade_node/src/node_sync.rs` (forge_one_from_recovered ‚Äî projects leadership only from the recovered BootstrapState); ci/ci_check_consensus_input_provenance.sh (guard (d) consume-side fence) |
| **Tests** | `forge_from_recovered_uses_recovered_pool_distr`, `forge_from_recovered_fails_closed_without_recovered_inputs` |
| **CI** | `ci/ci_check_consensus_input_provenance.sh` |

### `CN-CONS-01`: Chain selection must be deterministic for the same candidate chains and‚Ä¶

_tier: true ¬∑ status: enforced_ ¬∑ _strengthened_in: PHASE4-N-B, PHASE4-N-AI, PHASE4-N-AO_

> **Strengthened in PHASE4-N-AO (`strengthened_in += PHASE4-N-AO`).** The live multi-peer multi-candidate SELECT (CE-AO-6) is the LIVE analog of the arrival-order-independence proof ‚Äî the selected tip is independent of which peer's candidate arrives first (`DC-NODE-36`). The four-cell contract below is byte-unchanged; the strengthening is the live exercise, not a re-scope.
>
> **Flipped `partial` ‚Üí `enforced` in PHASE4-N-AI.** The prior pass carried `CN-CONS-01` as `partial` (determinism proven, but arrival-order-independence not separately gated). PHASE4-N-AI added two BLUE tests proving `select_best_chain` is INDEPENDENT of candidate arrival order ‚Äî `select_best_chain_arrival_order_independent_distinct_heights` (a permuted candidate set selects the same best chain by block-no) and `select_best_chain_arrival_order_independent_tiebreaker` (same under a full tiebreaker tie) ‚Äî plus a dedicated gate `ci_check_chain_selection_arrival_order_independent.sh`. With the arrival-order-independence cell now filled and CI-gated, the registry flips the rule to `enforced`. (Distinct from `CN-CONS-03` broad multi-node convergence, which stays `declared`.)

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | classification_table.md ¬ßD |
| **Requirement** | Chain selection must be deterministic for the same candidate chains and protocol observables ‚Äî same candidate set ‚Üí same selected best chain, INDEPENDENT of the order in which candidates arrive. |
