### `CN-CONS-03`: After temporary partition, honest nodes must converge using only‚Ä¶

_tier: derived ¬∑ status: enforced_ ¬∑ _strengthened_in: PHASE4-N-B, PHASE4-N-AI, PHASE4-N-AO_

> **FLIPPED `declared ‚Üí enforced` in PHASE4-N-AO (CE-AO-6).** Through PHASE4-N-AI this was the headline GAP ‚Äî the mechanism was wired (`DC-NODE-24` ‚Üí BLUE `select_best_chain`) but only the single-best-peer rollback-FOLLOW subset was exercised and the convergence witness was operator-gated / uncommitted. **PHASE4-N-AO closed it: the multi-candidate fork-choice SELECT cluster (S1‚ÄìS14) wired the full SELECT path live, and CE-AO-6 captured a NATURAL two-producer multi-candidate SELECT convergence pass.** 2026-06-13, `ade_node` @ `2a03ac73`, testnet-magic 42; both Haskell producers (cn1/cn2) live throughout, NO loser-freeze, NO post-fork operator intervention ‚Äî the SELECT decision is entirely Ade's. The replayable post-switch checker PASSED (`ci_check_post_switch_convergence_window.sh` invoking the `post_switch_continuity` reducer, `DC-EVIDENCE-05`): `ContinuesSelectedBranch`, terminal `AgreedAtSwitchTip{slot 391}` (exact agreement, our_hash==peer_hash), 25 admitted descendants chained, 0 diverged, every fork-choice win terminal. The flip rests on a REPLAYABLE verdict reducer + hermetic tests + a CI gate that re-derives the verdict from the transcript bytes ‚Äî NOT on an eyeballed transcript. **SCOPE (honest, NOT softened, NOT broadened):** proves convergence for the EXERCISED two-producer partition-and-reconverge venue (PHASE4-N-AO S1‚ÄìS14); NOT an unbounded multi-peer ChainSel claim; post-switch endless-flip-flop survival is out of scope. The CE-AO-6 transcript (`ao-CN-CONS-03-FLIP-natural-conv.jsonl`, sha256 `6713efe9‚Ä¶`) is preserved OUTSIDE the repo (competition-secrecy). A FREEZE-mode run (loser paused AFTER Ade's decision) is retained OUTSIDE the repo as a SELECT-independence diagnostic only, never as flip evidence.

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | classification_table.md ¬ßD |
| **Requirement** | After temporary partition, honest nodes must converge using only protocol-defined observables and declared emergency procedures ‚Äî Ade observes competing branches from multiple peers, SELECTS the best chain via BLUE `select_best_chain` over validated candidates, fetches+validates the winning branch's bodies, applies the fork-switch, and continues on the selected branch (or fails closed structurally), re-converging to the same tip the peers agree on. |
| **Code** | `crates/ade_core/src/consensus/fork_choice.rs` (`select_best_chain` ‚Äî the BLUE convergence primitive, the single live resolver target) driven by the full SELECT path: `crates/ade_node/src/candidate_aggregator.rs` (`build_candidate_fragment`, `DC-NODE-35`) + `crates/ade_node/src/lca_walk.rs` (`walk_to_durable_lca`, `DC-NODE-38`) + `crates/ade_node/src/fork_switch.rs` + `crates/ade_node/src/node_lifecycle.rs` (`dispatch_competing_fork_choice` + `apply_fork_switch` + `recover_missing_range`, `DC-NODE-36`/`37`/`39`/`41`) over the enforced `materialize_rolled_back_state` (`CN-STORE-07`) + lockstep reducer (`DC-CONS-20`) + `pump_block` (`DC-NODE-05`/`12`) authorities. |
| **Tests** | `higher_block_no_wins`, `equal_block_no_tiebreaker_decides`, `tiebreaker_loss_keeps_current` (the BLUE fork-choice ordering) + the full SELECT spine proven by `DC-NODE-34`‚Ä¶`41` / `DC-PUMP-04` / `DC-EVIDENCE-04`/`05` tests (e.g. `best_of_two_peers_wins_and_is_identified`, `multi_block_branch_walks_to_durable_lca`, `fork_switch_win_adopts_via_rolledback_then_chainselected`, `post_switch_continuity_replays_byte_identical`). The CE-AO-6 NATURAL two-producer convergence WITNESS is operator-produced + OUTSIDE-REPO (competition-secrecy); the replayable verdict that backs it is `DC-EVIDENCE-05`'s `post_switch_continuity` reducer + its 11 tests, all on disk. |
| **CI** | `ci/ci_check_no_density_in_fork_choice.sh` (the BLUE fork-choice ordering ‚Äî no density / operator heuristic in selection) + `ci/ci_check_post_switch_convergence_window.sh` (PHASE4-N-AO ‚Äî **the CE-AO-6 release gate**: invokes the `post_switch_continuity` reducer bin and enforces `ContinuesSelectedBranch` + a bounded post-switch window terminal of `agreement_verdict{agreed, our==peer}` at X-or-descendant OR a validated-prefix-of-peer, unbroken `prev_hash` lineage from X, 0 diverged, every win terminal). The full SELECT path is additionally fenced by the 12 PHASE4-N-AO gates (`ci_check_{peer_identity_preserved,candidate_construction_validated,live_selector_dispatch,fork_switch_never_abandons,lca_anchor_walk,wire_pump_fairness,fork_choice_evidence_closed,missing_bridge_fail_closed,rollback_retention_evidence,missing_bridge_refetch}.sh`). _Live convergence WITNESS (CE-AO-6) is operator-produced + OUTSIDE-REPO; the gate re-derives the verdict from the transcript bytes ‚Äî the mechanical contract is fully in CI._ |

### `CN-CONS-07`: Self-acceptance bridge + serve provenance ‚Äî every byte served traces to the single validated admit path (PHASE4-N-U: durable-provenance restatement)‚Ä¶

_tier: release ¬∑ status: enforced_ ¬∑ _introduced_in: PHASE4-N-C ¬∑ strengthened_in: PHASE4-N-G, PHASE4-N-H, PHASE4-N-F-G-B, PHASE4-N-U, PHASE4-N-AE_

> **Strengthened in PHASE4-N-AE (AE.B, 2026-06-07).** The serve-provenance clause is now exercised on the recover‚Üífollow‚Üíforge‚Üíserve spine that achieved live relay adoption (AE.E): the `--mode node` served view is the deterministic `ChainDbServedSource` projection of the durable ChainDb ‚Äî the live follow stores the followed lineage as a servable `StoredBlock` (so the forge parent is `FindIntersect`-able, `DC-NODE-14`), and a recover-only anchor with no servable successor is NEVER served as an intersectable head (fail-closed). No new serve path and no unvalidated bytes were introduced; serve remains a read-only projection of the single validated durable admit.

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | docs/planning/phase4-n-c-invariants.md ¬ß1 (NC-SELF-1); `docs/clusters/PHASE4-N-U/S3-serve-as-durable-chain-projection.md` (serve-provenance restatement); **PHASE4-N-AE:** `docs/clusters/PHASE4-N-AE/cluster.md` (serve-provenance on the recover‚Üífollow‚Üíforge spine) |
| **Requirement** | Self-acceptance bridge: a forged block is NOT eligible for RED broadcast unless Ade's own header validator (PHASE4-N-B path) and body validator (PHASE4-B1 path) accept it under the same slot, era, and context. Self-acceptance failure halts the producer deterministically; RED broadcast is gated on the BLUE self-accept verdict. SERVE PROVENANCE (no unvalidated bytes leave the node): every byte the node serves to a peer (ChainSync header advertisement / BlockFetch body) traces to the single validated admit path ‚Äî for `--mode node`, a deterministic PROJECTION of the durable ChainDb (whose sole production writers are `pump_block` / `DC-NODE-12` and the validated warm-start / genesis replay `bootstrap_initial_state`), covering BOTH forged (`self_accept`) and received (`admit_via_block_validity`) durable bytes through the one durable admit; for `--mode produce`, the `self_accept`'d `AcceptedBlock` served-chain index. **PHASE4-N-U restates the serve clause** from the in-memory-token dependency (N-G S2: served bytes must originate as a live `AcceptedBlock` token, lost on restart) to durable-provenance ‚Äî PRESERVING the TRUE invariant (no unvalidated bytes leave) while letting serve follow the durable chain (a follower fetches coherent history A‚ÜíB, never B without A; serve survives restart). See `DC-NODE-13`. |
| **Code** | `crates/ade_ledger/src/producer/self_accept.rs` (self_accept, AcceptedBlock, SelfAcceptError); `crates/ade_ledger/src/block_validity/transition.rs` (block_validity ‚Äî single closed validator authority self_accept wraps); `crates/ade_ledger/src/producer/served_chain.rs` (ServedChainSnapshot, served_chain_admit ‚Äî only AcceptedBlock values may enter the produce-mode served-chain index; PHASE4-N-G S2 strengthening preserves the broadcast gate across the network seam); `crates/ade_runtime/src/network/served_chain_projection.rs` (`ChainDbServedSource` ‚Äî PHASE4-N-U S3: the `--mode node` served view is a read-only projection of the durable ChainDb, whose sole production writers are `pump_block` + `bootstrap_initial_state`; serves `stored.bytes` verbatim, reuses the single `block_header_bytes` / DC-CONS-18 header authority); `crates/ade_runtime/src/network/serve_dispatch.rs` (`ServedChainSource` enum ‚Äî the single serve-dispatch authority reads either source; DC-NODE-07); `crates/ade_ledger/src/receive/admitted.rs` (AdmittedBlock, admit_via_block_validity ‚Äî PHASE4-N-H mirror; symmetric to AcceptedBlock); `crates/ade_ledger/src/receive/chain_write.rs` (ChainDbWrite trait takes AdmittedBlock by value) |
| **Tests** | `self_accept_accepts_freshly_forged_block`, `self_accept_rejects_corrupted_body_hash`, `self_accept_rejects_invalid_kes_signature`, `self_accept_rejects_unbalanced_tx_in_body`, `broadcast_callable_only_with_accept_verdict`, `served_chain_admit_admits_corpus_block`, `served_chain_admit_idempotent_on_byte_identity`, `served_chain_admit_independent_of_order`, `served_chain_snapshot_iteration_is_btreemap_ordered`, `served_chain_block_bytes_accessor_returns_accepted_block_slice`, `served_chain_range_bytes_returns_inclusive_window`, `served_chain_fingerprint_replay_byte_identical`, `admit_via_block_validity_accepts_corpus_block`, `admit_via_block_validity_rejects_corrupted_body`, `receive_apply_block_delivered_with_matching_header_admits`. (Serve-clause coverage is carried by the `DC-NODE-13` projection tests: `served_view_projects_durable_chain`, `follower_fetches_coherent_history_incl_ingested_predecessor`, `served_view_retires_accumulator`.) |
| **CI** | `ci/ci_check_self_accept_gate.sh`, `ci/ci_check_served_chain_closure.sh`, `ci/ci_check_admitted_block_closure.sh`, `ci/ci_check_receive_reducer_closure.sh`. (PHASE4-N-U serve-clause mechanics are fenced by `ci/ci_check_served_chain_projection.sh` via `DC-NODE-13`.) |

### `CN-FORGE-01`: The producer-mode forge handler is a closed transition from‚Ä¶

_tier: derived ¬∑ status: enforced_

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | docs/planning/phase4-n-r-invariants.md ¬ß1 (I1, I9); ¬ß2 (N1); ¬ß5 (state transitions) |
| **Requirement** | The producer-mode forge handler is a closed transition from CoordinatorEvent::RequestForge { slot, kes_period, ledger_snapshot_ref, chain_tip } to exactly one of three ForgeResult variants: ForgeSucceeded { slot, artifact } where artifact.bytes decodes via Ade's BLUE block decoder AND self_accept(artifact, chain_tip, ledger_snapshot) returns Accepted; ForgeNotLeader { slot, vrf_output_fingerprint }; or ForgeFailed { slot, structured_error }. No other outcome is permitted. ForgeSucceeded MUST NOT be emitted if self_accept rejects the artifact ‚Äî the handler emits ForgeFailed { SelfAcceptRejected } instead. Empty-block forging is the explicit scope; mempool integration is out of scope for the rule's enforcement evidence. |
| **Code** | `crates/ade_node/src/produce_mode.rs` (run_real_forge BLUE-then-RED-then-BLUE pipeline; apply_effects_with_forge_handler call site); `crates/ade_ledger/src/producer/forge.rs` (forge_block BLUE step 5); `crates/ade_ledger/src/producer/self_accept.rs` (self_accept BLUE step 6 gate) |
| **Tests** | `zero_stake_answer_emits_forge_not_leader`, `kes_period_outside_window_emits_forge_failed_kes_period_mismatch`, `full_stake_answer_reaches_self_accept_and_rejects`, `run_real_forge_is_byte_identical_across_two_runs`, `forge_block_accepts_empty_mempool`, `forge_block_empty_mempool_produces_empty_body`, `produce_mode_starts_runs_three_slots_and_exits_via_max_slots`, `forge_to_self_accept_succeeds` |
| **CI** | `ci/ci_check_producer_coordinator_no_secrets.sh`, `ci/ci_check_no_independent_forge_codepath.sh` |

### `CN-FORGE-02`: Leader-check splits across the RED/BLUE color boundary: RED produces a VRF‚Ä¶

_tier: derived ¬∑ status: enforced_

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | docs/planning/phase4-n-r-invariants.md ¬ß1 (I2); ¬ß2 (N12); ¬ß3 (D1); ¬ß4 (R3) |
| **Requirement** | Leader-check splits across the RED/BLUE color boundary: RED produces a VRF proof/output for the slot using the operator's VRF signing key; BLUE verifies the proof and evaluates leader eligibility from canonical inputs only (slot, eta0, stake_distribution, leader_threshold, vrf_vk, vrf_proof_or_output, LeaderScheduleAnswer). BLUE never sees the VRF / KES / cold signing keys. The BLUE evaluator (`verify_and_evaluate_leader`) lives at `ade_core::consensus::leader_check` and has no dependency on LedgerView, EraSchedule, ChainDepState, wall-clock, storage, or RED crates. Caller derives LeaderScheduleAnswer via the authority path (query_leader_schedule) and passes it in. The closed two-variant LeaderCheckVerdict (Eligible carries forge-capable material; NotEligible carries only bounded vrf_output_fingerprint evidence) makes illegal observation of forge-capable material structurally impossible. |
| **Code** | `crates/ade_core/src/consensus/leader_check.rs` (verify_and_evaluate_leader + LeaderCheckVerdict + LeaderCheckError); `crates/ade_node/src/produce_mode.rs` (run_real_forge composition ‚Äî RED vrf_prove ‚Üí BLUE verify_and_evaluate_leader ‚Üí RED kes_sign_at) |
| **Tests** | `eligible_on_threshold_with_high_stake_emits_eligible_verdict`, `not_eligible_with_zero_stake_emits_not_eligible_verdict`, `malformed_proof_emits_verification_failed`, `wrong_vk_emits_verification_failed`, `answer_slot_mismatch_emits_structured_error`, `vrf_input_mismatch_emits_structured_error`, `zero_stake_denominator_emits_structured_error`, `verdict_is_byte_identical_across_two_runs`, `vrf_output_fingerprint_is_first_8_bytes_of_output`, `zero_stake_answer_emits_forge_not_leader` |
| **CI** | `ci/ci_check_leader_check_authority.sh` |

### `CN-FORGE-03`: Producer/validator codec symmetry: forge_block emits the era-tagged [era‚Ä¶

_tier: derived ¬∑ status: enforced_

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | docs/planning/phase4-n-v-invariants.md; docs/clusters/PHASE4-N-V/cluster.md ¬ß1 |
| **Requirement** | Producer/validator codec symmetry: forge_block emits the era-tagged [era, block] envelope (era = Conway discriminant 7) via the single canonical ade_codec::encode_block_envelope (symmetric to decode_block_envelope), so forge_block output round-trips through the SAME decode_block authority that validates received blocks. decode_block(forge_block(tick).bytes) is Ok and yields a DecodedBlock whose header-body fields and four preserved body-bucket bytes equal what was forged. A bare-block (no-envelope) forge output, or any forge<->decode asymmetry, is CI-gated impossible. Root cause (PHASE4-N-T): forge_block emitted a bare array(5) block, so decode_block_envelope rejected EVERY forged block at offset 0 (BlockValidityError::Body(Decoding(InvalidStructure))) before any header/KES/leader/self_accept logic. |
| **Code** | `crates/ade_codec/src/cbor/envelope.rs` (encode_block_envelope, NEW); `crates/ade_ledger/src/producer/forge.rs` (forge_block wraps output via the encoder) |
| **Tests** | `encode_decode_block_envelope_round_trips`, `conway_envelope_head_is_82_07`, `encode_block_envelope_reencodes_corpus_block_identically`, `forge_block_output_decodes_via_decode_block` |
| **CI** | `ci/ci_check_forge_decode_round_trip.sh` |

For Conway/Praos the producer alpha MUST equal the validator alpha (praos_vrf_input(slot, eta0) = blake2b256(slot\|\|eta0) + vrfLeaderValue range-extension), NOT the TPraos role-tagged alpha (slot\|\|eta0\|\|0x4C). No verification/construction fallback may accept both TPraos and Praos VRF inputs ‚Äî for a given era/protocol version there is exactly one VRF transcript authority. |

### `CN-GENESIS-01`: The Shelley genesis closed-contract parser accepts a real cardano-cli‚Ä¶

_tier: derived ¬∑ status: enforced_

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | docs/planning/phase4-n-r-invariants.md ¬ß1 (I7); ¬ß2 (N7); ¬ß3 (D5); N-R-A A1 OQ7 fixtures |
| **Requirement** | The Shelley genesis closed-contract parser accepts a real cardano-cli `shelley-genesis.json` and produces a canonical `GenesisAnchor`. Required fields (networkMagic, systemStart, slotLength, slotsPerKESPeriod, maxKESEvolutions) fail-closed on missing / malformed / wrong-type input. No implicit defaults (e.g., 'if missing, assume preprod' rejected). No stringly fallback (e.g., `\"1\"` rejected for u32 fields). Extra unknown keys accepted-and-ignored for forward compatibility, iff they do not alter interpretation ‚Äî the `GenesisAnchor` produced from an extra-key fixture MUST byte-equal the canonical fixture's `GenesisAnchor`. The kes_anchor_slot is operator-supplied (not in genesis) and passed to the parser as a separate argument. systemStart parsing uses a deterministic ISO 8601 ‚Üí Unix epoch milliseconds conversion (Howard Hinnant proleptic Gregorian). |
| **Code** | `crates/ade_runtime/src/producer/genesis_parser.rs` (parse_shelley_genesis + closed GenesisParseError enum + parse_iso8601_to_unix_ms + days_since_unix_epoch) |
| **Tests** | `accepted_shelley_genesis_parses_to_expected_anchor`, `missing_required_field_emits_structured_error`, `stringly_int_emits_malformed_field_type`, `extra_inert_keys_produce_byte_identical_anchor`, `malformed_numeric_negative_slot_length_rejected`, `iso8601_parse_anchors_to_known_unix_ms_values` |
| **CI** | `ci/ci_check_node_forge_real_cli_ingress.sh`, `ci/ci_check_genesis_consistency_fixture_present.sh` |

> **Strengthened in PHASE4-N-F-G-A.** S2 / S1 ‚Äî the real `shelley-genesis.json` closed-contract parser (`parse_shelley_genesis`) is now the ingress on the `--mode node` operator-forge path, and the S1 genesis-consistency pinning harness drives the REAL `bootstrap_initial_state` warm-start against the committed private-net Ade-as-leader reference fixture. Backed by `ci/ci_check_node_forge_real_cli_ingress.sh` (CE-G-A-2) and `ci/ci_check_genesis_consistency_fixture_present.sh` (CE-G-A-1).

### `CN-KES-HEADER-01`: The KES signature in a forged block's header is over the canonical‚Ä¶

_tier: derived ¬∑ status: enforced_

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | docs/planning/phase4-n-s-invariants.md ¬ß1 (I1, I2); ¬ß2 (N1, N2) |
| **Requirement** | The KES signature in a forged block's header is over the canonical unsigned-header CBOR pre-image ‚Äî the CBOR encoding of ShelleyHeaderBody (the first element of the outer [header_body, kes_signature] header array). The producer-side recipe (unsigned_header_pre_image) and the validator-side extractor (header_input::decode_block.header_input.kes.header_body_bytes) produce byte-identical output for every corpus block. The branded UnsignedHeaderPreImage(Vec<u8>) type's only constructor is the canonical recipe; kes_sign_header accepts only this type ‚Äî arbitrary-byte signing is mechanically unrepresentable. |
| **Code** | `crates/ade_ledger/src/block_validity/unsigned_header_pre_image.rs` (UnsignedHeaderPreImage branded type + canonical recipe); `crates/ade_runtime/src/producer/producer_shell.rs` (ProducerShell::kes_sign_header accepts only the branded type); `crates/ade_node/src/produce_mode.rs` (run_real_forge two-pass bridge replaces the placeholder) |
| **Tests** | `unsigned_header_preimage_matches_decode_block_extraction_for_corpus`, `recipe_output_is_byte_identical_across_two_runs`, `shell_kes_sign_header_produces_verifiable_signature` |
| **CI** | `ci/ci_check_unsigned_header_preimage_single_source.sh` |

> **Strengthened in PHASE4-N-AC (`strengthened_in += "PHASE4-N-AC"`).** The KES-signs-the-real-unsigned-header-pre-image invariant now ALSO holds across KES periods, not only the minted period-0. Before N-AC the forge's single real KES sign signed the canonical pre-image only when the key was already at the requested period; once the chain aged past one KES period the minted-at-period-0 key could not sign (`KesPeriodNotCurrent`). `DC-CRYPTO-10` adds `kes_sign_header_advancing` (evolve the key forward to the requested period, then sign) so the signed pre-image is at the EVOLVED current period ‚Äî the real-pre-image KES sign now works across KES periods. This rule's own four-cell contract (Code / Tests / CI above) is unchanged; the strengthening is the cross-period extension of the same single-source pre-image authority, not a re-scope.

### `CN-NODE-03`: Operator-key ingress + forge-on flip for --mode node. Ingress constructs an‚Ä¶

_tier: constraint_network ¬∑ status: enforced_

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | docs/planning/phase4-n-f-f-invariants.md |
| **Requirement** | Operator-key ingress + forge-on flip for --mode node. Ingress constructs an operator-material-backed ForgeActivation STRICTLY through RED-parse -> BLUE-structural-validator -> canonical-type, reusing the existing KES / VRF / cold / opcert loaders (KES via ade_crypto::kes_sum::Sum6Kes::raw_deserialize_signing_key_kes; VRF/cold via the cardano-cli text-envelope loaders; opcert via the opcert parser). NO new BLUE authority, NO parser reimplementation, NO plugin/trait seam, NO second forge codepath, NO new BLUE crate change. Key custody stays RED-confined to ProducerShell: passing ProducerShell to the fenced forge handoff (forge_one_from_recovered) is allowed, but copying or extracting its private material into the GREEN coordinator state, the planner, any node/loop state, or any persisted / logged / hashed-for-evidence / replay surface is forbidden. Tests and debug output MUST NOT print, snapshot, serialize, hash-for-evidence, or compare private key bytes (assertions may compare public identifiers, structured outcomes, and forged artifacts only where already produced by the fenced forge path). Forge intent is a pure total function of CLI key-flag presence: the COMPLETE required operator set { cold skey, KES skey, VRF skey, opcert, genesis file } present => Some(activation) (forge on); all absent => None (byte-identical N-F-D relay); any partial subset => structured fail-closed error (never a silent relay fallback, never a missing / zero / fabricated key). pool_id is either added to the required set or derived in one named place -- never fabricated. The forge base is the SAME recovered/bootstrap BootstrapState that seeds the relay spine, obtained via the single bootstrap_initial_state / warm-start authority (no second bootstrap, no second recovered state); the recovered state outlives both ForwardSyncState and ForgeActivation. The forge remains subordinate + self-accept-only: the existing N-F-E containment gate stays SEMANTICALLY UNCHANGED (still exactly one fenced forge_one_from_recovered call, no run_real_forge, no serve / admit / gossip / broadcast / block-fetch / durable-tip mutation); N-F-F may ADD key-ingress gates but MUST NOT relax forge containment. N-F-F makes the binary forge-CAPABLE once paired with a live/continuing feed; it does NOT itself make forge observable on the current empty-source binary path (plan_loop_step halts cleanly on LoopState::Ending even when a slot is Due) and makes NO live forge / serve / gossip / peer-acceptance / BA-02 / RO-LIVE / durable tip-advance claim -- observable forge is the RO-LIVE-01 follow-on. pparams / protocol_version reuse the existing produce-path honest-scope defaults (ProtocolParameters::default + default protocol_version): this is ingress / activation wiring, NOT mainnet-complete ledger-valid block-production fidelity. |
| **Code** | `crates/ade_node/src/forge_intent.rs` (GREEN tri-state classifier); `crates/ade_node/src/operator_forge.rs` (RED ingress + activation assembly); `crates/ade_node/src/node_lifecycle.rs` (Some/None binary flip + ForgeKeyIngress) |
| **Tests** | `classify_forge_intent_total_over_all_32_flag_combinations`, `classify_forge_intent_none_present_is_off`, `forge_intent_error_carries_no_path_bytes`, `load_operator_producer_shell_builds_shell_from_complete_material`, `load_operator_producer_shell_kes_period_past_opcert_fails_closed`, `operator_forge_error_carries_no_path_or_key_bytes`, `build_operator_forge_material_from_complete_material`, `node_mode_with_operator_keys_warm_start_forge_capable_halts_clean`, `node_mode_partial_operator_keys_fail_closed`, `relay_loop_with_operator_material_forge_reaches_fenced_path`, `relay_loop_with_operator_material_two_runs_byte_identical` |
| **CI** | `ci/ci_check_forge_intent_closed.sh`, `ci/ci_check_operator_forge_no_secret_leak.sh`, `ci/ci_check_node_run_loop_containment.sh` |

### `CN-NODE-04`: `--mode node` emits a CLOSED, allow-listed feed/forge scheduling diagnostic event vocabulary‚Ä¶

_tier: operational ¬∑ status: enforced_ ¬∑ _introduced_in: PHASE4-N-F-G-J ¬∑ strengthened_in: PHASE4-N-AH_

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | `docs/planning/phase4-n-f-g-j-invariants.md`; cluster docs `docs/clusters/PHASE4-N-F-G-J/` (`cluster.md`, `S1-feed-forge-events-taxonomy.md`) |
| **Requirement** | `--mode node` emits a CLOSED, allow-listed diagnostic event vocabulary for feed/forge scheduling: `feed_unavailable{reason}` (closed reason enum), `forge_tick_considered`, `forge_tick_skipped{closed reason}`, `forge_attempted`, `forge_result{closed outcome}`. Closed reason/outcome enums only ‚Äî no stringly-typed authoritative errors, no catch-all / `Other` variant (a new variant is a compile error at the exhaustive JSONL encoder and fails the allow-list closedness test until wired + allow-listed). The S1-producible closed reason set is exactly three: `NoBlockAvailable` (WirePump open but momentarily empty) and `CleanEmpty` (an InMemory feed's provably-clean deterministic drain) are forge-eligible; `UnknownDisconnected` (a reason-less / ambiguous WirePump disconnect) is INELIGIBLE (fail-closed-on-ambiguity). The richer error reasons (`PeerLost` \| `DecodeError` \| `ProtocolError` \| `SourceInvalid`) + a reason-enriched live `AtTip` are a FUTURE wire-pump-enrichment prerequisite, NOT yet in the closed set. The events are operational/diagnostic ONLY: never a consensus-evidence, acceptance, or BA-02 signal; emitting them changes no forge scheduling, base, or authority. The events are emit-only, one-directional (planner ‚Üí log): the planner may EMIT but MUST NOT consume them. Only the forge-eligible reasons (`NoBlockAvailable` \| `CleanEmpty`) may be eligible for the `DC-NODE-08` forge allowance. |
| **Code** | `crates/ade_node/src/live_log/sched_event.rs` (the closed `SchedEvent` / closed reason + outcome enums + the exhaustive JSONL encoder ‚Äî a new variant is a compile error here); `crates/ade_node/src/live_log/sched_writer.rs` (emit-only JSONL writer ‚Äî append-only, never read back); `crates/ade_node/src/node_sync.rs` + `crates/ade_node/src/node_lifecycle.rs` (the planner EMIT sites ‚Äî one-directional, never a consume) |
| **Tests** | `node_sched_events_emit_closed_vocabulary` (`crates/ade_node/src/node_sync.rs` ‚Äî the planner emits the closed feed/forge sched events through the writer), `node_sched_event_allowlist_rejects_unknown_variants` (`crates/ade_node/src/live_log/sched_event.rs` ‚Äî the allow-list closedness test: an unknown variant string is rejected, pinning the closed enum) |
| **CI** | `ci/ci_check_node_sched_events_emit_only.sh` (S1, NEW ‚Äî the sched-event vocabulary is closed (no catch-all / `Other`) AND emit-only: the writer is append-only and the planner has no read/consume of the event log) |

### `CN-PEER-OUTBOUND-MAP-01`: Per-peer outbound senders are owned by an Arc<RwLock<BTreeMap<PeerId‚Ä¶

_tier: derived ¬∑ status: enforced_

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | docs/planning/phase4-n-s-invariants.md ¬ß1 (I5); ¬ß2 (N5) |
| **Requirement** | Per-peer outbound senders are owned by an Arc<RwLock<BTreeMap<PeerId, mpsc::Sender<OutboundCommand>>>>. Listener (run_per_peer_session) inserts on PeerConnected; MuxPump removes on emit_peer_disconnected. produce_mode looks up by PeerId and cannot fabricate senders. BTreeMap (not HashMap) for deterministic iteration order. Lookup failure is structured: DispatchError::{UnknownPeer, PeerOutboundMissing}. No cross-peer byte leakage is structurally possible ‚Äî bytes destined for PeerId(a) reach the MuxPump task owning PeerId(a)'s TCP socket, never another peer's. |

### `CN-PROD-02`: Producer slot loop never signs a block whose KES period has rotated past‚Ä¶

_tier: derived ¬∑ status: enforced_

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | docs/planning/phase4-n-q-invariants.md ¬ß1 (I3, I4, I7, I8); ¬ß2 (N4, N5, N8, N9); ¬ß5 |
| **Requirement** | Producer slot loop never signs a block whose KES period has rotated past current_period. Slot ‚Üí KES period is a pure function of (slot, genesis_kes_anchor, slots_per_kes_period); the coordinator fail-closes (slot_missed event + log) when wall-clock has advanced past the target slot before forge completes. No retroactive forge. The GREEN coordinator never owns or stores private signing material ‚Äî it emits a closed `RequestForge { slot, kes_period, ledger_snapshot_ref, chain_tip }` effect; the RED producer shell either returns an `AcceptedBlock` via a `ForgeSucceeded` event or a structured `ForgeFailed { slot, structured_error }` event. KesSecret / VrfSigningKey / ColdSigningKey never enter CoordinatorState. T-tier key-custody boundary. |
| **Code** | `crates/ade_runtime/src/producer/coordinator.rs` (GREEN ‚Äî CoordinatorState has no secret fields; type system prevents); `crates/ade_runtime/src/producer/producer_shell.rs` (RED ‚Äî sole key-custody surface; ProducerShell::init enforces KES period bounds vs opcert); `crates/ade_node/src/produce_mode.rs` (RED driver; PHASE4-N-R-A A3 wired the real run_real_forge composition; stub replaced); `crates/ade_runtime/src/producer/opcert_envelope.rs` (PHASE4-N-R-C C1 opcert parser); `crates/ade_runtime/src/producer/genesis_parser.rs` (PHASE4-N-R-C C2 genesis parser) |
| **Tests** | `init_emits_started_event_and_zero_other_effects`, `slot_tick_emits_request_forge_and_log`, `forge_succeeded_emits_broadcast_and_log`, `forge_not_leader_emits_log_and_clears_pending`, `forge_failed_emits_slot_missed_with_mapped_reason`, `stale_forge_result_after_new_tick_drops_with_slot_missed`, `kes_period_out_of_range_errors`, `shell_init_rejects_malformed_opcert_hot_vkey_length`, `shell_init_rejects_kes_period_below_opcert_start`, `shell_kes_sign_at_current_period_succeeds_and_verifies`, `shell_kes_sign_at_wrong_period_errors`, `shell_kes_advance_to_evolves_key_one_way`, `shell_debug_redacts_secret_fields`, `zero_stake_answer_emits_forge_not_leader`, `kes_period_outside_window_emits_forge_failed_kes_period_mismatch`, `full_stake_answer_reaches_self_accept_and_rejects` |

### `CN-PROD-04`: Every CoordinatorEffect::BroadcastBlock reconstructs the AcceptedBlock from‚Ä¶

| Aspect | Location |

_tier: release ¬∑ status: enforced_ ¬∑ _strengthened_in: PHASE4-N-F-G-J (S5 genesis-successor rehearsal coverage)_

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | `docs/planning/phase4-n-f-g-d-invariants.md`; cluster docs `docs/clusters/PHASE4-N-F-G-D/` (`cluster.md`, `S1-path-fidelity-proof-fence.md`, `S2-rehearsal-evidence-surface-gate.md`, `S3-c1-dry-run-runbook-operator-scaffold.md`, `S4-rehearsal-leak-gate-archived-home-hardening.md`); **G-J strengthening:** `docs/clusters/PHASE4-N-F-G-J/S5-c1-genesis-rehearsal.md` (the rehearsal harness now covers the genesis-successor cold-start path) |
| **Requirement** | Private-testnet accepted-block bounty dry-run fidelity (two coupled clauses; if either fails the rehearsal becomes misleading). (1) PATH FIDELITY: the C1 private dry-run uses the SAME --mode node accepted-block path as preview/preprod -- N-M-C extraction/import (import_live_consensus_inputs) -> forge -> self-accept -> sibling-serve -> block-fetch -> peer log -> correlate -- with NO private-only flag, branch, bootstrap authority, or from-genesis constructor. The only differences from the preprod pass are operator-controlled inputs (a private genesis whose stake allocation makes Ade win slots fast) and the evidence label (rehearsal). No private-only helper may make the rehearsal pass if the same condition would fail on preview/preprod -- such a condition is a shared-path bug to fix in the shared path, never special-cased. (2) EVIDENCE NON-PROMOTABILITY: any private-testnet manifest is clearly marked rehearsal / private-testnet, stored ONLY under the rehearsal home (docs/evidence/phase4-n-f-g-d-private-rehearsal-*.toml, never the bounty home docs/clusters/PHASE4-N-F-G-C/CE-G-C-LIVE_*.toml), sha256-bound to a real Haskell peer log, correlate-produced (ba02_evidence::correlate is the sole acceptance-evidence constructor; allow-list, hash-primary), and flips NO RO-LIVE rule. C1 rehearsal evidence may increase confidence in the bounty path, but it is NOT bounty evidence and MUST NOT be referenced by the CE-G-C-LIVE_* / ci_check_ba02_evidence_manifest_schema.sh gate. The single bounty deliverable is preview/preprod acceptance, captured separately. |
| **Code** | `crates/ade_node/src/rehearsal_evidence.rs` (GREEN ‚Äî `PrivateRehearsalManifest` WRAPS a `correlate`-produced `Ba02Manifest` in a structurally distinct, non-promotable envelope; sole ctor `from_correlate_outcome` returns `None` on `NoEvidence`; `to_canonical_toml` always emits `is_rehearsal = true` + `not_bounty_evidence = true` as literals ‚Äî the type cannot represent a non-rehearsal; closed 1-variant `RehearsalVenue::PrivateTestnetC1`); `crates/ade_node/src/rehearsal_pass.rs` (RED I/O ‚Äî `correlate_peer_log_file_into_rehearsal` reuses `ba02_pass::correlate_peer_log_file` verbatim, no alternate correlator; `write_private_rehearsal_manifest` accepts ONLY a `PrivateRehearsalManifest`); `crates/ade_node/src/ba02_evidence.rs` (`correlate` ‚Äî reused, the sole acceptance-evidence constructor; allow-list, hash-primary); `crates/ade_runtime/src/consensus_inputs/canonical.rs` (`import_live_consensus_inputs` / `import_live_consensus_inputs_from_bytes` ‚Äî the shared N-M-C extraction/import the S1 path-fidelity fence pins; venue-agnostic) |
| **Tests** | `node_accepted_block_consensus_inputs_via_shared_import` (`crates/ade_node/tests/node_path_fidelity.rs` ‚Äî clause 1: an epoch-0-shaped private bundle AND a synced-preprod-tip bundle both lift through the single shared importer with no venue branch), `rehearsal_envelope_wraps_correlate_produced_payload`, `rehearsal_correlate_no_evidence_writes_nothing`, `rehearsal_envelope_is_structurally_distinct_from_ba02_manifest` (the 3 `rehearsal_*` unit tests in `crates/ade_node/src/rehearsal_pass.rs` ‚Äî clause 2: the wrap, the `NoEvidence`‚Üínothing-written, and the structural distinctness from `Ba02Manifest`), `c1_dry_run_correlate_to_rehearsal_envelope`, `node_c1_dry_run_rehearsal_live` (`crates/ade_node/tests/node_c1_dry_run_rehearsal.rs` ‚Äî hermetic correlate‚Üírehearsal-envelope‚Üíwrite‚Üíread-back; plus the env-gated `ADE_LIVE_C1_DRY_RUN` operator harness, skipped in CI), `rehearsal_gate_fails_on_archived_home_leak` (`crates/ade_node/tests/rehearsal_gate_archived_home.rs` ‚Äî S4 regression: a rehearsal-marked `.toml` under the ARCHIVED bounty home FAILS the leak gate); **G-J S5 (genesis-successor coverage):** `genesis_rehearsal_manifest_binds_block_zero_genesis`, `genesis_rehearsal_no_evidence_writes_nothing` (`crates/ade_node/tests/forge_succeeds.rs` ‚Äî the genesis-rehearsal manifest binds the self-accepting block 0 + `Genesis` cold-start fixture; `NoEvidence`‚Üínothing-written), `node_c1_genesis_rehearsal_live` (`crates/ade_node/tests/node_c1_genesis_rehearsal.rs` ‚Äî env-gated genesis-successor live arm, skipped in CI) |

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | docs/clusters/PHASE4-N-M-FRAG/cluster.md ¬ß1 |
| **Requirement** | Session reducer per-mini-protocol payload reassembly: the GREEN session reducer maintains one accumulating Vec<u8> buffer per AcceptedMiniProtocol variant inside `ConnectedState`, and emits exactly one `SessionEffect::DeliverPeerFrame` per COMPLETE CBOR item observed in the wire stream ‚Äî never per mux frame. Same canonical inbound byte stream ‚Üí byte-identical `DeliverPeerFrame` sequence across runs. The per-protocol buffer is a CLOSED-sum- indexed struct (no HashMap), so iteration / membership / lookup are deterministic. |
| **Code** | `crates/ade_network/src/session/state.rs` (ProtoBuffers + ConnectedState.proto_buffers field), `crates/ade_network/src/session/core.rs` (drain_connected_frames + drain_protocol_items) |
| **Tests** | `crates/ade_network/src/session/core.rs::tests::fragmented_chain_sync_message_assembles_one_deliver`, `crates/ade_network/src/session/core.rs::tests::fragmented_block_fetch_block_assembles_one_deliver`, `crates/ade_network/src/session/core.rs::tests::interleaved_chain_sync_and_block_fetch_fragments_stay_isolated`, `crates/ade_network/src/session/core.rs::tests::pipelined_two_chain_sync_messages_in_one_mux_frame_emit_two_delivers`, `crates/ade_network/src/session/core.rs::tests::truncated_then_complete_two_step_drain`, `crates/ade_network/src/session/core.rs::tests::proto_buffers_isolation_across_accepted_protocols` |
| **CI** | `ci/ci_check_session_proto_reassembly.sh` |

_PHASE4-N-AB strengthening (`strengthened_in += "PHASE4-N-AB"`): the inbound reassembler now has a symmetric **outbound** segmenter (`CN-SESS-05`). Before N-AB, Ade could REASSEMBLE inbound multi-frame payloads (Conway blocks above the 65535-byte mux SDU limit) but could not SEGMENT its own outbound payloads the same way ‚Äî `handle_outbound` + `encode_inner_frame` errored above `MAX_PAYLOAD`. `CN-SESS-05` closes the receive+send asymmetry; this rule's own four-cell contract (Code / Tests / CI above) is unchanged._

### `CN-SESS-05`: Outbound mini-protocol payload segmentation ‚Äî the GREEN session reducer SEGMENTS an outbound payload larger than MAX_PAYLOAD into ordered, byte-preserving mux frames (the outbound inverse of CN-SESS-04 inbound reassembly)

_tier: derived ¬∑ status: enforced_ ¬∑ _introduced_in: PHASE4-N-AB_

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | `docs/clusters/PHASE4-N-AB/cluster.md ¬ß1` (archived to `docs/clusters/completed/PHASE4-N-AB/cluster.md` at close); `project_pre_rolive_hardening_queue.md` item 2 |
| **Requirement** | Outbound mini-protocol payloads larger than `MAX_PAYLOAD` are SEGMENTED into ordered mux frames, each no larger than `MAX_PAYLOAD`, preserving mini-protocol id, mode, and byte order. Concatenating segment payloads reconstructs the original payload exactly (lossless, byte-preserving). Payloads above `MAX_OUTBOUND_PAYLOAD_BYTES` (= 16 MiB, a fixed, non-configurable GREEN constant ‚Äî symmetric with the inbound `MAX_REASSEMBLY_TAIL_BYTES` / `DC-LIVEMEM-01`) fail closed (`SessionError::OutboundPayloadTooLarge`). Segmentation uses the SINGLE existing single-frame encoder authority (`encode_inner_frame` ‚Üí `mux::frame::encode_frame`) ‚Äî no second/alternate frame encoder ‚Äî and is the outbound inverse of `CN-SESS-04` inbound reassembly. One captured timestamp is reused across a message's segments (GREEN ‚Äî no per-segment clock). An empty payload still emits exactly one (empty) frame. |
| **Code** | `crates/ade_network/src/session/core.rs` (`handle_outbound` owns segmentation: above the `MAX_OUTBOUND_PAYLOAD_BYTES` fail-closed guard, splits `MAX_PAYLOAD < len <= MAX_OUTBOUND_PAYLOAD_BYTES` into ordered `<= MAX_PAYLOAD` frames via `payload.chunks(MAX_PAYLOAD)` ‚Üí `encode_inner_frame`, reusing one captured `timestamp`, concatenated into one `SessionEffect::SendBytes`; `encode_inner_frame` stays the single-frame encoder authority with its `MAX_PAYLOAD` per-frame guard; `MAX_OUTBOUND_PAYLOAD_BYTES` = 16 MiB fixed constant); `crates/ade_network/src/mux/frame.rs` (`MAX_PAYLOAD` = `u16::MAX` = 65535 ‚Äî the per-frame ceiling the encoder enforces) |
| **Tests** | `crates/ade_network/src/session/core.rs::tests::outbound_payload_at_max_payload_is_one_frame` ‚Äî a payload at exactly `MAX_PAYLOAD` emits one frame (no spurious split); `‚Ä¶::outbound_payload_over_max_payload_segments_into_two` ‚Äî a payload just over `MAX_PAYLOAD` segments into two ordered frames; `‚Ä¶::outbound_segment_order_preserved` ‚Äî segment byte order is preserved; `‚Ä¶::outbound_segments_keep_same_mini_protocol_id_and_mode` ‚Äî every segment carries the same mini-protocol id + mode; `‚Ä¶::outbound_large_payload_reassembles_byte_identical_via_inbound` ‚Äî the inverse round-trip: outbound segments fed back through `CN-SESS-04` inbound reassembly reconstruct the original payload byte-identically; `‚Ä¶::outbound_payload_at_upper_bound_is_allowed` ‚Äî a payload at exactly `MAX_OUTBOUND_PAYLOAD_BYTES` is segmented (allowed); `‚Ä¶::outbound_payload_over_upper_bound_fails_closed` ‚Äî a payload over `MAX_OUTBOUND_PAYLOAD_BYTES` fails closed with `OutboundPayloadTooLarge`. (7 named; all resolve on disk, exactly one `fn` each.) |
| **CI** | `ci/ci_check_outbound_segmentation.sh` ‚Äî fails the build if the serve path uses a second/alternate mux frame encoder (exactly one `encode_frame(` call + one `MuxFrame {` construction, both inside `encode_inner_frame`), if `MAX_OUTBOUND_PAYLOAD_BYTES` is not a fixed literal or gains a CLI/env/config escape, or if `handle_outbound` no longer segments via `encode_inner_frame`; present + executable on disk |

_cross-refs: `CN-SESS-04` (the inbound reassembly this is the outbound inverse of), `DC-LIVEMEM-01` (the symmetric inbound bound ‚Äî `MAX_OUTBOUND_PAYLOAD_BYTES` mirrors `MAX_REASSEMBLY_TAIL_BYTES`), `CN-WIRE-08` (tag-24 wire envelope on the served block), `DC-SERVEMEM-01` (the bounded serve READ ‚Äî this rule makes the bounded serve TRANSMIT a large in-range block), `DC-CONS-17` (byte-identical served block bytes). GREEN-only (no BLUE change); the single-frame `encode_inner_frame` / `mux::frame` authority is reused unchanged. The outbound segmenter makes a large served BlockFetch Block (a Conway block above the 65535-byte mux SDU limit) transmittable ‚Äî receive+send symmetry on the wire layer._

### `CN-SNAPSHOT-01`: A forged block becomes visible to peers only AFTER‚Ä¶

_tier: derived ¬∑ status: declared_

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | docs/planning/phase4-n-r-invariants.md ¬ß1 (I4); ¬ß2 (N11); ¬ß3 (D6) |
| **Requirement** | A forged block becomes visible to peers only AFTER ServedChainHandle::push_atomic succeeds. The push_atomic call covers the full served_chain_admit call inside a watch::Sender::send_modify closure ‚Äî no observer can read a torn snapshot mid-insertion. Coordinator emits BroadcastBlock; RED effect handler calls push_atomic; only on Ok(ServedTip) may per-peer reducers serve the block. Fail-closed shutdown on PushError. |
| **Code** | TBD ‚Äî populated by N-R-B B2 slice (ade_runtime::producer::served_chain_handle::ServedChainHandle::push_atomic) + B3 slice (produce_mode BroadcastBlock arm wiring) |

### `CN-STORE-07`: Single materialize authority for rolled-back state: the function that‚Ä¶

_tier: release ¬∑ status: enforced_ ¬∑ _strengthened_in: PHASE4-N-J, PHASE4-N-K, PHASE4-N-AI_

> **Strengthened in PHASE4-N-AI.** `materialize_rolled_back_state` is the SOLE rollback-materialize authority the live fork-choice apply driver (`DC-NODE-25`) and the `WalEntry::RollBack` replay arm (`DC-NODE-27`) both call ‚Äî the durable rollback record is NOT a second rollback implementation; it re-invokes this single authority. The four-cell contract below is unchanged.

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | docs/planning/ledger-snapshot-rollback-invariants.md ¬ß1 (I-5) |
| **Requirement** | Single materialize authority for rolled-back state: the function that materializes (LedgerState, PraosChainDepState) at a target point uses ONLY one SnapshotStore lookup + ChainDb::iter_from_slot + apply_block_with_verdicts (+ apply_epoch_boundary when crossing). No bypass; no parallel rolled-back-state computation path. Mirror of CN-CONS-08 (admission gate) for the rollback path. Single- public-function discipline; type-level + CI grep enforcement. |
| **Code** | `crates/ade_ledger/src/rollback/materialize.rs` (materialize_rolled_back_state ‚Äî the sole pub fn returning (LedgerState, PraosChainDepState) in the rollback module tree); `crates/ade_ledger/src/rollback/traits.rs` (SnapshotReader + BlockSource narrow read-only traits ‚Äî production impls in ade_runtime go through the same single composition) |
| **Tests** | `materialize_returns_rollback_too_deep_when_no_snapshot`, `materialize_with_snapshot_at_target_returns_snapshot_state`, `materialize_with_snapshot_below_target_replays_forward`, `materialize_fails_closed_on_invalid_block`, `materialize_replay_forward_equals_direct_apply` |
| **CI** | `ci/ci_check_rollback_materialize_closure.sh` |

### `CN-WIRE-08`: N2N tag-24 CBOR-in-CBOR payload envelopes are constructed and stripped through‚Ä¶

_tier: derived ¬∑ status: enforced_

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | docs/planning/phase4-n-x-invariants.md |
| **Requirement** | N2N tag-24 CBOR-in-CBOR payload envelopes are constructed and stripped through ONE shared BLUE byte authority in ade_codec (wrap_tag24/unwrap_tag24). Protocol-specific composition lives in ade_network BLUE codecs: a served BlockFetch MsgBlock payload is tag24(bytes([era,block])) (era inside the wrap); a served ChainSync RollForward header is [era_tag, tag24(bytes(header_cbor))] (era_tag outside the wrap). Both compositions are pinned byte-identically against captured cardano-node 11.0.1 wire fixtures, not codec comments. No bare [era,block] may be served over BlockFetch and no bare header over ChainSync RollForward. No hand-rolled tag-24 parse may exist in RED ‚Äî admission and interop call the shared authority. unwrap_tag24 fails closed (typed error) on non-(0xd8 0x18), wrong inner length, or trailing bytes. The inner bytes are copied verbatim (no re-encode). |
| **Code** | `crates/ade_codec/src/cbor/tag24.rs` (wrap_tag24/unwrap_tag24 + TagEnvelopeError); `crates/ade_codec/src/cbor/mod.rs` (read_bytes/read_text/skip_item length-arg overflow guard ‚Äî fail-closed, no panic); `crates/ade_network/src/codec/block_fetch.rs` + chain_sync.rs (per-protocol compose/decompose); `crates/ade_network/src/block_fetch/server.rs` + chain_sync/server.rs (serve emits composed bytes); `crates/ade_node/src/admission/runner.rs` + `crates/ade_core_interop/src/follow.rs` (RED unwraps migrated onto the shared authority) |
| **Tests** | `wrap_then_unwrap_is_identity_across_length_classes`, `wrap_emits_canonical_tag24_marker_and_length`, `unwrap_returns_zero_copy_borrow_of_input`, `unwrap_rejects_missing_tag24_marker`, `unwrap_rejects_non_byte_string_payload`, `unwrap_rejects_truncated_inner`, `unwrap_rejects_trailing_bytes`, `inner_bytes_are_verbatim_not_reencoded`, `unwrap_rejects_huge_declared_length_without_panic`, `read_bytes_rejects_overflowing_declared_length`, `read_text_rejects_overflowing_declared_length`, `producer_block_fetch_serve_block_payload_is_tag24_wrapped_and_decodes`, `producer_block_fetch_serve_block_bytes_equal_accepted_block_as_bytes`, `block_body_is_wrapped_cbor_item`, `captured_block_era_index_matches_ade_storage_scheme`, `chain_sync_wire_era_index_is_consensus_index`, `compose_decompose_rollforward_header_round_trips`, `decompose_rollforward_header_rejects_non_tag24_inner`, `conway_rollforward_header_served_shape_matches_oracle`, `producer_chain_sync_serve_roll_forward_header_equals_accepted_block_header_bytes`, `session_transcript_served_block_bytes_equal_admitted_accepted_block_bytes`, `session_transcript_announced_header_matches_served_body_recipe`, `cross_impl_server_pipeline_request_range_returns_decodable_bytes`, `cross_impl_server_pipeline_request_range_byte_identical_to_self_accept_input` |
| **CI** | `ci/ci_check_tag24_wire_authority.sh` |

### `CN-WIRE-09`: The Shelley-and-later header_body `prev_hash` is the closed wire grammar `$hash32 / null`‚Ä¶

_tier: derived ¬∑ status: enforced_ ¬∑ _introduced_in: PHASE4-N-F-G-J_

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | `docs/planning/phase4-n-f-g-j-genesis-successor-prevhash-invariants.md`; cluster docs `docs/clusters/PHASE4-N-F-G-J/` (`cluster.md`, `S2-prevhash-type-codec-authority.md`, `S3-position-validation-genesis-forge.md`) |
| **Requirement** | The Shelley-and-later `header_body.prev_hash` field is the closed wire grammar `$hash32 / null` (cardano-ledger `PrevHash = GenesisHash \| BlockHash`). Ade represents it as the closed sum `PrevHash = Genesis \| Block(Hash32)` ‚Äî never a flat `Hash32`. `PrevHash::Genesis` encodes to / decodes from CBOR null (`0xf6`); `PrevHash::Block(h)` encodes to / decodes from a 32-byte hash32. A genesis-successor block (`block_number` 0 on a from-genesis chain) MUST carry `PrevHash::Genesis`/null; a non-genesis block (`block_number > 0`) MUST carry `PrevHash::Block(hash32)`. Encoding is canonical and round-trips through ONE shared BLUE `ade_codec` authority; the raw byte codec is POSITION-BLIND (it decodes null ‚Üí `Genesis` and hash32 ‚Üí `Block` without knowing `block_number`). No all-zero `Hash32`, no anchor fingerprint, and no Shelley genesis hash may stand in for the genesis predecessor. The position-aware check (`block_number` 0 requires `Genesis`; `block_number > 0` requires `Block`) is enforced by the sibling forge/validation slice (CE-G-J-3, S3), NOT by this position-blind codec. |
| **Code** | `crates/ade_types/src/shelley/block.rs` (the closed `PrevHash = Genesis \| Block(Hash32)` sum + `ShelleyHeaderBody.prev_hash` + `block_hash()` accessor ‚Äî never a flat `Hash32`); `crates/ade_codec/src/shelley/block.rs` (`decode_prev_hash` + the `ShelleyHeaderBody` `AdeEncode` null/hash32 match ‚Äî the single POSITION-BLIND raw codec authority); `crates/ade_ledger/src/block_validity/header_position.rs` (`check_header_position` ‚Äî the single POSITION-AWARE authority, `block_number` 0 ‚áî `Genesis`; S3); `crates/ade_ledger/src/block_validity/header_input.rs` (`decode_block` calls `check_header_position` before the header authority; S3); `crates/ade_ledger/src/block_validity/verdict.rs` (`BlockValidityError::HeaderPositionInvalid` ‚Üí existing `HeaderInvalid` class; S3); `crates/ade_ledger/src/producer/forge.rs` + `crates/ade_ledger/src/block_validity/unsigned_header_pre_image.rs` (forge + KES pre-image carry `tick.prev_hash: PrevHash` directly ‚Äî `Genesis` for block 0, byte-identical `Block` path; S3); `crates/ade_runtime/src/producer/chain_evolution.rs` (`prev_hash()` cold-start ‚Üí `PrevHash::Genesis`, all-zero stand-in deleted; S3) ‚Äî producer `prev_hash` migrated `Hash32`‚Üí`PrevHash` end-to-end |
| **Tests** | Codec (POSITION-BLIND), `crates/ade_codec/src/shelley/block.rs`: `prevhash_genesis_round_trips_as_null`, `prevhash_block_round_trips_as_hash32`, `prevhash_codec_is_position_blind`, `genesis_successor_header_round_trips_with_null_prev`, `block_header_prev_hash_byte_identical_after_migration`. Position-aware check, `crates/ade_ledger/src/block_validity/header_position.rs`: `header_position_zero_requires_genesis_ok`, `header_position_zero_with_block_is_rejected`, `header_position_nonzero_requires_block_ok`, `header_position_nonzero_with_genesis_is_rejected`. Decode-path + corpus, `crates/ade_ledger/src/producer/forge.rs` (decode-rejects) + `crates/ade_ledger/src/block_validity/unsigned_header_pre_image.rs` (corpus): `decode_block_rejects_block_prev_at_block_number_zero`, `decode_block_rejects_genesis_prev_at_nonzero_block_number`, `corpus_blocks_pass_header_position_rule`. Forge + KES pre-image, `crates/ade_ledger/src/producer/forge.rs` + `crates/ade_ledger/src/block_validity/unsigned_header_pre_image.rs`: `forge_block_number_zero_emits_genesis_prev_hash`, `forge_nonzero_block_emits_block_prev_byte_identical`, `forge_block_zero_self_consistent_through_decode_block`, `pre_image_block_zero_emits_genesis_prev`, `pre_image_nonzero_block_prev_byte_identical`, `forged_block_zero_kes_preimage_equals_decoded_header_body_bytes`. Producer chain-evolution, `crates/ade_runtime/src/producer/chain_evolution.rs`: `chain_evolution_prev_hash_genesis_at_cold_start`, `chain_evolution_prev_hash_block_with_tip`. (20 named; all resolve on disk.) |
| **CI** | `ci/ci_check_prevhash_single_wire_authority.sh` (NEW ‚Äî `PrevHash` is the single shared wire authority: the null/hash32 codec lives in one `ade_codec` home, the position-aware `check_header_position` is the sole position authority, and no all-zero / anchor-fingerprint / genesis-hash stand-in for the genesis predecessor) |
### `CN-WIRE-10`: Serve-side N2N handshake `versionData` uses the single shared per-version authority (`encode_n2n_version_params`), NodeToNodeV_15 cardano-node compatible‚Ä¶

_tier: derived ¬∑ status: enforced_ ¬∑ _introduced_in: PHASE4-N-F-G-L_

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | `docs/clusters/PHASE4-N-F-G-L/cluster.md` |
| **Requirement** | Ade's serve-side N2N handshake RESPONDER must encode versionData / MsgAcceptVersion / query-reply in the closed Cardano NodeToNode wire grammar a real cardano-node decodes, through the SINGLE shared per-version authority (`encode_n2n_version_params`) the INITIATOR also uses ‚Äî the two directions cannot diverge. The versionData arity matches the negotiated version: V11..=15 emit the 4-element `[networkMagic, initiatorAndResponderDiffusionMode, peerSharing, query]`; V16+ append perasSupport. The responder MUST NOT emit a placeholder / bare value (the prior `VersionParams(vec![0x01])` = CBOR `TInt 1`, which a real cardano-node rejected with `HandshakeDecodeError NodeToNodeV_15 "unknown encoding: TInt 1"`). Closed grammar ‚Äî no fallback interpretation, no decoder loosening; the encoding is byte-pinned against captured real cardano-node fixtures, never an Ade‚ÜîAde round-trip. |
| **Code** | `crates/ade_network/src/handshake/version_table.rs` (`encode_n2n_version_params` ‚Äî the SINGLE per-version N2N versionData wire authority); `crates/ade_network/src/session/handshake_driver.rs` (the serve responder builds AcceptVersion via `encode_n2n_version_params(version.get(), params.network_magic)`, NOT a placeholder); `crates/ade_node/src/admission/bootstrap.rs` (`build_n2n_version_table` ‚Äî the initiator uses the SAME authority) |
| **Tests** | `crates/ade_network/tests/handshake_responder_cardano_node_fixture.rs`: `responder_v15_accept_matches_real_cardano_node_preprod_fixture`, `responder_v15_accept_matches_failing_c1_peer_fixture`, `responder_v15_versiondata_is_a_four_element_array_not_a_bare_int`. `crates/ade_node/tests/node_spine_serve_loopback.rs`: `node_spine_serve_loopback_follower_fetches_self_accepted_block`. (4 named; all resolve on disk.) |
| **CI** | `ci/ci_check_n2n_handshake_versiondata_authority.sh` (NEW ‚Äî pins `encode_n2n_version_params` as the single per-version versionData encoder and the per-version field shape against the real-node handshake fixture) |

### `CN-WIRE-11`: Serve-side ChainSync `MsgFindIntersect` wire-compat ‚Äî scoped indefinite-length points decode + `IntersectFound[Origin]` reply‚Ä¶

_tier: derived ¬∑ status: enforced_ ¬∑ _introduced_in: PHASE4-N-F-G-M_

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | `docs/clusters/PHASE4-N-F-G-M/cluster.md` |
| **Requirement** | Ade's serve-side ChainSync server must be wire-compatible with a real cardano-node follower's `MsgFindIntersect`, in two halves, served from the SINGLE `ServedChainView` authority. (A) REQUEST DECODE ‚Äî the codec MUST accept the `MsgFindIntersect` points list whether a real cardano-node encodes it as a CBOR INDEFINITE-length array (`0x9f .. 0xff`) or Ade encodes it definite-length. Scoped to THAT list ONLY: the outer message array, each Point, and the tip stay strictly definite (`decode_array_header` is unchanged and still rejects indefinite everywhere else); the indefinite form requires the `0xff` break and the message is full-consumed ‚Äî no catch-all, no fallback, no unknown-CBOR acceptance. (B) REPLY ‚Äî Origin is the universal common ancestor (every chain descends from genesis), so a `MsgFindIntersect` whose points include Origin MUST be answered `IntersectFound[Origin]`; block points resolve through the existing closed `ServedHeaderLookup::intersect`; no match yields `IntersectNotFound` ‚Äî no widening beyond the Origin intersect. Closed grammar, byte-pinned against captured real cardano-node fixtures (the follower's `MsgFindIntersect` request + the node's `MsgIntersectFound` reply), never an Ade‚ÜîAde round-trip (which passes against Ade's own definite-length encoding and so cannot catch the indefinite-array incompatibility). |
| **Code** | `crates/ade_network/src/codec/primitives.rs` (`decode_array_head_two_form` + `try_consume_break` ‚Äî the SCOPED two-form array head; `decode_array_header` stays definite-only; the closed `ArrayHead = Definite(u64) \| Indefinite` is the one NEW BLUE canonical type of the span); `crates/ade_network/src/codec/chain_sync.rs` (`decode_find_intersect_points` ‚Äî accepts the indefinite points list for `MsgFindIntersect` ONLY); `crates/ade_network/src/chain_sync/server.rs` (`producer_chain_sync_serve` FindIntersect arm ‚Äî Origin ‚Üí `IntersectFound[Origin]`, block points via the existing closed intersect) |
| **Tests** | `crates/ade_network/tests/serve_chainsync_findintersect_cardano_node_fixture.rs`: `real_cardano_node_findintersect_indefinite_points_list_decodes`, `real_cardano_node_findintersect_yields_intersect_found_origin`. `crates/ade_network/src/chain_sync/server.rs`: `producer_chain_sync_serve_find_intersect_origin_yields_intersect_found_origin`, `producer_chain_sync_serve_find_intersect_known_point_yields_intersect_found`, `producer_chain_sync_serve_find_intersect_unknown_point_yields_intersect_not_found`. `crates/ade_network/src/codec/primitives.rs`: `decode_array_header_still_rejects_indefinite`, `two_form_accepts_definite_and_indefinite`. (7 named; all resolve on disk.) |
| **CI** | `ci/ci_check_chainsync_findintersect_compat.sh` (NEW ‚Äî pins the scoped two-form FindIntersect decode + the `Origin ‚Üí IntersectFound[Origin]` reply against the real-node fixtures; `decode_array_header` stays definite-only) |

### `CN-WIRE-12`: Feed/receive-side BlockFetch removes the tag-24 envelope via the single `ade_codec::unwrap_tag24` authority before authoritative decode‚Ä¶

_tier: derived ¬∑ status: enforced_ ¬∑ _introduced_in: PHASE4-N-F-G-O_

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | `docs/clusters/PHASE4-N-F-G-O/cluster.md` |
| **Requirement** | Ade's FEED/receive-side BlockFetch path MUST remove the protocol tag-24 wrapper using the SINGLE `ade_codec` unwrap authority (`decompose_blockfetch_block = ade_codec::unwrap_tag24`) before authoritative block decode, so `decode_block` / `pump_block` receive ONLY bare `[era, block]` bytes. This is the receive-side mirror of the serve-side `compose_blockfetch_block` (`wrap_tag24`, `CN-WIRE-08`) ‚Äî NOT a new block decoder, NOT a second unwrap implementation. The wire pump performs the unwrap EXACTLY ONCE, at the `MsgBlock` receive boundary, before it emits `AdmissionPeerEvent::Block`; the bare-bytes contract downstream (`run_node_sync ‚Üí pump_block`, and recovery/restart from WAL/db) is unchanged ‚Äî so the unwrap belongs on the FEED path, NOT inside `pump_block` (which recovery also feeds with bare bytes). Fail-closed: a malformed tag-24, a non-tag-24 payload where the BlockFetch protocol requires tag-24, or inner bytes that are not `[era, block]` ‚Üí a structured `BlockFetchDecode` error / peer drop, never a silent pass-through, skip, or fallback. |
| **Code** | `crates/ade_runtime/src/admission/wire_pump.rs` (`handle_block_fetch` `BlockFetchMessage::Block` arm ‚Äî calls `decompose_blockfetch_block` ONCE at the receive boundary, emits bare `[era, block]`; fail-closed `BlockFetchDecode` on a non-tag-24 payload); `crates/ade_network/src/codec/block_fetch.rs` (`decompose_blockfetch_block = ade_codec::unwrap_tag24` ‚Äî the SINGLE inverse of `compose_blockfetch_block`, unchanged); `crates/ade_node/src/node_sync.rs` (`run_node_sync ‚Üí pump_block` consumes the bare `[era, block]` the wire pump now delivers) |
| **Tests** | `crates/ade_node/tests/forge_succeeds.rs`: `feed_unwrap_decodes_genesis_successor_block_zero`. `crates/ade_runtime/src/admission/wire_pump.rs`: `block_fetch_unwraps_tag24_emitting_bare_block`, `block_fetch_fails_closed_on_non_tag24_payload`. `crates/ade_node/tests/node_spine_serve_loopback.rs`: `node_spine_serve_loopback_follower_fetches_self_accepted_block`. (4 named; all resolve on disk.) |
| **CI** | `ci/ci_check_feed_tag24_unwrap.sh` (NEW ‚Äî pins that the feed-side WirePump unwraps tag-24 via `ade_codec::unwrap_tag24` before decode, and adds no hand-rolled tag-24 parse) |


---

## RO ‚Äî Release Obligations

Release-gate obligations ‚Äî the live-pass / bounty-acceptance / corpus-presence legs. Several are operator-gated (require an operator-action live pass against a real peer) and are recorded here with their gating status.

_16 rules._

### `RO-CLOSE-01`: Unmasked close-gate discipline. Any slice that changes canonical bytes‚Ä¶

_tier: release ¬∑ status: enforced_

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | docs/clusters/completed/PHASE4-N-V/CLOSURE.md; user-direction (PHASE4-N-V close correction) |
| **Requirement** | Unmasked close-gate discipline. Any slice that changes canonical bytes, encoded forms, decoder inputs, or golden fixtures MUST run an UNMASKED full close gate (cargo test --workspace) and use cargo's REAL exit status / result line as the sole pass/fail authority for cluster closure. Piped output (\| tail, \| grep) may be used for display only, NEVER as the pass/fail authority ‚Äî a pipeline's exit code is the last stage's, not cargo's. Before closure, ALL consumers of the changed canonical output (every golden fixture, decoder, re-encode, and byte-identity test, across all crates ‚Äî not just the edited crate) MUST be grepped/audited. A cluster is not closed until the unmasked close gate exits successfully. |
| **Code** | process/release discipline ‚Äî no BLUE code locus; binds /cluster-close and any slice touching canonical output |
| **Tests** | _(no tests named in registry ‚Äî gap)_ |
| **CI** | _(no CI script ‚Äî gap)_ |

### `RO-LIVE-04`: Live wire-smoke pass: operator runs `ade_node --mode wire_only --peer ADDR‚Ä¶

_tier: release ¬∑ status: enforced_

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | docs/planning/phase4-n-l-live-wire-smoke-invariants.md ¬ß1 |
| **Requirement** | Live wire-smoke pass: operator runs `ade_node --mode wire_only --peer ADDR --network NAME` against a private cardano-node peer. The binary opens TCP, completes the N2N handshake, issues one chain-sync FindIntersect(Origin), reads the peer's announced tip, emits a closed-vocabulary JSONL log of the exchange, and exits cleanly. The JSONL event vocabulary is closed: only node_started / peer_dial_started / handshake_ok / peer_tip_read / peer_dial_failed / wire_smoke_complete / node_shutdown variants are emitted. ### `RO-LIVE-06`: BA-02 peer-acceptance evidence closure (SCHEMA + CORRELATION MECHANICS ONLY)‚Ä¶

_tier: release ¬∑ status: enforced_

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | docs/clusters/PHASE4-N-F-C/cluster.md; L6-peer-acceptance-evidence-manifest.md |
| **Requirement** | BA-02 peer-acceptance evidence closure (SCHEMA + CORRELATION MECHANICS ONLY). The BA-02 evidence surface is a closed, versioned manifest (Ba02Manifest) plus a pure, total, deterministic, HASH-PRIMARY correlator: correlate is the SOLE Ba02Manifest constructor; the forged-block hash is the REQUIRED correlation key; a peer-accept signal's slot is OPTIONAL context that must AGREE when present (a present-but-different slot contradicts -> NoEvidence); conflicting peer signals -> NoEvidence; and the peer-accept-log parser is allow-list only (peer_served_block / peer_chain_tip), dropping every weaker/self/unknown/ malformed line (ForgeSucceeded / self_accept / block_received / agreement_verdict are never coerced to acceptance). The forged evidence uses only forge-event- exposed fields (ForgedBlockArtifact.{hash,slot}); the hash is never recomputed and block bytes are never parsed. ENFORCED for the schema + correlation mechanics; NOT a claim that BA-02 was achieved live. |
| **Code** | `crates/ade_node/src/ba02_evidence.rs` (Ba02Manifest, BA02Outcome, PeerAcceptEvent, NoEvidenceReason, parse_peer_accept_events, correlate); **(G-C)** `crates/ade_node/src/ba02_pass.rs` (RED operator-pass evidence I/O ‚Äî `correlate_peer_log_file` reads the operator-captured peer log into the GREEN `correlate`; `write_ba02_manifest` accepts ONLY a `Ba02Manifest`); ci/ci_check_ba02_evidence_closed.sh; ci/ci_check_ba02_evidence_manifest_schema.sh |
| **Tests** | `ba02_manifest_schema_round_trips`, `ba02_correlate_served_block_yields_manifest`, `ba02_correlate_chain_tip_only_yields_manifest`, `ba02_correlate_both_signals_agree_records_served_primary`, `ba02_correlate_served_block_without_slot_yields_manifest`, `ba02_correlate_conflicting_signals_is_no_evidence`, `ba02_correlate_wrong_hash_is_no_evidence`, `ba02_correlate_chain_point_mismatch_is_no_evidence`, `ba02_correlate_no_slot_wrong_hash_is_no_evidence`, `ba02_correlate_stale_log_is_no_evidence`, `ba02_correlate_empty_peer_log_is_no_evidence`, `ba02_self_accept_is_not_evidence`, `ba02_forge_succeeded_alone_is_not_evidence`, `ba02_block_received_alone_is_not_evidence`, `ba02_agreement_verdict_is_not_evidence`, `ba02_parser_accepts_well_formed_served_block`, `ba02_parser_drops_unknown_and_malformed_lines`, `ba02_correlate_two_runs_byte_identical`, `correlate_wired_to_operator_peer_log` _(G-C; `crates/ade_node/tests/node_operator_pass_ba02.rs`)_, `correlate_from_operator_log_file_is_deterministic` _(G-C; same file)_ |

### `OP-OPS-04`: Operator-supplied keys. Ade supports both KES key flows: (a) Ade-native‚Ä¶

_tier: operational ¬∑ status: enforced_

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | docs/planning/phase4-n-c-invariants.md ¬ß7 (OQ1); docs/active/op-ops-04-ade-native-kes-flow.md; docs/planning/phase4-n-p-invariants.md |
| **Requirement** | Operator-supplied keys. Ade supports both KES key flows: (a) Ade-native `ade_node --mode key_gen_kes --out-file PATH` emitting an `ade.kes.seed.v1` envelope loaded via `ade_runtime::producer::keys::load_ade_kes_signing_key`; (b) cardano-cli `node key-gen-KES` emitting a 608-byte `KesSigningKey_ed25519_kes_2^6` envelope loaded via `ade_runtime::producer::keys::load_kes_signing_key_skey`. After PHASE4-N-P S5 the cardano-cli path routes through the Ade-owned BLUE deserializer (`ade_crypto::kes_sum::Sum6Kes::raw_deserialize_signing_key_kes`); both flows produce a `KesSecret` whose inner is `ade_crypto::kes_sum::Sum6Kes::SigningKey` (BLUE-owned algorithm). VRF and cold (Ed25519) keys continue to be operator-supplied via cardano-cli text-envelope `.skey` files. Private-key material never crosses into BLUE ‚Äî the entire RED custody surface lives under `crates/ade_runtime/src/producer/{keys,signing,ade_kes_envelope}.rs`. Wrong-size payloads fail-close via `KeyLoadError::UnsupportedExpandedKesKeyFormat`; structurally-invalid 608-byte payloads fail-close via `KeyLoadError::KesParse(KesParseError::*)`. Mechanical enforcement: ci/ci_check_private_key_custody.sh + ci/ci_check_kes_envelope_closed.sh + ci/ci_check_kes_sum_compatibility.sh. |
| **Code** | `crates/ade_runtime/src/producer/keys.rs` (load_*_signing_key_skey, load_ade_kes_signing_key, write_ade_kes_envelope, KeyLoadError); `crates/ade_runtime/src/producer/ade_kes_envelope.rs` (closed envelope grammar); `crates/ade_runtime/src/producer/signing.rs` (RED-confined custody, KesSecret with BLUE-owned inner); crates/ade_crypto/src/kes_sum/ (BLUE Sum6KES algorithm + serde + ground-truth corpus); `crates/ade_node/src/key_gen.rs` (one-shot key-gen-KES surface) |
| **Tests** | `ade_envelope_round_trips_through_loader_at_period_0`, `ade_envelope_loader_returns_kes_at_loaded_period`, `ade_envelope_loader_rejects_signing_at_past_period`, `cardano_cli_kes_envelope_rejects_32_byte_payload`, `cardano_cli_kes_envelope_rejects_synthetic_608_byte_payload`, `cardano_cli_kes_envelope_accepts_real_608_byte_payload`, `cardano_cli_kes_envelope_rejects_612_byte_payload`, `cardano_cli_kes_envelope_rejects_608_byte_leaf_zero_payload`, `ade_envelope_loader_returns_unknown_format`, `ade_envelope_loader_returns_wrong_role`, `ade_envelope_loader_returns_unsupported_crypto`, `ade_envelope_loader_returns_missing_seed_32`, `ade_envelope_loader_returns_period_idx_overflow`, `ade_envelope_loader_returns_malformed_json`, `write_ade_kes_envelope_sets_0600_permissions`, `vrf_and_cold_cardano_cli_skey_envelopes_round_trip`, `keys_loader_rejects_wrong_envelope_type`, `keys_loader_rejects_malformed_cbor_hex`, `key_load_error_io_carries_no_path_bytes`, `ade_envelope_load_error_io_carries_no_path_bytes`, `run_key_gen_kes_writes_loadable_envelope`, `run_key_gen_kes_writes_at_loaded_period`, `run_key_gen_kes_rejects_short_seed_file`, `cardano_cli_corpus_skey_deserializes_and_vk_matches_ground_truth`, `cardano_cli_corpus_sign_then_upstream_verifies` |
| **CI** | `ci/ci_check_private_key_custody.sh`, `ci/ci_check_kes_envelope_closed.sh`, `ci/ci_check_kes_sum_compatibility.sh` |

It references all 11 new rule IDs (`DC-NODE-34`‚Ä¶`41`, `DC-PUMP-04`, `DC-EVIDENCE-04/05`) and the 12 new gates. Every **Code**-row module of the 11 NEW rows maps to a CODEMAP entry (the six new modules + the already-mapped `ade_node::node_lifecycle` dispatch/apply taps + the `ade_core::consensus::fork_choice` `select_best_chain` it routes to). **No CODEMAP drift** (CI 173 and rules 372 agree; all referenced modules present).
- **HEAD_DELTAS** (`docs/ade-HEAD_DELTAS.md`) was **REGENERATED to this HEAD** (`862cd2cb`, the sibling `/head-deltas` PHASE4-N-AO close pass) ‚Äî ¬ß0 HEAD `862cd2cb`; ¬ß5 @ **173 CI**; ¬ß7 @ **372 rules** / 239 enforced. **All 11 named PHASE4-N-AO gates are catalogued in ¬ß5 (0 orphans)** bound to their owning rule: `ci_check_{peer_identity_preserved,candidate_construction_validated,live_selector_dispatch,fork_switch_never_abandons,lca_anchor_walk,wire_pump_fairness,fork_choice_evidence_closed,post_switch_convergence_window,missing_bridge_fail_closed,rollback_retention_evidence,missing_bridge_refetch}.sh`. The new `ade_node` modules (`candidate_aggregator`, `lca_walk`, `fair_merge`, `fork_switch`, `post_switch_continuity`, `selector_state`) are GREEN/RED orchestration + a closed observe-only evidence vocabulary over those closed surfaces ‚Äî NOT new authority and NOT open extension points. The closed `AdmissionLogEvent` fork-choice vocabulary (10 variants + an emit-only allow-list) is a CLOSED registry entry SEAMS should record (a versioned evidence vocabulary, additive, fail-closed on an unknown variant), not a new extensible seam.

The RED signing shell EVOLVES the operator KES signing key forward to the requested KES period BEFORE signing: NEW `ProducerShell::kes_sign_header_advancing(&mut self, period, preimage)` = `kes_advance_to(period)?` then `kes_sign_header`. `kes_advance_to ‚Üí kes_update` is the EXISTING deterministic Sum6KES update ‚Äî no-op at the current period (period-0 signing unchanged), forward-evolves in window, fail-closed `Signing(EvolutionBackwards)` on a backwards period (forward-secrecy ‚Äî a destroyed past period cannot be re-signed) and `Signing(EvolutionExhausted)` beyond the key lifetime / `SUM6_MAX_PERIOD = 63`. The `period` is passed VERBATIM (no `period ¬± N`). Its own four-cell contract (branded `UnsignedHeaderPreImage` + the single-source recipe + 3 tests + `ci_check_unsigned_header_preimage_single_source.sh`) is unchanged; the strengthening is the cross-period extension, not a re-scope.

**Root cause (surfaced by the C1 genesis-rehearsal re-run ‚Äî recorded honestly, NOT a regression from N-U/AA/AB):** the C1 rehearsal stopped reproducing once the private net aged past one KES period (slot ~249659 / `slotsPerKESPeriod` 129600 ‚Üí KES period 1), because the forge's only real KES sign called the raw `shell.kes_sign_header(kes_period, ‚Ä¶)`, which requires `kes.current_period() == requested` ‚Äî and NOTHING evolved the minted-at-period-0 operator key forward ‚Äî so every leader slot failed `KesPeriodNotCurrent { requested: 1, current: 0 }` (`succeeded = 0`; the follower KeepAlive-timed-out waiting for a block). The wire/serve/intersection path was healthy. **Live proof (non-promotable rehearsal, acceptance #3):** with the fix Ade forged 3 period-1 blocks + self-accepted them, and the real cardano-node DOWNLOADED the period-1 header with NO KES/parse rejection. **Genesis-window finding (recorded honestly):** `slotsPerKESPeriod = 129600 == 3k/f = 129600`, so KES period 1 begins exactly when the genesis density window closes ‚Äî a from-genesis rehearsal can never show forge-at-period-1 AND follower-adopt simultaneously; the period-1 follower rejection is `CandidateTooSparse` (genesis-density-window limit, KES-INDEPENDENT), not a KES rejection. Cross-period end-to-end forge‚Üíadopt is proven on the dense C2 tip path, NOT a net reset (which returns to period 0). Two pre-existing fail-closed INFO items handed to C2 (registry `evidence_notes`): (1) `kes_advance_to` zeroes the key on a FAILED advance ‚Äî UNREACHABLE via the forge (the `kes_period_in_window` + `kes_period_for_slot` pre-check bounds the period), fail-safe; (2) the opcert window upper bound `opcert_start + 63` can diverge from the absolute Sum6KES ceiling 63 when `opcert_start > 0` (real preprod opcerts) ‚Äî still fail-closed (`EvolutionExhausted`), but the C2 config must derive `kes_max_period` from the absolute ceiling.

**Registry reconciliations: NONE ‚Äî 0 open on either re-traced row.** The registry `tests` / `ci_script` / `code_locus` for both N-AC rows are exact on disk (`DC-CRYPTO-10`: 4 leaf-fns + `ci_check_kes_evolution_before_sign.sh` + `kes_sign_header_advancing`/`kes_advance_to` loci + the `produce_mode.rs` call site all resolve; `CN-KES-HEADER-01`: all 3 cited leaves + the gate + loci resolve; `0` drifts).
